def append_project_icons_directory_listing(lines: list[str]) -> None:
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append(f'DIRECTORY LISTING: {PROJECT_ICONS_DIR_DISPLAY}')
  lines.append('AVAILABLE PROJECT ICONS')
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('')
  lines.append('This section lists available project icon assets only.')
  lines.append('Icon file contents are intentionally not exported.')
  lines.append('')

  if not PROJECT_ICONS_DIR.exists():
    lines.append('[DIRECTORY NOT FOUND]')
    lines.append('')
    return

  icon_files = sorted(
    path
    for path in PROJECT_ICONS_DIR.iterdir()
    if path.is_file()
  )

  if not icon_files:
    lines.append('[NO ICON FILES FOUND]')
    lines.append('')
    return

  for icon_file in icon_files:
    relative_path = icon_file.relative_to(ROOT).as_posix()
    lines.append(f'- {relative_path}')

  lines.append('')


def export_files() -> None:
  lines: list[str] = []
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('PROJECT EXPORT')
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('')

  for relative_path in PROJECT_FILES:
    file_path = ROOT / relative_path

    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append(f'FILE: {relative_path}')
    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append('')

    if not file_path.exists():
      lines.append('[FILE NOT FOUND]')
      lines.append('')
      continue

    try:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')

    lines.append(content)
    lines.append('')

  append_project_icons_directory_listing(lines)

  OUTPUT_FILE.write_text('\n'.join(lines), encoding='utf-8')
  print(f'Export finished: {OUTPUT_FILE}')


if __name__ == '__main__':
  export_files()

FILE: tools/metagen/metagen_siemens_generator.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import ast
import re
import sys
import shutil
from collections import OrderedDict
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Iterable

import yaml

METAGEN_KIND = "metagen.component"
SCL_ENCODING = "utf-8"
CONF_DB_NAME = "Conf_DB"
MAIN_FB_NAME = "_MetaGenMain"

# Defaults for library instance DBs. Unknown FB types fall back to DEFAULT_LIBRARY_* values.
DEFAULT_LIBRARY_VERSION = "0.1"
DEFAULT_LIBRARY_OPTIMIZED_ACCESS = "TRUE"
LIBRARY_INSTANCE_METADATA: dict[str, dict[str, str]] = {
    "CCabinetController": {"version": "2.3", "optimized_access": "TRUE"},
    "CCascade": {"version": "0.2", "optimized_access": "FALSE"},
}

PARAM_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\|([^|]+)\|")
EVAL_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"%(.*?)%", re.DOTALL)

DATA_COLUMN_TYPE = "Тип"
DATA_COLUMN_TAG = "Имя переменной"
DATA_COLUMN_VALUE = "Значение"
DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT = "Комментарий"
DATA_COLUMN_CONF = "Conf"
DATA_COLUMN_TYPE_ALIASES = (DATA_COLUMN_TYPE, "Type", "type")
DATA_COLUMN_TAG_ALIASES = (DATA_COLUMN_TAG, "Tag", "tag")
DATA_COLUMN_VALUE_ALIASES = (DATA_COLUMN_VALUE, "Value", "value")
DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT_ALIASES = (DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT, "Comment", "comment")
DATA_COLUMN_CONF_ALIASES = (DATA_COLUMN_CONF, "Conf", "conf")

DATA_COLUMN_CONTRACT: tuple[tuple[str, str, tuple[str, ...]], ...] = (
    (DATA_COLUMN_TYPE, "Type", DATA_COLUMN_TYPE_ALIASES),
    (DATA_COLUMN_TAG, "Tag", DATA_COLUMN_TAG_ALIASES),
    (DATA_COLUMN_VALUE, "Value", DATA_COLUMN_VALUE_ALIASES),
    (DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT, "Comment", DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT_ALIASES),
    (DATA_COLUMN_CONF, "Conf", DATA_COLUMN_CONF_ALIASES),
)
SUPPORTED_DATA_COLUMN_ALIASES: dict[str, tuple[str, ...]] = {
    canonical_name: aliases for canonical_name, _display_name, aliases in DATA_COLUMN_CONTRACT
}
DATA_COLUMN_REQUIRED_DISPLAY_NAMES: dict[str, str] = {
    canonical_name: display_name for canonical_name, display_name, _aliases in DATA_COLUMN_CONTRACT
}
REQUIRED_DATA_COLUMNS: tuple[str, ...] = tuple(canonical_name for canonical_name, _display_name, _aliases in DATA_COLUMN_CONTRACT)
EXPECTED_STATIC_ARTIFACT_NAMES: tuple[str, ...] = (
    f"{CONF_DB_NAME}.scl",
    f"{MAIN_FB_NAME}.scl",
)


def _normalize_column_alias_token(value: str) -> str:
    normalized = str(value or "").strip()
    if not normalized:
        return ""
    return normalized.casefold() if normalized.isascii() else normalized


def _build_data_column_alias_index(
    supported_aliases: dict[str, tuple[str, ...]] | None = None,
) -> dict[str, str]:
    aliases_by_canonical = supported_aliases or SUPPORTED_DATA_COLUMN_ALIASES
    alias_to_canonical: dict[str, str] = {}
    for canonical_name, aliases in aliases_by_canonical.items():
        for alias in aliases:
            normalized_alias = _normalize_column_alias_token(alias)
            if not normalized_alias:
                continue
            existing = alias_to_canonical.get(normalized_alias)
            if existing and existing != canonical_name:
                raise RuntimeError(
                    f"Conflicting data column alias {alias!r}: {existing!r} vs {canonical_name!r}"
                )
            alias_to_canonical[normalized_alias] = canonical_name
    return alias_to_canonical


DATA_COLUMN_ALIAS_TO_CANONICAL = _build_data_column_alias_index()


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class InstanceSpec:
    name: str
    fb_type: str


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConfEntry:
    tag: str
    data_type: str
    value: str
    comment: str


@dataclass
class TemplateDoc:
    source_path: Path
    name: str
    params_header: list[str]
    params_rows: list[list[str]]
    data_columns: list[str]
    data_rows: list[list[str]]
    instances_rows: list[list[str]]
    code_text: str


def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description=(
            "Generate Siemens SCL artifacts from MetaGen YAML documents. "
            "Inputs may be YAML files and/or directories. Directories are searched recursively "
            "for YAML files with kind: metagen.component."
        )
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "inputs",
        nargs="+",
        help="YAML files and/or directories to scan recursively.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--output-dir",
        "-o",
        required=True,
        help="Directory where generated .scl files will be written. No subdirectories are created.",
    )
    return parser.parse_args()


def sanitize_cli_path(value: str) -> str:
    """Normalize Windows shell path quirks.

    In PowerShell/native Windows process launching, a quoted path ending with a backslash
    may arrive with a stray trailing double quote, for example:
    Such a quote is never valid in a Windows path, so we can safely trim it.
    """
    sanitized = value.strip()
    while sanitized.endswith(('"', "'")):
        sanitized = sanitized[:-1]
    return sanitized


def main() -> int:
    args = parse_args()
    input_paths = [Path(sanitize_cli_path(value)).expanduser().resolve() for value in args.inputs]
    output_dir = Path(sanitize_cli_path(args.output_dir)).expanduser().resolve()

    yaml_paths = discover_metagen_yaml_paths(input_paths)
    if not yaml_paths:
        raise SystemExit("No MetaGen YAML documents found in the provided inputs.")

    documents = [load_template_doc(path) for path in yaml_paths]

    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    clean_output_directory(output_dir)

    conf_entries = collect_conf_entries(documents)
    library_instances = collect_library_instances(documents)
    template_names = [document.name for document in documents]

    write_text(output_dir / conf_db_artifact_name(), render_conf_db(conf_entries))

    for instance in library_instances.values():
        write_text(output_dir / library_instance_artifact_name(instance.name), render_library_instance_db(instance))

    for document in documents:
        fb_name = document.name
        write_text(output_dir / template_fb_artifact_name(fb_name), render_template_fb(document))
        write_text(output_dir / template_db_artifact_name(fb_name), render_template_db(fb_name))

    write_text(output_dir / main_fb_artifact_name(), render_main_fb(template_names))

    return 0


def conf_db_artifact_name() -> str:
    return f"{CONF_DB_NAME}.scl"


def main_fb_artifact_name() -> str:
    return f"{MAIN_FB_NAME}.scl"


def template_fb_artifact_name(template_name: str) -> str:
    return f"{template_name}.scl"


def template_db_artifact_name(template_name: str) -> str:
    return f"{template_name}_DB.scl"


def library_instance_artifact_name(instance_name: str) -> str:
    return f"{instance_name}.scl"


def expected_generated_artifact_names(
    *,
    template_names: Iterable[str],
    library_instance_names: Iterable[str],
) -> list[str]:
    artifact_names = set(EXPECTED_STATIC_ARTIFACT_NAMES)
    artifact_names.update(library_instance_artifact_name(name) for name in library_instance_names)
    for template_name in template_names:
        artifact_names.add(template_fb_artifact_name(template_name))
        artifact_names.add(template_db_artifact_name(template_name))
    return sorted(artifact_names)


def expected_generated_artifact_names_for_documents(documents: Iterable[TemplateDoc]) -> list[str]:
    materialized_documents = list(documents)
    library_instances = collect_library_instances(materialized_documents)
    template_names = [document.name for document in materialized_documents]
    return expected_generated_artifact_names(
        template_names=template_names,
        library_instance_names=library_instances.keys(),
    )


def discover_metagen_yaml_paths(input_paths: Iterable[Path]) -> list[Path]:
    discovered: list[Path] = []
    seen: set[Path] = set()

    for input_path in input_paths:
        if not input_path.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"Input path does not exist: {input_path}")

        if input_path.is_dir():
            candidates = sorted(
                path for path in input_path.rglob("*") if path.is_file() and path.suffix.lower() in {".yaml", ".yml"}
            )
        else:
            candidates = [input_path]

        for candidate in candidates:
            resolved = candidate.resolve()
            if resolved in seen:
                continue
            if is_metagen_component_yaml(resolved):
                discovered.append(resolved)
                seen.add(resolved)

    return discovered


def is_metagen_component_yaml(path: Path) -> bool:
    if path.suffix.lower() not in {".yaml", ".yml"}:
        return False
    try:
        text = path.read_text(encoding=SCL_ENCODING)
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig")
    try:
        payload = yaml.safe_load(text)
    except yaml.YAMLError:
        return False
    return isinstance(payload, dict) and payload.get("kind") == METAGEN_KIND


def load_template_doc(path: Path) -> TemplateDoc:
    payload = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding=SCL_ENCODING))
    if not isinstance(payload, dict) or payload.get("kind") != METAGEN_KIND:
        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported MetaGen document: {path}")

    component = require_dict(payload, "component", path)
    params = require_dict(payload, "params", path)
    data = require_dict(payload, "data", path)
    instances = require_dict(payload, "instances", path)
    code = require_dict(payload, "code", path)

    name = str(component.get("name") or "").strip()
    if not name:
        raise ValueError(f"component.name is required in {path}")

    params_header = normalize_string_list(params.get("header", []), path, "params.header")
    params_rows = normalize_rows(params.get("rows", []), len(params_header), path, "params.rows")

    raw_data_columns = normalize_string_list(data.get("columns", []), path, "data.columns")
    data_columns = normalize_data_columns(raw_data_columns, path)
    if not data_columns:
        raise ValueError(f"data.columns is required in {path}")
    assert_canonical_persisted_data_columns(raw_data_columns, path)
    data_rows = normalize_rows(data.get("rows", []), len(data_columns), path, "data.rows")

    instances_rows = normalize_rows(instances.get("rows", []), 2, path, "instances.rows")
    raw_code_text = code.get("text")
    code_text = "" if raw_code_text is None else stringify_scalar(raw_code_text)

    return TemplateDoc(
        source_path=path,
        name=name,
        params_header=params_header,
        params_rows=params_rows,
        data_columns=data_columns,
        data_rows=data_rows,
        instances_rows=instances_rows,
        code_text=code_text,
    )


def require_dict(payload: dict[str, Any], key: str, path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
    value = payload.get(key)
    if not isinstance(value, dict):
        raise ValueError(f"{key} must be a mapping in {path}")
    return value


def normalize_string_list(values: Any, path: Path, field_name: str) -> list[str]:
    if not isinstance(values, list):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be a list in {path}")
    return ["" if value is None else str(value) for value in values]


def canonicalize_data_column_name(column_name: str) -> str | None:
    normalized_alias = _normalize_column_alias_token(column_name)
    if not normalized_alias:
        return None
    return DATA_COLUMN_ALIAS_TO_CANONICAL.get(normalized_alias)


def normalize_data_columns(columns: list[str], path: Path) -> list[str]:
    normalized_columns: list[str] = []
    seen_required_columns: set[str] = set()

    for index, raw_column in enumerate(columns):
        stripped_column = str(raw_column or "").strip()
        canonical_name = canonicalize_data_column_name(stripped_column)
        column_name = canonical_name or stripped_column
        normalized_columns.append(column_name)

        if not canonical_name:
            continue
        if canonical_name in seen_required_columns:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Duplicate data column alias for {DATA_COLUMN_REQUIRED_DISPLAY_NAMES[canonical_name]!r} "
                f"at data.columns[{index}] in {path}"
            )
        seen_required_columns.add(canonical_name)

    return normalized_columns


def assert_canonical_persisted_data_columns(columns: list[str], path: Path) -> None:
    expected_columns = list(REQUIRED_DATA_COLUMNS)
    normalized_columns = [str(column or "").strip() for column in columns]
    if normalized_columns != expected_columns:
        raise ValueError(f"data.columns must match canonical persisted contract order {expected_columns} in {path}")


def normalize_rows(values: Any, expected_length: int, path: Path, field_name: str) -> list[list[str]]:
    if not isinstance(values, list):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be a list in {path}")

    normalized: list[list[str]] = []
    for index, row in enumerate(values):
        if row is None:
            normalized.append([""] * expected_length)
            continue
        if not isinstance(row, list):
            raise ValueError(f"{field_name}[{index}] must be a list in {path}")
        if len(row) > expected_length:
            raise ValueError(
                f"{field_name}[{index}] has {len(row)} items, expected at most {expected_length} in {path}"
            )
        normalized_row = ["" if value is None else stringify_scalar(value) for value in row]
        if len(normalized_row) < expected_length:
            normalized_row.extend([""] * (expected_length - len(normalized_row)))
        normalized.append(normalized_row)
    return normalized


def stringify_scalar(value: Any) -> str:
    if isinstance(value, bool):
        return "true" if value else "false"
    if isinstance(value, (int, float)):
        return str(value)
    return str(value)


def build_param_contexts(document: TemplateDoc) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
    header = document.params_header
    rows = document.params_rows
    if not header:
        return [{}]

    if not rows:
        return [dict(zip(header, [""] * len(header), strict=False))]

    return [dict(zip(header, row, strict=False)) for row in rows]


def apply_template(text: str, context: dict[str, str]) -> str:
    def replace_param(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
        key = match.group(1)
        return context.get(key, match.group(0))

    substituted = PARAM_TOKEN_RE.sub(replace_param, text)

    def replace_eval(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
        expr = match.group(1)
        env: dict[str, Any] = {}
        env.update(context)
        try:
            env.update({name: parse_eval_value(value) for name, value in context.items()})
        except Exception:
            pass
        value = eval(expr, {"__builtins__": __builtins__}, env)
        return stringify_scalar(value)

    return EVAL_TOKEN_RE.sub(replace_eval, substituted)


def parse_eval_value(value: str) -> Any:
    if value == "":
        return ""
    lowered = value.strip().lower()
    if lowered in {"true", "false"}:
        return lowered == "true"
    try:
        return ast.literal_eval(value)
    except Exception:
        return value


def collect_conf_entries(documents: Iterable[TemplateDoc]) -> list[ConfEntry]:
    entries: list[ConfEntry] = []
    seen_tags: set[str] = set()

    for document in documents:
        contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
        _assert_required_data_columns(document)

        for context in contexts:
            for row in document.data_rows:
                mapped = row_to_mapping(document.data_columns, row)
                conf_flag = resolve_data_column_value(mapped, DATA_COLUMN_CONF_ALIASES).strip()
                if not conf_flag:
                    continue
                tag = apply_template(resolve_data_column_value(mapped, DATA_COLUMN_TAG_ALIASES), context).strip()
                if not tag:
                    continue
                if tag in seen_tags:
                    continue
                seen_tags.add(tag)
                data_type = normalize_scl_type(
                    apply_template(resolve_data_column_value(mapped, DATA_COLUMN_TYPE_ALIASES), context).strip()
                )
                entries.append(
                    ConfEntry(
                        tag=tag,
                        data_type=data_type,
                        value=normalize_scl_value(
                            apply_template(resolve_data_column_value(mapped, DATA_COLUMN_VALUE_ALIASES), context).strip(),
                            data_type,
                        ),
                        comment=apply_template(resolve_data_column_value(mapped, DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT_ALIASES), context).strip(),
                    )
                )
    return entries


def _assert_required_data_columns(document: TemplateDoc) -> None:
    column_names = set(document.data_columns)
    missing = [
        DATA_COLUMN_REQUIRED_DISPLAY_NAMES[column_name]
        for column_name in REQUIRED_DATA_COLUMNS
        if column_name not in column_names
    ]
    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f"Missing required data columns {sorted(missing)} in {document.source_path}")


def resolve_data_column_value(mapped: dict[str, str], aliases: tuple[str, ...]) -> str:
    for alias in aliases:
        if alias in mapped:
            return mapped.get(alias, "")
    return ""


def collect_library_instances(documents: Iterable[TemplateDoc]) -> OrderedDict[str, InstanceSpec]:
    instances: OrderedDict[str, InstanceSpec] = OrderedDict()
    for document in documents:
        contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
        for context in contexts:
            for row in document.instances_rows:
                if not any(cell.strip() for cell in row):
                    continue
                raw_name = row[0].strip()
                raw_type = row[1].strip() if len(row) > 1 else ""
                if not raw_name or not raw_type:
                    continue
                name = apply_template(raw_name, context).strip()
                fb_type = apply_template(raw_type, context).strip()
                existing = instances.get(name)
                if existing and existing.fb_type != fb_type:
                    raise ValueError(
                        f"Conflicting instance type for {name}: {existing.fb_type!r} vs {fb_type!r}"
                    )
                instances.setdefault(name, InstanceSpec(name=name, fb_type=fb_type))
    return instances


def row_to_mapping(columns: list[str], row: list[str]) -> dict[str, str]:
    return {column: row[index] for index, column in enumerate(columns)}


def normalize_scl_type(value: str) -> str:
    if not value:
        return value
    mapping = {
        "bool": "Bool",
        "int": "Int",
        "dint": "DInt",
        "real": "Real",
        "word": "Word",
    }
    return mapping.get(value.lower(), value)


def normalize_scl_value(value: str, data_type: str) -> str:
    if value == "":
        return value
    lowered = value.lower()
    normalized_type = data_type.lower()

    if normalized_type == "bool":
        if lowered in {"0", "false"}:
            return "false"
        if lowered in {"1", "true"}:
            return "true"

    if normalized_type == "real":
        if re.fullmatch(r"[-+]?\d+", value):
            return f"{value}.0"

    if lowered in {"true", "false"}:
        return lowered

    return value


def render_conf_db(entries: list[ConfEntry]) -> str:
    header_lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{CONF_DB_NAME}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        "   VAR RETAIN",
    ]

    for entry in entries:
        comment = f"   // {entry.comment}" if entry.comment else ""
        header_lines.append(f"      {entry.tag} : {entry.data_type};{comment}")

    header_lines.extend(["   END_VAR", "", "", "BEGIN"])

    body_lines = [f"   {entry.tag} := {entry.value};" for entry in entries]

    return "\n".join(header_lines + body_lines + ["", "END_DATA_BLOCK", ""])


def render_library_instance_db(instance: InstanceSpec) -> str:
    metadata = LIBRARY_INSTANCE_METADATA.get(instance.fb_type, {})
    version = metadata.get("version", DEFAULT_LIBRARY_VERSION)
    optimized_access = metadata.get("optimized_access", DEFAULT_LIBRARY_OPTIMIZED_ACCESS)
    lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{instance.name}"',
        f"{{ S7_Optimized_Access := '{optimized_access}' }}",
        f"VERSION : {version}",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        f'"{instance.fb_type}"',
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        "END_DATA_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_db(fb_name: str) -> str:
    db_name = f"{fb_name}_DB"
    lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{db_name}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        f'"{fb_name}"',
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        "END_DATA_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_fb(document: TemplateDoc) -> str:
    rendered_body = render_template_code(document)
    lines = [
        f'FUNCTION_BLOCK "{document.name}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
    ]
    if rendered_body:
        lines.extend(rendered_body.splitlines())
    lines.extend(["", "END_FUNCTION_BLOCK", ""])
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_main_fb(template_names: list[str]) -> str:
    body_lines: list[str] = []
    for template_name in template_names:
        body_lines.append(f'        "{template_name}_DB"();')
        body_lines.append("")
    lines = [
        f'FUNCTION_BLOCK "{MAIN_FB_NAME}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        *body_lines,
        "END_FUNCTION_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_code(document: TemplateDoc) -> str:
    contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
    chunks: list[str] = []

    for context in contexts:
        rendered = apply_template(document.code_text, context)
        rendered = preserve_template_code(rendered)
        if rendered:
            chunks.append(rendered)
    return "\n".join(chunks)


def preserve_template_code(text: str) -> str:
    return text.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n").strip("\n")

def write_text(path: Path, content: str) -> None:
    path.write_text(content, encoding=SCL_ENCODING, newline="\n")



def clean_output_directory(output_dir: Path) -> None:
    for child in output_dir.iterdir():
        if child.is_dir():
            shutil.rmtree(child)
        else:
            child.unlink()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        raise SystemExit(main())
    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover - CLI friendly error path.
        print(f"Error: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
        raise

export function getCurrentBackendProjectId({ projectManager, backendSource }) {
