const lifecycleOutcomeStatuses = resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses();
const closeFlowDecisions = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions;
const backendLockReleaseResultStates = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.releaseResultStates;
const confirmContinueDecision = String(closeFlowDecisions?.continue || '').trim();
const confirmCancelDecision = String(closeFlowDecisions?.cancel || '').trim();
const successBackendLockReleaseStates = new Set([
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.released,
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.noBackendProject,
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.noLockToken
].map((state) => String(state || '').trim()).filter(Boolean));
const blockedBackendLockReleaseStates = new Set([
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.blockedActiveProcessBusy,
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.blockedLostProjectLock,
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.blockedFailure
].map((state) => String(state || '').trim()).filter(Boolean));
const malformedBackendLockReleaseState = String(
  backendLockReleaseResultStates.noClosePayload || ''
).trim();

function resolveConfirmSaveLifecycleOutcome({
  confirmResult,
  cancelDecision = ''
}) {
  const normalizedCancelDecision = String(cancelDecision || confirmCancelDecision).trim();
  const normalizedConfirmResult = typeof confirmResult === 'string'
    ? String(confirmResult).trim()
    : '';
  if (normalizedConfirmResult) {
    if (normalizedCancelDecision && normalizedConfirmResult === normalizedCancelDecision) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
      });
    }
    if (confirmContinueDecision && normalizedConfirmResult === confirmContinueDecision) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
      });
    }
    if (confirmCancelDecision && normalizedConfirmResult === confirmCancelDecision) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
      });
    }
  }

  return normalizeLifecycleOutcome(confirmResult, {
    fallbackStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
    truthyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
    falsyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
  });
}

function resolveReleaseLifecycleOutcome(releaseResult) {
  const legacyCanContinue = typeof releaseResult?.canContinue === 'boolean'
    ? releaseResult.canContinue
    : null;
  const legacyCanContinueFields = legacyCanContinue === null
    ? {}
    : { canContinue: legacyCanContinue };

  if (releaseResult && typeof releaseResult === 'object' && !Array.isArray(releaseResult)) {
    const legacyState = String(releaseResult.state || '').trim();
    if (legacyState) {
      if (successBackendLockReleaseStates.has(legacyState)) {
        return {
          ...createLifecycleOutcome({
            status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
            state: legacyState,
            errorCode: releaseResult.errorCode
          }),
          ...legacyCanContinueFields
        };
      }

      if (legacyState === malformedBackendLockReleaseState) {
        return {
          ...createLifecycleOutcome({
            status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
            state: legacyState,
            errorCode: releaseResult.errorCode
          }),
          ...legacyCanContinueFields
        };
      }

      if (blockedBackendLockReleaseStates.has(legacyState)) {
        return {
          ...createLifecycleOutcome({
            status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.blocked,
            state: legacyState,
            errorCode: releaseResult.errorCode
          }),
          ...legacyCanContinueFields
        };
      }
    }

    const normalized = normalizeLifecycleOutcome(releaseResult, {
      fallbackStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
      truthyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
      falsyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
    });
    if (normalized.status !== lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed || typeof releaseResult.canContinue === 'boolean') {
      return {
        ...normalized,
        ...legacyCanContinueFields
      };
    }
  }

  const normalizedRelease = normalizeLifecycleOutcome(releaseResult, {
    fallbackStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
    truthyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
    falsyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
  });
  return {
    ...normalizedRelease,
    ...legacyCanContinueFields
  };
}

function shouldContinueAfterBackendLockReleaseByStatus({ releaseResult }) {
  return resolveReleaseLifecycleOutcome(releaseResult).status === lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success;
}

export async function runNewProjectCreateFirstTransition({
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  cancelDecision,
  releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
  shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockReleaseByStatus,
  onBackendLockReleaseBlocked,
  stopReasonSwitch,
  closeAllTabs,
  clearLogs,
  closeProject,
  refreshProjectCatalog
}) {
  const confirmOutcome = resolveConfirmSaveLifecycleOutcome({
    confirmResult: await confirmSaveIfDirty(),
    cancelDecision
  });
  if (confirmOutcome.status !== lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success) {
    return confirmOutcome;
  }

  const releaseResult = resolveReleaseLifecycleOutcome(
    await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason: stopReasonSwitch })
  );
  const canContinueAfterRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease({ releaseResult });
  if (!canContinueAfterRelease) {
    onBackendLockReleaseBlocked?.(releaseResult);
    return releaseResult;
  }
  await closeAllTabs();
  clearLogs();
  await closeProject();
  await refreshProjectCatalog?.();
  return createLifecycleOutcome({
    status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
  });
}

export async function runCloseProjectTransition({
  getCurrentProject,
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  cancelDecision,
  releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
  shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockReleaseByStatus,
  onBackendLockReleaseBlocked,
  stopReasonClose,
  closeAllTabs,
  clearLogs,
  closeProject
}) {
  if (!getCurrentProject?.()) {
    return createLifecycleOutcome({
      status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
    });
  }

  const confirmOutcome = resolveConfirmSaveLifecycleOutcome({
    confirmResult: await confirmSaveIfDirty(),
    cancelDecision
  });
  if (confirmOutcome.status !== lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success) {
    return confirmOutcome;
  }

  const releaseResult = resolveReleaseLifecycleOutcome(
    await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason: stopReasonClose })
  );
  const canContinueAfterRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease({ releaseResult });
  if (!canContinueAfterRelease) {
    onBackendLockReleaseBlocked?.(releaseResult);
    return releaseResult;
  }
  await closeAllTabs();
  clearLogs();
  await closeProject();
  return createLifecycleOutcome({
    status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
  });
}

export async function runOpenBackendProjectTransition({
  projectId,
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  cancelDecision,
  releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
  shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockReleaseByStatus,
  onBackendLockReleaseBlocked,
  stopReasonSwitch,
  closeAllTabs,
  clearLogs,
  closeProject,
  openProjectById
}) {
  const normalizedProjectId = String(projectId || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedProjectId) {
    return createLifecycleOutcome({
      status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
    });
  }

  const confirmOutcome = resolveConfirmSaveLifecycleOutcome({
    confirmResult: await confirmSaveIfDirty(),
    cancelDecision
  });
  if (confirmOutcome.status !== lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success) {
    return confirmOutcome;
  }

  const releaseResult = resolveReleaseLifecycleOutcome(
    await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason: stopReasonSwitch })
  );
  const canContinueAfterRelease = shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease({ releaseResult });
  if (!canContinueAfterRelease) {
    onBackendLockReleaseBlocked?.(releaseResult);
    return releaseResult;
  }

  await closeAllTabs();
  clearLogs();
  await closeProject();
  return normalizeLifecycleOutcome(await openProjectById(normalizedProjectId), {
    fallbackStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
    truthyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
    falsyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
  });
}

export function shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease({ releaseResult }) {
  return shouldContinueAfterBackendLockReleaseByStatus({ releaseResult });
}

export function resolveBackendLockReleaseBlockedMessage({
  releaseResult,
  releaseResultStates,
  text
}) {
  return resolveBackendLockReleaseBlockedMessageRuntime({
    releaseResult,
    releaseResultStates,
    text
  });
}

export function logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransition({
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  releaseResult,
  reason = '',
  releaseResultStates,
  text
}) {
  return logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransitionRuntime({
    loggerWarn,
    loggerSource,
    releaseResult,
    reason,
    releaseResultStates,
    text
  });
}

export function resolveBackendProjectNextFreeNumber({
  projects = [],
  namePrefix = '',
  separator = ' ',
  minimumNumber = 1
}) {
  const normalizedPrefix = String(namePrefix || '').trim();
  const normalizedSeparator = String(separator || '');
  const normalizedMinimumNumber = Number.isInteger(minimumNumber) && minimumNumber > 0
    ? minimumNumber
    : 1;
  if (!normalizedPrefix) {
    return normalizedMinimumNumber;
  }

  const expectedPrefix = `${normalizedPrefix}${normalizedSeparator}`;
  const usedNumbers = new Set();

  for (const project of projects) {
    const projectName = String(project?.name || '').trim();
    if (!projectName.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
      continue;
    }
    const suffix = projectName.slice(expectedPrefix.length).trim();
    if (!/^\d+$/.test(suffix)) {
      continue;
    }
    const number = Number.parseInt(suffix, 10);
    if (Number.isInteger(number) && number >= normalizedMinimumNumber) {
      usedNumbers.add(number);
    }
  }

  let candidate = normalizedMinimumNumber;
  while (usedNumbers.has(candidate)) {
    candidate += 1;
  }
  return candidate;
}

export function resolveBackendProjectDefaultName({
  projects = [],
  namePrefix = '',
  separator = ' ',
  minimumNumber = 1
}) {
  const nextNumber = resolveBackendProjectNextFreeNumber({
    projects,
    namePrefix,
    separator,
    minimumNumber
  });
  return `${String(namePrefix || '').trim()}${String(separator || '')}${nextNumber}`.trim();
}

function buildMalformedRuntimeSuccessFailureFields({
  message = '',
  result = null
} = {}) {
  const normalizedMessage = String(message || '').trim();
  return buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields({
    error: {
      message: normalizedMessage,
      details: {
        result: result ?? null
      }
    }
  });
}

export async function importBackendProjectFlow({
  openProjectImportArchiveDialog,
  importProjectArchive,
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  backendImportFailedText,
  backendActiveProcessBusyText,
  activeProcessBusyErrorCode
}) {
  const selectedArchive = await openProjectImportArchiveDialog();
  if (!selectedArchive) {
    return '';
  }

  let response = null;
  try {
    response = await importProjectArchive({
      fileName: selectedArchive.fileName,
      bytes: selectedArchive.bytes
    });
  } catch (error) {
    loggerWarn(
      loggerSource,
      backendImportFailedText,
      buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields({ error })
    );
    return '';
  }

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorCode = String(response?.error?.code || '').trim();
    const warningText = errorCode === String(activeProcessBusyErrorCode || '').trim()
      ? backendActiveProcessBusyText
      : backendImportFailedText;
    const failureFields = buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields(response);
    loggerWarn(
      loggerSource,
      warningText,
      failureFields
    );
    return '';
  }

  const importedProjectId = String(response?.result?.project?.id || '').trim();
  if (!importedProjectId) {
    loggerWarn(
      loggerSource,
      backendImportFailedText,
      buildMalformedRuntimeSuccessFailureFields({
        message: backendImportFailedText,
        result: response?.result ?? null
      })
    );
    return '';
  }

  return importedProjectId;
}

export function resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation({
  errorCode,
  errorCodes,
  text
}) {
  return resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentationRuntime({
    errorCode,
    errorCodes,
    text
  });
}

export function resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource
}) {
  return resolveBackendProjectForExportFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });
}

export function resolvePlatformActionEnabledState({
  actionId,
  actionIds,
  currentProject,
  backendSource
}) {
  const hasProject = Boolean(currentProject);
  const exportProject = resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });

  if (actionId === actionIds.closeProject) {
    return hasProject;
  }
  if (
    actionId === actionIds.saveProject
    || actionId === actionIds.saveProjectAs
    || actionId === actionIds.exportProject
  ) {
    return Boolean(exportProject);
  }

  return true;
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
  applyStaticText();

  const logger = createCoreLogger({
    sinks: [
      createDomLogSink({ output: document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.logContainerId) }),
      createConsoleLogSink()
    ]
  });
  const commandBus = createCommandBus({ logger });
  const moduleRegistry = createModuleRegistry({ logger });
  const shell = createShellAdapter();
  const workbenchLayout = initWorkbenchLayout();
  const backendRuntimeClient = createRuntimeClient({
    adapter: createHttpRuntimeAdapter({
      baseUrl: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.baseUrl,
      endpointPath: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandsEndpoint,
      importEndpointPath: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.projectImportsEndpoint,
      timeoutMs: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestTimeoutMs,
      defaultHeaders: {
        [APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.headerName]: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.userId
      },
      errorCodes: {
        internal: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.internal
      },
      importArchiveFieldName: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.importContract.archiveFieldName
    })
  });

  let projectManager = null;
  const getProjectManager = () => projectManager;

  const metaGenModule = createMetaGenModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaLabModule = createMetaLabModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaViewModule = createMetaViewModule({ logger, getProjectManager });

  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaGenModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaLabModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaViewModule);

  const paramsUndoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsUndoButtonId);
  const paramsRedoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsRedoButtonId);
  let disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;
  let disposeGenerationReadinessSubscription = null;
  let activeGenerationReadinessState = null;

  function updateActiveGenerationReadinessState(nextReadiness = null) {
    activeGenerationReadinessState = nextReadiness && typeof nextReadiness === 'object'
      ? nextReadiness
      : null;
  }

  function readActiveRuntimeGenerationReadiness() {
    const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
    if (typeof runtime?.getGenerationReadiness !== 'function') {
      return null;
    }

    return runtime.getGenerationReadiness();
  }

  async function applyDocumentSnapshotToProjectState(record, metadata = {}) {
    if (!record?.moduleId || !record?.path || !record?.document) {
      return null;
    }

    if (record.moduleId === APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.temporary || metadata?.isTemporary) {
      return record;
    }

    try {
      await projectManager?.replaceDocumentRecord(record);
      return record;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project,
        'Не удалось синхронизировать snapshot документа в состояние проекта',
        {
          reason: String(metadata?.reason || ''),
          tabId: String(metadata?.tabId || ''),
          identity: getDocumentIdentityKey(record),
          message: error?.message || String(error)
        }
      );
      return null;
    }
  }

  const tabs = createWorkbenchTabs({
    logger,
    onActiveEntryChanged: () => {
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription?.();
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;
      disposeGenerationReadinessSubscription?.();
      disposeGenerationReadinessSubscription = null;

      const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
      if (typeof runtime?.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState === 'function') {
        disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = runtime.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState(() => {
          updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
        });
      }
      if (typeof runtime?.subscribeGenerationReadiness === 'function') {
        disposeGenerationReadinessSubscription = runtime.subscribeGenerationReadiness((readiness) => {
          updateActiveGenerationReadinessState(readiness);
          renderProcessPanel();
        });
      }

      updateActiveGenerationReadinessState(readActiveRuntimeGenerationReadiness());

      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      renderProcessPanel();
    },
    onRenameDocument: async (...args) => projectManager?.renameDocument(...args),
    onSyncDocumentRecord: async (record, metadata) => applyDocumentSnapshotToProjectState(record, metadata),
    openEditor: async ({ documentRecord, mountElement }) => {
      const module = moduleRegistry.findModuleByDocumentKind(documentRecord.document?.kind);

      if (!module) {
        throw new Error(`Не найден модуль для kind=${documentRecord.document?.kind}`);
      }

      const runtime = await module.openDocument({
        documentRecord,
        mountElement,
        onDirty: () => projectManager?.markDocumentDirty(getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord))
      });

      decorateEditorPanelHeaders(mountElement);
      return runtime;
    }
  });

  function decorateEditorPanelHeaders(rootNode) {
    const headerIconByLabel = new Map([
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.params, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.params],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.data, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.data],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.code, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.code],
      [METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.instances, METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.instances]
    ]);
    const headerSelector = `.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`;
    const headerNodes = rootNode.querySelectorAll?.(headerSelector) || [];

    for (const headerNode of headerNodes) {
      const normalizedText = String(headerNode.textContent || '').trim();
      const iconAssetPath = headerIconByLabel.get(normalizedText);
      if (!iconAssetPath) {
        continue;
      }

      headerNode.innerHTML = '';

      const iconHost = document.createElement('span');
      iconHost.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.iconHost);
      const iconImage = document.createElement('img');
      iconImage.src = iconAssetPath;
      iconImage.alt = '';
      iconImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
      iconImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
      iconImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
      iconImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
      iconImage.decoding = 'async';
      iconImage.loading = 'eager';
      iconImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      iconHost.appendChild(iconImage);
      headerNode.appendChild(iconHost);

      const textNode = document.createElement('span');
      textNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.panelHeaderText);
      textNode.textContent = normalizedText;
      headerNode.appendChild(textNode);
    }
  }

  const {
    processPanelNode,
    processTitleNode,
    processContextNode,
    processGenerateButton,
    processStopButton,
    processCommandLabelNode,
    processCommandNode,
    processStatusLabelNode,
    processStatusNode,
    processExitCodeLabelNode,
    processExitCodeNode,
    processOutputNode
  } = resolveProcessPanelSurfaceNodes({
    dom: APP_CONFIG.ui.dom
  });
  const platformActionIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.platformActions.ids;
  const {
    surfaceNode: platformActionSurfaceNode,
    buttonsById: platformActionButtonsById
  } = resolvePlatformActionSurfaceNodes({
    actionIds: platformActionIds
  });
  const platformActionSource = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.source;
  const platformActionLoggerSource = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.loggerSource;
  const platformActionDispatchMessages = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.dispatchMessages;
  const platformActionTransitionPrefix = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.webActionPrefix;
  const webSurfacePlatformActionOrder = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.webSurfaceActionOrder;
  const webSurfacePlatformActionDomByActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.webSurfaceDomByActionId;
  const platformActionLabels = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionLabels;
  const platformActionAriaLabels = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionAriaLabels;
  const platformActionDisabledHints = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionDisabledHints;
  const backendLockReleaseStates = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.releaseResultStates;
  const processRuntimeConfig = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.processExecution;
  const processExecutionPreflightConfig = processRuntimeConfig.preflight;
  const processCommandIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands;
  const backendPayloadFieldNames = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.payloadFields;
  const processStatusByCode = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processStatusByCode;
  const backendCatalogFlowConfig = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendCatalogFlow;
  const backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints = backendCatalogFlowConfig.entryPoints;
  const backendCatalogFlowActionContexts = backendCatalogFlowConfig.actionContexts;
  const backendCatalogFlowEventIds = backendCatalogFlowConfig.eventIds;
  const backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons = backendCatalogFlowConfig.failureReasons;
  const backendCatalogFlowLoggerSource = backendCatalogFlowConfig.loggerSource;
  const backendLockReleaseLoggerSource = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend;
  let nextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse;
  let backendRequestCounter = 0;

  function logBackendCatalogFlowInfo(message, details = null) {
    logger.info(backendCatalogFlowLoggerSource, message, details);
  }

  function logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(message, details = null) {
    logger.warn(backendCatalogFlowLoggerSource, message, details);
  }

  function resolveBackendCommandFailureFields(commandOutcome) {
    return buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields(commandOutcome);
  }

  function resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
    message = '',
    result = null
  } = {}) {
    return buildMalformedRuntimeSuccessFailureFields({
      message,
      result
    });
  }

  function logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransitionWithAppLogger(releaseResult, reason = '') {
    logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransition({
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: backendLockReleaseLoggerSource,
      releaseResult,
      reason,
      releaseResultStates: backendLockReleaseStates,
      text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
    });
  }

  function setNextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint(entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse) {
    nextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint = entryPoint;
  }

  function consumeBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint() {
    const entryPoint = nextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint;
    nextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse;
    return entryPoint;
  }

  const platformActionSurfaceController = createPlatformActionSurfaceController({
    surfaceNode: platformActionSurfaceNode,
    buttonsById: platformActionButtonsById,
    actionIds: platformActionIds,
    actionOrder: webSurfacePlatformActionOrder,
    actionDomByActionId: webSurfacePlatformActionDomByActionId,
    classNames: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames,
    labelsByActionId: platformActionLabels,
    ariaLabelsByActionId: platformActionAriaLabels,
    disabledHintsByActionId: platformActionDisabledHints,
    getCurrentProject: () => projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null,
    resolveEnabledState: resolvePlatformActionEnabledState,
    backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
  });
  platformActionSurfaceController.updateState();

  setupProcessPanelSurface({
    processPanelNode,
    processTitleNode,
    processContextNode,
    processGenerateButton,
    processStopButton,
    processCommandLabelNode,
    processCommandNode,
    processStatusLabelNode,
    processStatusNode,
    processExitCodeLabelNode,
    processExitCodeNode,
    processOutputNode,
    classNames: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames,
    text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
  });

  function resolveProcessContextProjectId() {
    return getCurrentBackendProjectId({
      projectManager,
      backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
    });
  }

  let processExecutionOrchestrator = null;

  function readProcessSnapshot() {
    const snapshot = processExecutionOrchestrator?.getSnapshot?.();
    if (!snapshot || typeof snapshot !== 'object') {
      return {
        process: null,
        commandFailure: null,
        outputChunks: []
      };
    }

    return {
      process: snapshot.process || null,
      commandFailure: snapshot.commandFailure || null,
      outputChunks: Array.isArray(snapshot.outputChunks) ? snapshot.outputChunks : []
    };
  }

  function renderProcessPanel({ preflightRejection = null } = {}) {
    const snapshot = readProcessSnapshot();
    const viewState = resolveProcessPanelPresentationState({
      contextProjectId: resolveProcessContextProjectId(),
      runtimeSnapshot: snapshot,
      preflightRejection,
      generationReadiness: activeGenerationReadinessState,
      processRuntimeConfig,
      processStatusByCode,
      processStreams: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.process.streams,
      classNames: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames,
      text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
    });

    if (processContextNode) {
      processContextNode.textContent = viewState.contextText;
    }

    if (processCommandNode) {
      processCommandNode.textContent = viewState.commandText;
    }

    if (processStatusNode) {
      processStatusNode.textContent = viewState.statusText;
    }

    if (processExitCodeNode) {
      processExitCodeNode.textContent = viewState.exitCodeText;
    }

    if (processGenerateButton) {
      processGenerateButton.disabled = !viewState.canGenerate;
      processGenerateButton.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionDisabled, !viewState.canGenerate);
    }

    if (processStopButton) {
      processStopButton.disabled = !viewState.canStop;
      processStopButton.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionDisabled, !viewState.canStop);
    }

    if (!processOutputNode) {
      return;
    }

    processOutputNode.replaceChildren();

    if (viewState.outputIsEmpty) {
      processOutputNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode(viewState.outputEmptyText));
      return;
    }

    for (const line of viewState.outputLines) {
      const lineNode = document.createElement('span');
      lineNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutputLine);
      lineNode.classList.add(line.className);
      lineNode.textContent = line.text;
      processOutputNode.appendChild(lineNode);
      processOutputNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode('\n'));
    }
    processOutputNode.scrollTop = processOutputNode.scrollHeight;
  }

  function nextBackendRequestId() {
    backendRequestCounter += 1;
    return `${APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestIdPrefix}${backendRequestCounter}`;
  }

  const backendCommandSessionOrchestrator = createBackendCommandSessionOrchestrator({
    backendRuntimeClient,
    nextBackendRequestId,
    getProjectManager: () => projectManager,
    resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation,
    loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
    loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
    backendText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text,
    commandModuleId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.moduleIds.platform,
    backendCommands: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands,
    backendErrorCodes: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes,
    backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
    backendLockReleaseStates,
    backendHeartbeatIntervalMs: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.lockSession.heartbeatIntervalMs,
    backendHeartbeatFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendHeartbeatFailed,
    backendHeartbeatStopReasonLost: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonLost,
    backendHeartbeatStopReasonSwitch: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch
  });

  function stopBackendHeartbeat(reason = '') {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.stopBackendHeartbeat(reason);
  }

  function handleLostBackendProjectLock() {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.handleLostBackendProjectLock();
  }

  async function executeBackendCommand(command, payload = {}) {
    return backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.executeBackendCommand(command, payload);
  }

  processExecutionOrchestrator = createProcessExecutionOrchestrator({
    executeBackendCommand,
    commandIds: {
      metagenGenerate: processCommandIds.metagenGenerate,
      processGetState: processCommandIds.processGetState,
      processReadOutput: processCommandIds.processReadOutput,
      processStop: processCommandIds.processStop
    },
    terminalStatuses: processRuntimeConfig.terminalStatuses,
    pollingIntervalMs: processRuntimeConfig.pollingIntervalMs,
    onUpdate: () => {
      renderProcessPanel();
    }
  });

  const metagenGeneratorBridge = createMetaGenGeneratorBridge({
    launchGenerate: (payload) => processExecutionOrchestrator.launchGenerate(payload),
    resolveGenerationReadiness: () => activeGenerationReadinessState,
    preflightErrorCode: processExecutionPreflightConfig.errorCodes.generateBlocked
  });

  async function syncProcessSurfaceWithContext() {
    updateActiveGenerationReadinessState(readActiveRuntimeGenerationReadiness());
    const contextProjectId = resolveProcessContextProjectId();
    if (!contextProjectId) {
      processExecutionOrchestrator?.clearSnapshot?.();
      return;
    }
    await processExecutionOrchestrator.syncActiveProcess();
  }

  async function runMetagenGenerate() {
    updateActiveGenerationReadinessState(readActiveRuntimeGenerationReadiness());
    const contextProjectId = resolveProcessContextProjectId();
    if (!contextProjectId) {
      processExecutionOrchestrator.clearSnapshot();
      return;
    }
    try {
      await metagenGeneratorBridge.generate({ projectId: contextProjectId });
    } catch (error) {
      const preflightGenerateBlockedCode = processExecutionPreflightConfig.errorCodes.generateBlocked;
      const errorCode = String(error?.code || '').trim();
      if (errorCode === preflightGenerateBlockedCode) {
        renderProcessPanel({
          preflightRejection: {
            command: processCommandIds.metagenGenerate,
            code: preflightGenerateBlockedCode,
            message: String(error?.message || '').trim()
          }
        });
      } else {
        logger.warn(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
          { message: String(error?.message || String(error)).trim(), errorCode }
        );
        renderProcessPanel();
      }
    }
  }

  async function stopActiveProcess() {
    await processExecutionOrchestrator.stopProcess();
  }

  processGenerateButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void runMetagenGenerate();
  });

  processStopButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void stopActiveProcess();
  });

  renderProcessPanel();
  void syncProcessSurfaceWithContext();

  async function releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason = '' } = {}) {
    return backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason });
  }

  function startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(reason = '') {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(reason);
  }

  async function exportBackendProject(project) {
    await runBackendProjectExport({
      project,
      exportCommandId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.exportProject,
      executeBackendCommand,
      downloadBinary: (downloadUrl) => backendRuntimeClient.downloadBinary(downloadUrl),
      saveBinaryFileAsDialog: (payload) => shell.requestBinarySaveAs(payload),
      dialogs: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs,
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
      downloadFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendExportDownloadFailed,
      backendCommandFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed
    });
  }

  async function refreshBackendProjectCatalog({
    refreshProjects = false
  } = {}) {
    if (!refreshProjects) {
      return [];
    }

    try {
      return await loadBackendProjectCatalogForPicker();
    } catch (_error) {
      return [];
    }
  }

  async function loadBackendProjectCatalogForPicker({
    entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
    actionContext = backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.loadProjects
  } = {}) {
    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.listProjects
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok) {
      const failureFields = resolveBackendCommandFailureFields(commandResult);
      logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowBrowseLoadFailed,
        {
          eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.browseLoadFailed,
          entryPoint,
          actionContext,
          ...failureFields
        }
      );
      throw new Error(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerError);
    }

    const projects = commandResult?.result?.projects;
    if (!Array.isArray(projects)) {
      logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowBrowseLoadFailed,
        {
          eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.browseLoadFailed,
          entryPoint,
          actionContext,
          reason: backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.transitionBlocked,
          ...resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
            message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowBrowseLoadFailed,
            result: commandResult?.result ?? null
          })
        }
      );
      throw new Error(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerError);
    }

    return projects;
  }

  async function openBackendProjectById(
    projectId,
    {
      entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
      actionContext = backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.open
    } = {}
  ) {
    return runOpenBackendProjectTransition({
      projectId,
      confirmSaveIfDirty,
      cancelDecision: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled,
      releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
      shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease,
      onBackendLockReleaseBlocked: (releaseResult) => {
        logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransitionWithAppLogger(
          releaseResult,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch
        );
      },
      stopReasonSwitch: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch,
      closeAllTabs: () => tabs.closeAllTabs(),
      clearLogs: () => logger.clear(),
      closeProject: () => projectManager.closeProject(),
      openProjectById: async (normalizedProjectId) => {
        const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
          APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.openProject,
          {
            projectId: normalizedProjectId
          }
        );
        const snapshot = commandResult?.result?.snapshot || null;
        const lockToken = String(commandResult?.result?.lockToken || '').trim();

        if (!commandResult?.ok || !snapshot || !lockToken) {
          let failureReason = backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.transitionBlocked;
          let failureFields = resolveBackendCommandFailureFields(commandResult);
          if (!commandResult?.ok) {
            failureReason = backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.openCommandFailed;
          } else if (!snapshot) {
            failureReason = backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.missingSnapshot;
            failureFields = resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
              message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowOpenRejected,
              result: commandResult?.result ?? null
            });
          } else {
            failureReason = backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.missingLockToken;
            failureFields = resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
              message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowOpenRejected,
              result: commandResult?.result ?? null
            });
          }
          if (commandResult?.ok && !lockToken) {
            logger.warn(
              APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
              APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost
            );
            handleLostBackendProjectLock();
          }
          logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
            APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowOpenRejected,
            {
              eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.openRejected,
              entryPoint,
              actionContext,
              projectId: normalizedProjectId,
              reason: failureReason,
              ...failureFields
            }
          );
          return createLifecycleOutcome({
            status: commandResult?.ok
              ? lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
              : lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed,
            reason: failureReason,
            errorCode: commandResult?.errorCode || ''
          });
        }

        await projectManager.openProjectSnapshot(snapshot, { lockToken });
        await renderTree();
        logger.clear();
        startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
        logBackendCatalogFlowInfo(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowOpenSucceeded,
          {
            eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.openSucceeded,
            entryPoint,
            actionContext,
            projectId: normalizedProjectId
          }
        );
        return createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
        });
      }
    });
  }

  async function importBackendProject() {
    return importBackendProjectFlow({
      openProjectImportArchiveDialog: () => shell.requestProjectImportArchive(),
      importProjectArchive: (payload) => backendRuntimeClient.importProjectArchive(payload),
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: backendCatalogFlowLoggerSource,
      backendImportFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendImportFailed,
      backendActiveProcessBusyText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendActiveProcessBusy,
      activeProcessBusyErrorCode: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.activeProcessBusy
    });
  }

  const backendProjectPickerActionHandlers = new Map([
    [
      APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.importProject,
      async ({
        entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
        actionContext = backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.import
      } = {}) => {
        const importedProjectId = await importBackendProject();
        const normalizedProjectId = String(importedProjectId || '').trim();
        if (normalizedProjectId) {
          logBackendCatalogFlowInfo(
            APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowImportSucceeded,
            {
              eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.importSucceeded,
              entryPoint,
              actionContext,
              projectId: normalizedProjectId
            }
          );
        }
        return normalizedProjectId
          ? { projectId: normalizedProjectId }
          : null;
      }
    ],
    [
      APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.createProject,
      async ({
        payload = {},
        projects = [],
        entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
        actionContext = backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.create
      } = {}) => {
        const requestedProjectName = String(payload?.name || '').trim();
        const defaultProjectName = resolveBackendProjectDefaultName({
          projects: Array.isArray(projects) ? projects : [],
          namePrefix: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.prefix,
          separator: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.separator,
          minimumNumber: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.minimumNumber
        });
        const projectNameToCreate = requestedProjectName || defaultProjectName;
        const createResult = await executeBackendCommand(
          APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.createProject,
          {
            name: projectNameToCreate,
            [backendPayloadFieldNames.projectComment]: String(payload?.comment || '').trim()
          }
        );
        const createdProjectId = String(createResult?.result?.project?.id || '').trim();
        if (!createResult?.ok || !createdProjectId) {
          const failureFields = !createResult?.ok
            ? resolveBackendCommandFailureFields(createResult)
            : resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
              message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowCreateRejected,
              result: createResult?.result ?? null
            });
          const failureReason = !createResult?.ok
            ? backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.createCommandFailed
            : backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.createResultMissingProjectId;
          logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
            APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowCreateRejected,
            {
              eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.createRejected,
              entryPoint,
              actionContext,
              projectName: projectNameToCreate,
              ...failureFields,
              reason: failureReason
            }
          );
          return null;
        }
        logBackendCatalogFlowInfo(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowCreateSucceeded,
          {
            eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.createSucceeded,
            entryPoint,
            actionContext,
            projectId: createdProjectId,
            projectName: projectNameToCreate
          }
        );
        return { projectId: createdProjectId };
      }
    ],
    [
      APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.deleteProject,
      async ({
        payload = {},
        entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
        actionContext = backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.delete
      } = {}) => {
        const projectIdToDelete = String(payload?.projectId || '').trim();
        if (!projectIdToDelete) {
          return null;
        }
        const deleteResult = await executeBackendCommand(
          APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.deleteProject,
          {
            projectId: projectIdToDelete
          }
        );
        if (!deleteResult?.ok) {
          const failureFields = resolveBackendCommandFailureFields(deleteResult);
          logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
            APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowDeleteRejected,
            {
              eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.deleteRejected,
              entryPoint,
              actionContext,
              projectId: projectIdToDelete,
              ...failureFields,
              reason: backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.deleteCommandFailed
            }
          );
          return null;
        }
        const currentBackendProjectId = getCurrentBackendProjectId({
          projectManager,
          backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
        });
        if (currentBackendProjectId === projectIdToDelete) {
          await tabs.closeAllTabs();
          logger.clear();
          await projectManager.closeProject();
        }
        logBackendCatalogFlowInfo(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowDeleteSucceeded,
          {
            eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.deleteSucceeded,
            entryPoint,
            actionContext,
            projectId: projectIdToDelete
          }
        );
        return { deletedProjectId: projectIdToDelete };
      }
    ],
    [
      APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.exportProject,
      async ({
        payload = {},
        projects = []
      } = {}) => {
        const projectIdToExport = String(payload?.projectId || '').trim();
        if (!projectIdToExport) {
          return null;
        }
        const targetProject = (Array.isArray(projects) ? projects : []).find((item) => {
          return String(item?.id || '').trim() === projectIdToExport;
        });
        if (!targetProject) {
          return null;
        }

        await exportBackendProject({
          ...targetProject,
          id: projectIdToExport
        });
        return {
          projectId: projectIdToExport,
          project: targetProject
        };
      }
    ]
  ]);

  async function executeBackendProjectPickerAction({
    actionId,
    payload = {},
    projects = [],
    entryPoint = backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse
  } = {}) {
    const normalizedActionId = String(actionId || '').trim();
    if (!normalizedActionId) {
      return null;
    }

    const actionHandler = backendProjectPickerActionHandlers.get(normalizedActionId);
    if (typeof actionHandler !== 'function') {
      return null;
    }

    const actionContext = normalizedActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.createProject
      ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.create
      : normalizedActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.deleteProject
        ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.delete
        : normalizedActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.exportProject
          ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.open
      : backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.import;

    return actionHandler({
      payload,
      projects: Array.isArray(projects) ? projects : [],
      entryPoint,
      actionContext
    });
  }

  function getActiveParamsUndoRedoState() {
    const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
    if (!runtime?.supportsParamsUndoRedo?.()) {
      return {
        runtime: null,
        supported: false,
        isContextActive: false,
        canUndo: false,
        canRedo: false
      };
    }

    const state = runtime.getParamsUndoRedoState?.();
    const isContextActive = Boolean(
      state?.isContextActive
      ?? state?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive
      ?? state?.isHotkeyContextActive
      ?? runtime?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive?.()
    );

    return {
      runtime,
      supported: Boolean(state?.supported ?? true),
      isContextActive,
      canUndo: Boolean(state?.canUndo ?? runtime?.canUndoParams?.()),
      canRedo: Boolean(state?.canRedo ?? runtime?.canRedoParams?.())
    };
  }

  function updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState() {
    if (!paramsUndoButton || !paramsRedoButton) {
      return;
    }

    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();

    paramsUndoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo;
    paramsRedoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo;
  }

  async function triggerParamsUndo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.undoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  async function triggerParamsRedo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.redoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  paramsUndoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsUndo();
  });

  paramsRedoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsRedo();
  });

  document.addEventListener('focusin', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  });
  document.addEventListener('pointerdown', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }, true);
  updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();


  projectManager = createProjectManager({
    logger,
    runtimeShell: shell,
    moduleRegistry,
    onProjectLoaded: ({ projectRuntime }) => {
      platformActionSurfaceController.updateState();
      void syncProcessSurfaceWithContext();
    },
    onProjectClosed: () => {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonClose);
      processExecutionOrchestrator?.clearSnapshot?.();
      platformActionSurfaceController.updateState();
    }
  });

  const tree = createProjectTree({
    logger,
    projectManager,
    tabs
  });

  const renderTree = async () => {
    await tree.renderSafely();
  };

  projectManager.subscribe(() => {
    void renderTree();
  });
  async function finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow() {
    await renderTree();
    logger.clear();
    return createLifecycleOutcome({
      status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
    });
  }

  async function saveBackendProjectFlow(openDocuments) {
    let payload = null;
    try {
      payload = buildBackendSavePayloadForSession({
        currentProject: projectManager.getCurrentProject(),
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
        projectSnapshot: projectManager.exportProjectSnapshot(openDocuments)
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost,
        { message: error?.message || String(error) }
      );
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }
    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveAll,
      payload
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed,
        errorCode: commandResult?.errorCode || ''
      });
    }

    if (!commandResult?.result || typeof commandResult.result !== 'object') {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }

    if (!commandResult?.result?.project || typeof commandResult.result.project !== 'object') {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
        resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
          message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
          result: commandResult?.result ?? null
        })
      );
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }

    const isCommitted = projectManager.commitBackendSave(commandResult.result.project);
    if (!isCommitted) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
      });
    }
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
    return finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow();
  }

  async function saveBackendProjectAsFlow({ project, openDocuments }) {
    const initialProjectDisplayFields = resolveBackendProjectDisplayFieldsFromRuntimeProject({
      currentProject: project,
      backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
      fallbackName: APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName
    }) || {
      name: APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName,
      hasComment: false,
      comment: ''
    };
    const initialName = initialProjectDisplayFields.name;
    const initialComment = initialProjectDisplayFields.comment;

    let existingProjects = [];
    try {
      existingProjects = await loadBackendProjectCatalogForPicker({
        entryPoint: backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
        actionContext: backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.loadProjects
      });
    } catch (_error) {
      existingProjects = [];
    }
    const duplicateValidationProjects = existingProjects.filter((catalogProject) => {
      const projectId = String(catalogProject?.id || '').trim();
      const currentProjectId = resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject({
        currentProject: project,
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
      });
      return projectId && projectId !== currentProjectId;
    });

    const dialogResult = await showProjectSaveAsDialog({
      initialName,
      initialComment,
      existingProjects: duplicateValidationProjects
    });
    const normalizedDialogResult = normalizeProjectSaveAsDialogResult(dialogResult);

    if (normalizedDialogResult.isCancelled) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
      });
    }
    if (normalizedDialogResult.isMalformed) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }

    let payload = null;
    try {
      payload = buildBackendSaveAsPayloadForSession({
        currentProject: projectManager.getCurrentProject(),
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
        projectSnapshot: projectManager.exportProjectSnapshot(openDocuments),
        payloadFields: backendPayloadFieldNames,
        newName: normalizedDialogResult.name,
        comment: normalizedDialogResult.comment
      });
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost,
        { message: error?.message || String(error) }
      );
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }

    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveProjectAs,
      payload
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed,
        errorCode: commandResult?.errorCode || ''
      });
    }

    if (!commandResult?.result?.project || !commandResult?.result?.lockToken) {
      if (commandResult?.ok && !commandResult?.result?.project) {
        logger.warn(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
          resolveMalformedBackendCommandSuccessFailureFields({
            message: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCommandFailed,
            result: commandResult?.result ?? null
          })
        );
      }
      if (commandResult?.ok && !commandResult?.result?.lockToken) {
        logger.warn(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost
        );
        handleLostBackendProjectLock();
      }
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
        state: !commandResult?.result?.project
          ? backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.missingSnapshot
          : backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.missingLockToken
      });
    }

    const isCommitted = projectManager.commitBackendSaveAs({
      ...(commandResult.result?.project || {}),
      lockToken: commandResult.result?.lockToken
    });
    if (!isCommitted) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
      });
    }
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
    return finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow();
  }

  async function syncOpenDocumentsToProjectState(openDocuments = []) {
    for (const record of openDocuments) {
      await applyDocumentSnapshotToProjectState(record, {
        reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.collectOpenDocumentRecords
      });
    }
  }

  async function saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs = false } = {}) {
    const project = projectManager.getCurrentProject();

    if (!project) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, APP_CONFIG.ui.text.noProjectToSave);
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
      });
    }

    if (project.source !== APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendSaveRequiresOpenedBackendProject, {
        source: project.source || ''
      });
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
      });
    }

    const openDocuments = await tabs.collectOpenDocumentRecords();
    await syncOpenDocumentsToProjectState(openDocuments);
    if (forceSaveAs) {
      return saveBackendProjectAsFlow({ project, openDocuments });
    }

    return saveBackendProjectFlow(openDocuments);
  }

  async function confirmSaveIfDirty() {
    if (!projectManager.hasDirtyProject()) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
      });
    }

    const decision = await showSaveChangesDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.saveChangesTitle
    });
    const normalizedDialogDecision = normalizeSaveChangesDialogResult(decision);

    if (normalizedDialogDecision.isMalformed) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }
    if (normalizedDialogDecision.isCancel) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
      });
    }
    if (normalizedDialogDecision.isDiscard) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success
      });
    }

    return normalizeLifecycleOutcome(await saveProjectFlow(), {
      fallbackStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed,
      truthyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.success,
      falsyStatus: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
    });
  }

  async function newProjectFlow() {
    setNextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint(backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse);
    return openProjectFlow();
  }

  async function importProjectFlow() {
    const importedProjectId = await importBackendProject();
    if (!importedProjectId) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.failed
      });
    }

    return openBackendProjectById(importedProjectId, {
      entryPoint: backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.browse,
      actionContext: backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.import
    });
  }

  async function openProjectFlow() {
    const entryPoint = consumeBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint();
    const pickerSelection = await showBackendProjectPickerDialog({
      loadProjects: () => loadBackendProjectCatalogForPicker({
        entryPoint,
        actionContext: backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.loadProjects
      }),
      executeAction: ({ actionId, projects, payload }) => executeBackendProjectPickerAction({
        actionId,
        payload,
        projects,
        entryPoint
      })
    });
    if (!pickerSelection) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled
      });
    }

    const pickerActionId = String(pickerSelection?.actionId || '').trim();
    const openActionContext = pickerActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.createProject
      ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.create
      : pickerActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.deleteProject
        ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.delete
      : pickerActionId === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.importProject
        ? backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.import
        : backendCatalogFlowActionContexts.open;

    const projectIdToOpen = String(
      pickerSelection.projectId
      || pickerSelection?.project?.id
      || ''
    ).trim();

    if (!projectIdToOpen) {
      logBackendCatalogFlowWarn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCatalogFlowOpenRejected,
        {
          eventId: backendCatalogFlowEventIds.openRejected,
          entryPoint,
          actionContext: openActionContext,
          reason: backendCatalogFlowFailureReasons.invalidProjectId
        }
      );
      return createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.malformed
      });
    }

    return openBackendProjectById(projectIdToOpen, {
      entryPoint,
      actionContext: openActionContext
    });
  }

  async function closeProjectFlow() {
    return runCloseProjectTransition({
      getCurrentProject: () => projectManager.getCurrentProject(),
      confirmSaveIfDirty,
      cancelDecision: lifecycleOutcomeStatuses.cancelled,
      releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
      shouldContinueAfterBackendLockRelease,
      onBackendLockReleaseBlocked: (releaseResult) => {
        logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransitionWithAppLogger(
          releaseResult,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonClose
        );
      },
      stopReasonClose: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonClose,
      closeAllTabs: () => tabs.closeAllTabs(),
      clearLogs: () => logger.clear(),
      closeProject: () => projectManager.closeProject()
    });
  }

  const appCloseCoordinator = createAppCloseCoordinator({
    confirmSaveIfDirty,
    hasDirtyProject: () => projectManager.hasDirtyProject(),
    requestAppQuit: () => shell.requestApplicationExit(),
    guardBrowserCloseDecision: () => shell.cancelCloseIntent(),
    allowBrowserClose: () => shell.approveCloseIntent()
  });

  async function exitFlow() {
    await appCloseCoordinator.requestExit();
  }

  function resolveCurrentBackendProjectForExport() {
    return resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
      currentProject: projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null,
      backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
    });
  }

  async function exportBackendProjectArchiveFlow() {
    const projectForExport = resolveCurrentBackendProjectForExport();
    if (!projectForExport) {
      return false;
    }

    return exportBackendProject(projectForExport);
  }

  const platformActionHandlers = new Map([
    [platformActionIds.createProject, async () => newProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.openProject, async () => openProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.closeProject, async () => closeProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.saveProject, async () => saveProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.saveProjectAs, async () => saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs: true })],
    [platformActionIds.importProject, async () => importProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.exportProject, async () => exportBackendProjectArchiveFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.exit, async () => exitFlow()]
  ]);

  function resolvePlatformActionLoggerSource(source) {
    if (source === platformActionSource) {
      return platformActionLoggerSource;
    }
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.platform;
  }

  async function dispatchPlatformAction(actionId, { source = platformActionSource } = {}) {
    const loggerSource = resolvePlatformActionLoggerSource(source);
    const stateVersionBeforeDispatch = platformActionSurfaceController.getStateVersion();
    try {
      const transitionResult = await tabs.finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({
        reason: `${platformActionTransitionPrefix}${actionId}`,
        blockOnFailure: true
      });

      if (!transitionResult.continued) {
        logger.error(loggerSource, platformActionDispatchMessages.blockedByEditorContext, {
          action: actionId,
          source,
          outcome: transitionResult.outcome,
          reason: transitionResult.reason
        });
        return false;
      }

      const actionHandler = platformActionHandlers.get(actionId);
      if (!actionHandler) {
        return false;
      }

      await actionHandler();
      if (platformActionSurfaceController.getStateVersion() === stateVersionBeforeDispatch) {
        platformActionSurfaceController.updateState();
      }
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(loggerSource, platformActionDispatchMessages.executionFailed, {
        action: actionId,
        source,
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      if (platformActionSurfaceController.getStateVersion() === stateVersionBeforeDispatch) {
        platformActionSurfaceController.updateState();
      }
      return false;
    }
  }

  for (const actionId of webSurfacePlatformActionOrder) {
    const buttonNode = platformActionButtonsById.get(actionId);
    if (!buttonNode) {
      continue;
    }
    buttonNode.addEventListener('click', () => {
      void dispatchPlatformAction(actionId, { source: platformActionSource });
    });
  }

  function handleBrowserCloseIntentRequested() {
    try {
      const guardDecision = appCloseCoordinator.resolveBrowserCloseGuardDecision();
      void appCloseCoordinator.applyBrowserCloseGuardDecision(guardDecision);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.windowClose, 'Ошибка обработки запроса закрытия окна', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      void shell.cancelCloseIntent();
    }
  }

  const disposePrimaryCloseIntent = shell.subscribeToCloseIntent(() => {
    handleBrowserCloseIntentRequested();
  });

  window.addEventListener(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserClose.eventName, () => {
    disposePrimaryCloseIntent?.();
    processExecutionOrchestrator?.dispose?.();
  });

  logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.platform, 'Инициализация MetaPlatform...');
  await renderTree();
  setNextBackendCatalogFlowOpenEntryPoint(backendCatalogFlowEntryPoints.startup);
  await openProjectFlow();
});

FILE: ui/renderer/core/commandBus.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.commandBus;
const COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.commandBusMessages;

export function createCommandBus({ logger }) {
  const handlers = new Map();

  function register(commandType, handler) {
    handlers.set(commandType, handler);
  }

  async function execute(command) {
    const type = command?.type;

    if (!type) {
      throw new Error(COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.commandTypeRequired);
    }

    const handler = handlers.get(type);

    if (!handler) {
      logger.warn(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.missingHandlerPrefix}${type}`);
      return null;
    }

    logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.executionPrefix}${type}`, command?.meta || null);

    try {
      const result = await handler(command);
      logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.successPrefix}${type}`);
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.failurePrefix}${type}`, {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  return {
    register,
    execute
  };
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import Split from 'split.js';

function getSplitSharedOptions() {
  return {
    elementStyle: (dimension, size, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `calc(${size}% - ${gutterSize}px)`
    }),
    gutterStyle: (dimension, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `${gutterSize}px`
    })
  };
}

export function initWorkbenchLayout() {
  const horizontalSplit = Split([`#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectTreeColumnId}`, `#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.workbenchRightColumnId}`], {
    ...APP_CONFIG.ui.layout.split.horizontal,
    ...getSplitSharedOptions()
  });

  const verticalSplit = Split([`#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.editorHostContainerId}`, `#${APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.bottomPanelId}`], {
    ...APP_CONFIG.ui.layout.split.vertical,
    ...getSplitSharedOptions()
  });

  return {
    dispose() {
      horizontalSplit?.destroy?.();
      verticalSplit?.destroy?.();
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/core/logger.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { normalizeLogDetails } from './loggerShared.js';

const LOGGER_LEVELS = APP_CONFIG.logger.levels;
const LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES = APP_CONFIG.logger.levelNames;

function resolveConfigLevel() {
  return APP_CONFIG.platform?.logging?.level || LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.info;
}

function shouldWrite(level) {
  const targetLevel = resolveConfigLevel();
  const targetPriority = LOGGER_LEVELS[targetLevel] ?? LOGGER_LEVELS.info;
  const entryPriority = LOGGER_LEVELS[level] ?? LOGGER_LEVELS.info;
  return entryPriority >= targetPriority && targetPriority < LOGGER_LEVELS.none;
}

export function createCoreLogger({ sinks = [] } = {}) {
  function write(level, source, message, details = null) {
    if (!shouldWrite(level)) {
      return;
    }

    const ts = new Date().toLocaleTimeString(APP_CONFIG.platform.locale);
    const line = `[${ts}] [${source}] ${level.toUpperCase()} ${message}`;
    const detailsText = details != null ? normalizeLogDetails(details) : '';
    const entry = { level, source, message, line, details, detailsText, ts };

    sinks.forEach((sink) => sink?.write?.(entry));
  }

  function clear() {
    sinks.forEach((sink) => sink?.clear?.());
  }

  return {
    debug: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.debug, source, message, details),
    info: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.info, source, message, details),
    warn: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.warn, source, message, details),
    error: (source, message, details = null) => write(LOGGER_LEVEL_NAMES.error, source, message, details),
    clear
  };
}

export { shouldWrite };


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/core/loggerShared.js

import { LOGGER_CONFIG } from '../../config/logger-config.js';

const LOGGER_PRETTY_PRINT_INDENT = LOGGER_CONFIG.format.prettyPrintIndent;

export function normalizeLogDetails(details) {
  if (details == null) {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof details === 'string') {
    return details;
  }

  try {
    return JSON.stringify(details, null, LOGGER_PRETTY_PRINT_INDENT);
  } catch {
    return String(details);
  }
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/core/loggerSinks.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const LOG_ENTRY_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logEntry;
const LOG_LINE_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logLine;
const LOG_DETAILS_CLASS = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.logDetails;
const CONSOLE_METHODS_BY_LEVEL = APP_CONFIG.logger.console.methodsByLevel;
const DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD = APP_CONFIG.logger.console.defaultMethod;

export function createDomLogSink({ output }) {
  return {
    write(entry) {
      if (!output) {
        return;
      }

      const node = document.createElement('div');
      node.className = LOG_ENTRY_CLASS;

      const lineNode = document.createElement('div');
      lineNode.className = LOG_LINE_CLASS;
      lineNode.textContent = entry.line;
      node.appendChild(lineNode);

      if (entry.detailsText) {
        const detailsNode = document.createElement('pre');
        detailsNode.className = LOG_DETAILS_CLASS;
        detailsNode.textContent = entry.detailsText;
        node.appendChild(detailsNode);
      }

      output.appendChild(node);
      output.scrollTo({ top: output.scrollHeight });
    },
    clear() {
      if (output) {
        output.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }
  };
}

export function createConsoleLogSink({ mirrorToConsole = APP_CONFIG.platform?.logging?.mirrorToConsole } = {}) {
  return {
    write(entry) {
      if (!mirrorToConsole) {
        return;
      }

      const methodName = CONSOLE_METHODS_BY_LEVEL[entry.level] || DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD;
      const method = console[methodName]?.bind(console) ?? console[DEFAULT_CONSOLE_METHOD].bind(console);
      method(entry.line);

      if (entry.detailsText) {
        method(entry.detailsText);
      }
    },
    clear() {}
  };
}

export function createMemoryLogSink() {
  const entries = [];

  return {
    write(entry) {
      entries.push(entry);
    },
    clear() {
      entries.length = 0;
    },
    getEntries() {
      return [...entries];
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/core/moduleRegistry.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const MODULE_REGISTRY_LOG_SOURCE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.moduleRegistry;

export function createModuleRegistry({ logger }) {
  const modulesById = new Map();
  const documentKindToModuleId = new Map();

  function registerModule(module) {
    if (!module?.id) {
      throw new Error('Module id is required');
    }

    modulesById.set(module.id, module);

    for (const kind of module.documentKinds || []) {
      documentKindToModuleId.set(kind, module.id);
    }

    logger.info(MODULE_REGISTRY_LOG_SOURCE, 'Модуль зарегистрирован', {
      id: module.id,
      name: module.name,
      documentKinds: module.documentKinds || []
    });
  }

  function getModule(moduleId) {
    return modulesById.get(moduleId) || null;
  }

  function getAllModules() {
    return [...modulesById.values()];
  }

  function findModuleByDocumentKind(kind) {
    const moduleId = documentKindToModuleId.get(kind);
    return moduleId ? getModule(moduleId) : null;
  }

  return {
    registerModule,
    getModule,
    getAllModules,
    findModuleByDocumentKind
  };
}
