import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { createDocumentLoader } from '../runtime/documentLoader.js';
import {
  createDocumentGuid,
  getDocumentName,
  normalizeDocumentName,
  setDocumentName,
  isUnsavedDocumentPath,
  ensureDocumentId,
  getDocumentIdentityKey,
  getMetaGenNameSurfaceStatus
} from '../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';
import { areDocumentSnapshotsSemanticallyEqual } from '../runtime/documentSnapshot.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';
const PROJECT_MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds;
const PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS = (APP_CONFIG.project.primaryModuleIds || [])
  .filter((moduleId) => Boolean(PROJECT_MODULE_IDS[moduleId]));
const PROJECT_MODULE_FOLDERS = PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS.reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
  acc[moduleId] = APP_CONFIG.project.fileTransport.moduleFolders[moduleId];
  return acc;
}, {});
const PROJECT_FILE_TRANSPORT = APP_CONFIG.project.fileTransport;
const DEFAULT_PROJECT_YAML_EXTENSION = PROJECT_FILE_TRANSPORT.defaultYamlExtension;
const PROJECT_SOURCES = APP_CONFIG.project.sources;
const BACKEND_SOURCE_ID = PROJECT_SOURCES.backend;
const BACKEND_DOCUMENT_PATH_PREFIX = `${BACKEND_SOURCE_ID}://`;

function createPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets() {
  return PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS.reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
    acc[moduleId] = [];
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

function flattenPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets(documentsByModule = {}) {
  return PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS.flatMap((moduleId) => documentsByModule[moduleId] || []);
}

function getProjectModuleDisplayNames() {
  return PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS
    .map((moduleId) => APP_CONFIG.project.moduleDisplayNames[moduleId])
    .filter(Boolean);
}

function cloneDocumentPayload(document) {
  if (typeof structuredClone === 'function') {
    return structuredClone(document);
  }

  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(document));
}

function splitPathSegments(targetPath) {
  return String(targetPath || '').replace(/\\/g, '/').split('/').filter(Boolean);
}

function getPathBaseName(targetPath) {
  const segments = splitPathSegments(targetPath);
  return segments.length ? segments[segments.length - 1] : '';
}

function buildBackendDocumentPath(projectId, moduleId, fileName) {
  return `${BACKEND_DOCUMENT_PATH_PREFIX}${projectId}/${moduleId}/${fileName}`;
}


function createDefaultProjectRaw() {
  // File-transport metadata for YAML ZIP import/export and compatibility tooling.
  // Backend project identity/lifecycle is represented by backendProject + source.
  return {
    kind: APP_CONFIG.project.projectKinds.root,
    version: APP_CONFIG.project.schemaVersion,
    project: {
      id: createDocumentGuid(),
      name: APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName,
      description: ''
    },
    modules: getProjectModuleDisplayNames(),
    paths: {
      ...PROJECT_MODULE_FOLDERS,
      generated: PROJECT_FILE_TRANSPORT.generatedFolderName
    }
  };
}

export function createProjectManager({ logger, runtimeShell, moduleRegistry, onProjectLoaded, onProjectClosed }) {
  const documentLoader = createDocumentLoader({ fileSystem: runtimeShell });
  let currentProject = null;
  const listeners = new Set();
  let unsavedCounter = 0;

  function emitChange() {
    for (const listener of listeners) {
      listener(currentProject);
    }
  }

  function subscribe(listener) {
    listeners.add(listener);
    return () => listeners.delete(listener);
  }

  function setDirty(value = true) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return;
    }

    // Dirty-state относится к runtime state проекта в целом.
    // Только успешный full project save (commitBackendSave/commitBackendSaveAs) переводит проект в clean state.
    currentProject.isDirty = Boolean(value);
    emitChange();
  }

  function clearDirty() {
    setDirty(false);
  }

  function getAllDocuments() {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return [];
    }

    return flattenPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets(currentProject.documents);
  }

  function createProjectRuntime({
    raw,
    documents,
    isUnsaved = false,
    isDirty = false,
    source = BACKEND_SOURCE_ID,
    backendProject = null
  }) {
    for (const moduleId of Object.keys(documents || {})) {
      for (const record of documents[moduleId] || []) {
        ensureDocumentId(record);
      }
    }

    return {
      source,
      backendProject,
      raw,
      project: raw.project,
      documents,
      isUnsaved,
      isDirty
    };
  }

  function hydrateSnapshotDocuments(snapshotDocuments = {}) {
    const buckets = createPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets();

    for (const moduleId of PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS) {
      const entries = Array.isArray(snapshotDocuments[moduleId]) ? snapshotDocuments[moduleId] : [];
      const records = [];

      for (const entry of entries) {
        if (!entry || typeof entry !== 'object' || !entry.document || typeof entry.document !== 'object') {
          continue;
        }

        const path = String(entry.path || '').trim()
          || `${APP_CONFIG.project.unsavedDocumentPathPrefix}${moduleId}/${++unsavedCounter}${DEFAULT_PROJECT_YAML_EXTENSION}`;
        const record = {
          moduleId,
          path: String(path).replace(/\\/g, '/'),
          document: cloneDocumentPayload(entry.document)
        };
        ensureDocumentId(record);
        records.push(record);
      }

      records.sort((a, b) => getDocumentName(a).localeCompare(getDocumentName(b)));
      buckets[moduleId] = records;
    }

    return buckets;
  }

  function hydrateSnapshotRaw(snapshot) {
    const fallbackProject = snapshot?.project || {};
    const hasCatalogComment = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(fallbackProject, 'comment');
    const catalogComment = String(fallbackProject?.comment || '').trim();
    const snapshotDescription = String(snapshot?.raw?.project?.description || '');
    const raw = cloneDocumentPayload(
      snapshot?.raw && typeof snapshot.raw === 'object'
        ? snapshot.raw
        : createDefaultProjectRaw()
    );

    raw.project = {
      ...(raw.project || {}),
      id: String(raw?.project?.id || fallbackProject.projectId || createDocumentGuid()),
      name: String(raw?.project?.name || fallbackProject.name || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName),
      // Catalog metadata comment is canonical for opened backend projects.
      // Keep legacy raw.project.description only when snapshot.project.comment is absent.
      description: hasCatalogComment ? catalogComment : snapshotDescription
    };

    return raw;
  }

  async function openProjectSnapshot(snapshot, options = {}) {
    const raw = hydrateSnapshotRaw(snapshot);
    const lockToken = String(options?.lockToken || '').trim();
    currentProject = createProjectRuntime({
      raw,
      documents: hydrateSnapshotDocuments(snapshot?.documents || {}),
      source: BACKEND_SOURCE_ID,
      backendProject: {
        ...(snapshot?.project || {}),
        lockToken
      },
      // Snapshot is already bound to backend catalog entity and backend command flow.
      isUnsaved: false,
      isDirty: false
    });

    onProjectLoaded?.({ projectRuntime: currentProject });
    emitChange();
    return currentProject;
  }

  async function closeProject() {
    currentProject = null;
    emitChange();
    onProjectClosed?.();
  }

  function getDocumentsByModule(moduleId) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return [];
    }

    return currentProject.documents[moduleId] || [];
  }

  function getDocumentByPath(targetPath) {
    return getAllDocuments().find((entry) => entry.path === targetPath) || null;
  }

  function getDocumentById(targetId) {
    const normalizedId = String(targetId || '').trim();

    if (!normalizedId) {
      return null;
    }

    return getAllDocuments().find((entry) => ensureDocumentId(entry) === normalizedId) || null;
  }



  function resolveDocumentRecord(targetIdentity) {
    if (!targetIdentity) {
      return null;
    }

    if (typeof targetIdentity === 'object') {
      const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(targetIdentity);

      if (identityKey) {
        return getAllDocuments().find((entry) => getDocumentIdentityKey(entry) === identityKey) || null;
      }

      return null;
    }

    const normalizedIdentity = String(targetIdentity).trim();

    if (!normalizedIdentity) {
      return null;
    }

    const recordByIdentityKey = getAllDocuments().find((entry) => getDocumentIdentityKey(entry) === normalizedIdentity);

    if (recordByIdentityKey) {
      return recordByIdentityKey;
    }

    const recordById = getDocumentById(normalizedIdentity);

    if (recordById) {
      return recordById;
    }

    return null;
  }

  function replaceDocumentRecord(nextRecord) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return null;
    }

    if (!nextRecord?.moduleId || !nextRecord?.path || !nextRecord?.document) {
      return null;
    }

    const moduleDocuments = currentProject.documents[nextRecord.moduleId];

    if (!Array.isArray(moduleDocuments)) {
      return null;
    }

    const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(nextRecord);
    const index = moduleDocuments.findIndex((entry) => getDocumentIdentityKey(entry) === identityKey);

    if (index < 0) {
      return null;
    }

    const previousRecord = moduleDocuments[index];
    moduleDocuments[index] = nextRecord;
    moduleDocuments.sort((a, b) => getDocumentName(a).localeCompare(getDocumentName(b)));

    if (!areDocumentSnapshotsSemanticallyEqual(previousRecord, nextRecord) || previousRecord?.path !== nextRecord?.path) {
      setDirty(true);
    }

    return moduleDocuments.find((entry) => getDocumentIdentityKey(entry) === identityKey) || null;
  }

  function isDocumentNameTaken(moduleId, name, excludeIdentity = null) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return false;
    }

    const normalizedTarget = normalizeDocumentName(name);

    if (!normalizedTarget) {
      return false;
    }

    return getDocumentsByModule(moduleId).some((record) => {
      if (excludeIdentity && getDocumentIdentityKey(record) === excludeIdentity) {
        return false;
      }

      return getDocumentName(record) === normalizedTarget;
    });
  }

  function isMetaGenNameTaken(name, excludeIdentity = null) {
    return isDocumentNameTaken(APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen, name, excludeIdentity);
  }

  function setDocumentNameWithModuleSemantics(record, resolvedName) {
    if (record?.moduleId !== APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen) {
      setDocumentName(record, resolvedName);
      return true;
    }

    const nameSurfaceStatus = getMetaGenNameSurfaceStatus(record);
    if (nameSurfaceStatus !== 'canonical-component') {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project,
        'MetaGen rename rejected: canonical component.name requires valid document.component on metagen.component documents',
        {
          moduleId: record?.moduleId || '',
          path: record?.path || '',
          reason: nameSurfaceStatus
        }
      );
      return false;
    }

    record.document.component.name = resolvedName;
    return true;
  }

  function getNextMetaGenDefaultName() {
    let index = 1;

    while (true) {
      const candidate = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName} ${index}`;

      if (!isMetaGenNameTaken(candidate)) {
        return candidate;
      }

      index += 1;
    }
  }

  async function createDocument(moduleId, name = null) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      throw new Error('Project is not opened');
    }

    const module = moduleRegistry.getModule(moduleId);

    if (!module) {
      throw new Error(`Module not found: ${moduleId}`);
    }

    const fallbackName = moduleId === APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen
      ? getNextMetaGenDefaultName()
      : APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;
    const resolvedName = normalizeDocumentName(name || fallbackName);

    if (!resolvedName) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Пустое имя документа отклонено', { moduleId });
      return null;
    }

    if (isDocumentNameTaken(moduleId, resolvedName)) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Имя документа уже занято', { moduleId, name: resolvedName });
      return null;
    }

    const document = module.createDefaultDocument({ name: resolvedName });
    const virtualPath = `${APP_CONFIG.project.unsavedDocumentPathPrefix}${moduleId}/${++unsavedCounter}${DEFAULT_PROJECT_YAML_EXTENSION}`;

    const record = { moduleId, path: virtualPath, document };
    ensureDocumentId(record);
    currentProject.documents[moduleId].push(record);
    currentProject.documents[moduleId].sort((a, b) => getDocumentName(a).localeCompare(getDocumentName(b)));

    setDirty(true);
    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Создан документ', { moduleId, path: virtualPath, name: resolvedName });
    return record;
  }

  async function renameDocument(targetIdentity, nextName) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return null;
    }

    const record = resolveDocumentRecord(targetIdentity);

    if (!record) {
      return null;
    }

    const resolvedName = normalizeDocumentName(nextName);

    if (!resolvedName) {
      return null;
    }

    if (isDocumentNameTaken(record.moduleId, resolvedName, getDocumentIdentityKey(record))) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Имя документа уже занято', { moduleId: record.moduleId, name: resolvedName });
      return null;
    }

    const previousPath = record.path;
    // Backend catalog is canonical; path remains display/transport-only metadata.
    if (!setDocumentNameWithModuleSemantics(record, resolvedName)) {
      return null;
    }

    currentProject.documents[record.moduleId].sort((a, b) => getDocumentName(a).localeCompare(getDocumentName(b)));
    setDirty(true);

    return {
      record,
      previousPath,
      nextPath: record.path
    };
  }

  function markDocumentDirty(_targetIdentity = null) {
    setDirty(true);
  }

  // INTERNAL: marks a document record as changed for compatibility adapters.
  // Does not represent project-level save lifecycle and does not clear project dirty-state.
  // Clean state is restored only by commitBackendSave()/commitBackendSaveAs().
  async function touchDocumentRecord(documentRecord) {
    if (!documentRecord?.path || !documentRecord?.document) {
      throw new Error('Invalid document record');
    }

    const normalizedPath = String(documentRecord.path || '').trim();
    const isBackendRuntimeProject = currentProject?.source === BACKEND_SOURCE_ID;
    const isBackendTransportPath = normalizedPath.startsWith(BACKEND_DOCUMENT_PATH_PREFIX);

    if (isUnsavedDocumentPath(normalizedPath) || isBackendRuntimeProject || isBackendTransportPath) {
      setDirty(true);
      return true;
    }

    await documentLoader.saveYaml(normalizedPath, documentRecord.document);
    setDirty(true);
    return true;
  }

  async function deleteDocument(targetIdentity) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      return false;
    }

    const record = resolveDocumentRecord(targetIdentity);

    if (!record) {
      return false;
    }

    const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(record);
    currentProject.documents[record.moduleId] = currentProject.documents[record.moduleId].filter((entry) => getDocumentIdentityKey(entry) !== identityKey);

    setDirty(true);
    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, 'Документ удалён', { identityKey, path: record.path });
    return true;
  }

  function collectCurrentDocumentRecords(openDocuments = []) {
    const recordsByIdentity = new Map();

    for (const record of getAllDocuments()) {
      const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(record);

      if (!identityKey) {
        continue;
      }

      recordsByIdentity.set(identityKey, record);
    }

    for (const record of openDocuments) {
      if (!record?.document) {
        continue;
      }

      const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(record);

      if (!identityKey || !recordsByIdentity.has(identityKey)) {
        continue;
      }

      recordsByIdentity.set(identityKey, record);
    }

    return Array.from(recordsByIdentity.values());
  }

  function exportProjectSnapshot(openDocuments = []) {
    if (!currentProject) {
      throw new Error('Project is not opened');
    }

    const documents = createPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets();
    const records = collectCurrentDocumentRecords(openDocuments);

    for (const record of records) {
      if (!record?.moduleId || !record?.document || !PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS.includes(record.moduleId)) {
        continue;
      }

      documents[record.moduleId].push({
        moduleId: record.moduleId,
        path: String(record.path || ''),
        document: cloneDocumentPayload(record.document)
      });
    }

    for (const moduleId of PRIMARY_MODULE_IDS) {
      documents[moduleId].sort((a, b) => getDocumentName(a).localeCompare(getDocumentName(b)));
    }

    return {
      source: currentProject.source,
      project: currentProject.backendProject ? cloneDocumentPayload(currentProject.backendProject) : null,
      raw: cloneDocumentPayload(currentProject.raw),
      documents
    };
  }

  function commitBackendSave(projectMeta = null) {
    if (!currentProject || currentProject.source !== BACKEND_SOURCE_ID) {
      return false;
    }

    if (projectMeta && typeof projectMeta === 'object') {
      currentProject.backendProject = {
        ...(currentProject.backendProject || {}),
        ...projectMeta
      };
    }

    currentProject.isUnsaved = false;
    clearDirty();
    return true;
  }

  function commitBackendSaveAs(projectMeta = null) {
    if (!currentProject || currentProject.source !== BACKEND_SOURCE_ID) {
      return false;
    }

    const explicitProjectMeta = projectMeta && typeof projectMeta === 'object'
      ? projectMeta
      : null;
    const nextMeta = explicitProjectMeta
      ? {
          ...(currentProject.backendProject || {}),
          ...explicitProjectMeta
        }
      : (currentProject.backendProject || {});

    const nextProjectId = String(
      nextMeta.projectId
      || currentProject.backendProject?.projectId
      || currentProject.raw?.project?.id
      || ''
    ).trim();
    const nextProjectName = String(
      nextMeta.name
      || currentProject.raw?.project?.name
      || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName
    ).trim() || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName;
    const hasExplicitComment = Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(nextMeta, 'comment');
    const nextProjectComment = String(
      hasExplicitComment
        ? nextMeta.comment
        : (currentProject.raw?.project?.description || '')
    ).trim();

    if (nextProjectId) {
      for (const record of getAllDocuments()) {
        const fallbackFileName = `${record.moduleId}${DEFAULT_PROJECT_YAML_EXTENSION}`;
        const fileName = getPathBaseName(record.path) || fallbackFileName;
        record.path = buildBackendDocumentPath(nextProjectId, record.moduleId, fileName);
      }
    }

    const resolvedLockToken = String(
      explicitProjectMeta?.lockToken
      ?? currentProject.backendProject?.lockToken
      ?? ''
    ).trim();
    currentProject.backendProject = {
      ...nextMeta,
      lockToken: resolvedLockToken,
      ...(nextProjectId ? { projectId: nextProjectId } : {}),
      name: nextProjectName,
      comment: nextProjectComment
    };
    currentProject.raw.project = {
      ...(currentProject.raw.project || {}),
      id: nextProjectId || currentProject.raw?.project?.id,
      name: nextProjectName,
      description: nextProjectComment
    };
    currentProject.project = currentProject.raw.project;
    currentProject.isUnsaved = false;
    clearDirty();
    return true;
  }

  function setBackendProjectLockToken(lockToken = '') {
    if (!currentProject || currentProject.source !== BACKEND_SOURCE_ID) {
      return false;
    }

    const normalizedLockToken = String(lockToken || '').trim();
    const previousLockToken = String(currentProject.backendProject?.lockToken || '').trim();
    if (previousLockToken === normalizedLockToken) {
      return true;
    }

    currentProject.backendProject = {
      ...(currentProject.backendProject || {}),
      lockToken: normalizedLockToken
    };
    emitChange();
    return true;
  }

  return {
    openProjectSnapshot,
    exportProjectSnapshot,
    commitBackendSave,
    commitBackendSaveAs,
    setBackendProjectLockToken,
    closeProject,
    subscribe,
    getCurrentProject: () => currentProject,
    getMetaGenDocuments: () => currentProject?.documents?.[APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen] || [],
    getDocumentsByModule,
    getDocumentByPath,
    getDocumentById,
    resolveDocumentRecord,
    replaceDocumentRecord,
    createDocument,
    renameDocument,
    getNextMetaGenDefaultName,
    isMetaGenNameTaken,
    touchDocumentRecord,
    deleteDocument,
    markDocumentDirty,
    hasDirtyProject: () => Boolean(currentProject?.isDirty),
    clearDirty
  };
}

function createElement(tagName, classNames = []) {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);
  classNames.forEach((className) => node.classList.add(className));
  return node;
}

function buildLocale() {
  const locale = mergeLocales(UniverPresetSheetsCoreRuRU, UniverPresetSheetsDataValidationRuRU);
  const labels = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.contextMenuLabels;

  if (locale.rightClick) {
    locale.rightClick.copy = labels.copy;
    locale.rightClick.cut = labels.cut;
    locale.rightClick.paste = labels.paste;
    locale.rightClick.insertRowBefore = labels.insertRowBefore;
    locale.rightClick.insertColumnBefore = labels.insertColumnBefore;
  }

  return locale;
}

function createPanel({ headerText, panelClassName, contentNode }) {
  const panelNode = createElement('div', [panelClassName]);
  const headerNode = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader]);
  const contentWrapperNode = createElement('div', ['metagen-editor-panel-content']);

  headerNode.textContent = headerText;
  contentWrapperNode.appendChild(contentNode);
  panelNode.appendChild(headerNode);
  panelNode.appendChild(contentWrapperNode);

  return panelNode;
}

function createSplitOptions(layoutConfig) {
  return {
    direction: layoutConfig.direction,
    sizes: layoutConfig.sizes,
    minSize: layoutConfig.minSize,
    gutterSize: layoutConfig.gutterSize,
    cursor: layoutConfig.cursor,
    elementStyle: (dimension, size, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `calc(${size}% - ${gutterSize}px)`
    }),
    gutterStyle: (dimension, gutterSize) => ({
      'flex-basis': `${gutterSize}px`
    })
  };
}

function buildEditor(documentRecord) {
  const root = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorRoot]);
  const grid = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorGrid]);
  const rightArea = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorRightStack]);
  const centerStack = createElement('div', [METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.classNames.centerStack]);

  const paramsContainer = createElement('div', ['metagen-editor-table-container']);
  const codeTextarea = createElement('textarea', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorTextarea]);
  const dataContainer = createElement('div', ['metagen-editor-table-container']);
  const instancesContainer = createElement('div', ['metagen-editor-table-container']);

  const uid = String(documentRecord.path || documentRecord.document?.component?.id || 'metagen').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, '_');
  const containerIdPrefixes = METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.containerIdPrefixes;

  paramsContainer.id = `${containerIdPrefixes.params}${uid}`;
  dataContainer.id = `${containerIdPrefixes.data}${uid}`;
  instancesContainer.id = `${containerIdPrefixes.instances}${uid}`;

  const paramsPanel = createPanel({
    headerText: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.params,
    panelClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanel,
    contentNode: paramsContainer
  });

  const codePanel = createPanel({
    headerText: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.code,
    panelClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanel,
    contentNode: codeTextarea
  });

  const dataPanel = createPanel({
    headerText: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.data,
    panelClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanel,
    contentNode: dataContainer
  });

  const instancesPanel = createPanel({
    headerText: METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.instances,
    panelClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanel,
    contentNode: instancesContainer
  });

  centerStack.appendChild(dataPanel);
  centerStack.appendChild(codePanel);
  rightArea.appendChild(centerStack);
  rightArea.appendChild(instancesPanel);

  grid.appendChild(paramsPanel);
  grid.appendChild(rightArea);
  root.appendChild(grid);

  return {
    root,
    grid,
    rightArea,
    centerStack,
    paramsPanel,
    codePanel,
    dataPanel,
    instancesPanel,
    paramsContainer,
    dataContainer,
    instancesContainer,
    codeTextarea
  };
}

function bindSaveShortcut(textarea, trySave) {
  textarea.addEventListener('keydown', async (event) => {
    if (event.ctrlKey && event.key.toLowerCase() === METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.saveShortcutKey) {
      event.preventDefault();
      await trySave();
    }
  });
}

function safeSerialize(value) {
  try {
    return JSON.stringify(value);
  } catch {
    return '';
  }
}

function cloneDocumentSnapshot(documentRecord, nextDocument) {
  return {
    ...documentRecord,
    document: nextDocument
  };
}

const METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI = APP_CONFIG.ui.validation.metaGen;
const METAGEN_GENERATION_BLOCKED_REASON_PREFIX = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processGenerateBlockedByValidationPrefix;
const METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_SCOPE_BY_SECTION = Object.freeze({
  [METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.root]: METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.scopes.root,
  [METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.params]: METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.scopes.params,
  [METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.data]: METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.scopes.data,
  [METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.instances]: METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.scopes.instances,
  [METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.code]: METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.scopes.code
});

function normalizeComparableParamsRow(rowValues) {
  if (!Array.isArray(rowValues)) {
    return [];
  }

  const normalized = rowValues.map((value) => {
    if (value == null) {
      return '';
    }

    if (typeof value === 'object') {
      if ('v' in value) {
        return normalizeComparableParamsRow([value.v])[0];
      }

      return '';
    }

    return String(value);
  });

  while (normalized.length > 0 && normalized[normalized.length - 1] === '') {
    normalized.pop();
  }

  return normalized;
}

function areParamsRowsEqual(leftRow, rightRow) {
  const left = normalizeComparableParamsRow(leftRow);
  const right = normalizeComparableParamsRow(rightRow);

  if (left.length !== right.length) {
    return false;
  }

  for (let index = 0; index < left.length; index += 1) {
    if (left[index] !== right[index]) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  return true;
}

function getParamsReplayRefreshBounds(currentSnapshot, nextSnapshot) {
  const currentRows = [currentSnapshot?.header || [], ...(currentSnapshot?.rows || [])];
  const nextRows = [nextSnapshot?.header || [], ...(nextSnapshot?.rows || [])];
  const maxLength = Math.max(currentRows.length, nextRows.length);
  let startRow = -1;
  let endRow = -1;

  for (let rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < maxLength; rowIndex += 1) {
    if (!areParamsRowsEqual(currentRows[rowIndex], nextRows[rowIndex])) {
      startRow = rowIndex;
      break;
    }
  }

  if (startRow < 0) {
    return null;
  }

  for (let rowIndex = maxLength - 1; rowIndex >= 0; rowIndex -= 1) {
    if (!areParamsRowsEqual(currentRows[rowIndex], nextRows[rowIndex])) {
      endRow = rowIndex;
      break;
    }
  }

  return {
    startRow,
    endRow: Math.max(startRow, endRow)
  };
}

function bindTableDirtyTracker(tableRuntime, extractDocumentValue, markDirty, onAfterDirty = null) {
  if (typeof tableRuntime?.workbook?.onCommandExecuted !== 'function') {
    return null;
  }

  let previousSnapshot = safeSerialize(extractDocumentValue());

  return tableRuntime.workbook.onCommandExecuted(() => {
    const nextSnapshot = safeSerialize(extractDocumentValue());

    if (nextSnapshot !== previousSnapshot) {
      previousSnapshot = nextSnapshot;
      markDirty();
      onAfterDirty?.();
    }
  });
}

function buildWorkbookRuntimeNames(runtimeNamePartConfig, componentId, suffix = '') {
  return {
    workbookId: `${runtimeNamePartConfig.workbookIdPrefix}${componentId}${suffix}`,
    sheetId: `${runtimeNamePartConfig.sheetIdPrefix}${componentId}${suffix}`,
    sheetName: `${runtimeNamePartConfig.sheetNamePrefix}${componentId}${suffix}`
  };
}

function setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(targetNode, section) {
  if (!targetNode || typeof targetNode.setAttribute !== 'function') {
    return;
  }

  const scope = METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_SCOPE_BY_SECTION[section];
  if (!scope) {
    return;
  }

  targetNode.setAttribute(METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.attributes.scope, scope);
}

function setValidationFeedbackTargetState(targetNode, errors = [], options) {
  if (!targetNode) {
    return;
  }

  const normalizedErrors = Array.isArray(errors) ? errors.filter(Boolean) : [];
  const hasErrors = normalizedErrors.length > 0;
  const state = hasErrors
    ? METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.states.invalid
    : METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.states.valid;
  const ariaInvalid = hasErrors
    ? METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.ariaInvalid.invalid
    : METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.ariaInvalid.valid;

  targetNode.classList?.toggle?.(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.metagenValidationInvalid, hasErrors);
  targetNode.setAttribute?.(METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.attributes.state, state);
  targetNode.setAttribute?.(METAGEN_EDITOR_VALIDATION_UI.attributes.ariaInvalid, ariaInvalid);
  const resolvedOptions = options && typeof options === 'object' ? options : {};
  const tooltipText = typeof resolvedOptions.tooltipText === 'string'
    ? resolvedOptions.tooltipText.trim()
    : '';
  targetNode.title = hasErrors
    ? (tooltipText || normalizedErrors.join('\n'))
    : '';
}

export async function createMetaGenEditor({ documentRecord, mountElement, logger, onSave, onDirty }) {
  clearMountElement(mountElement);

  const locale = buildLocale();
  const tableConfig = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime;
  const sectionDefaults = createMetaGenDocumentSectionDefaults();
  const normalizedInitialDocument = normalizeMetaGenDocumentForPersistence(
    documentRecord.document || sectionDefaults,
    tableConfig.tables
  );
  const logMessages = tableConfig.logMessages;
  const loggerSources = tableConfig.loggerSources;
  const loggerSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.editor}`;
  const lifecycleSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.lifecycle}`;
  const paramsSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.tables.params}`;
  const dataSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.tables.data}`;
  const instancesSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.tables.instances}`;
  const autoStyleSource = `${METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId}.${loggerSources.paramsAutoStyle}`;

  const {
    root,
    grid,
    rightArea,
    centerStack,
    paramsPanel,
    codePanel,
    dataPanel,
    instancesPanel,
    paramsContainer,
    dataContainer,
    instancesContainer,
    codeTextarea
  } = buildEditor(documentRecord);
  const paramsHeaderNode = paramsPanel.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`);
  const dataHeaderNode = dataPanel.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`);
  const instancesHeaderNode = instancesPanel.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`);
  const codeHeaderNode = codePanel.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(root, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.root);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(paramsHeaderNode, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.params);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(dataHeaderNode, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.data);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(instancesHeaderNode, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.instances);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(codeHeaderNode, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.code);
  setValidationFeedbackTargetScope(codeTextarea, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.code);

  codeTextarea.value = normalizedInitialDocument.code.text;

  mountElement.appendChild(root);

  const outerSplit = Split(
    [paramsPanel, rightArea],
    createSplitOptions(METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.layout.outerSplit)
  );
  const centerSplit = Split(
    [dataPanel, codePanel],
    createSplitOptions(METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.layout.innerSplit)
  );
  const rightAreaSplit = Split(
    [centerStack, instancesPanel],
    createSplitOptions(METAGEN_CONFIG.editor.layout.rightAreaSplit)
  );

  const documentComponentId = String(documentRecord.document?.component?.id || 'component');
  const runtimeNameParts = tableConfig.workbooks.runtimeNameParts;
  const runtimeSuffixes = tableConfig.workbooks.runtimeSuffixes;
  const paramsRuntimeNames = buildWorkbookRuntimeNames(runtimeNameParts.params, documentComponentId, runtimeSuffixes.params);
  const dataRuntimeNames = buildWorkbookRuntimeNames(runtimeNameParts.data, documentComponentId, runtimeSuffixes.data);
  const instancesRuntimeNames = buildWorkbookRuntimeNames(runtimeNameParts.instances, documentComponentId, runtimeSuffixes.instances);

  const paramsTable = createMetaGenParamsSheet({
    container: paramsContainer.id,
    locale,
    logger,
    source: paramsSource,
    autoStyleSource,
    workbookId: paramsRuntimeNames.workbookId,
    workbookName: tableConfig.workbooks.displayNames.params,
    sheetId: paramsRuntimeNames.sheetId,
    sheetName: paramsRuntimeNames.sheetName,
    tableConfig: tableConfig.tables.params,
    hiddenMenuCommands: tableConfig.hiddenTableMenuCommands.params,
    logMessages,
    paramsDocument: normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(normalizedInitialDocument.params)
  });

  const dataTable = await createMetaGenDataSheet({
    container: dataContainer.id,
    locale,
    logger,
    source: dataSource,
    workbookId: dataRuntimeNames.workbookId,
    workbookName: tableConfig.workbooks.displayNames.data,
    sheetId: dataRuntimeNames.sheetId,
    sheetName: dataRuntimeNames.sheetName,
    tableConfig: tableConfig.tables.data,
    hiddenMenuCommands: tableConfig.hiddenTableMenuCommands.data,
    logMessages,
    dataValidationPreset: UniverSheetsDataValidationPreset,
    dataDocument: normalizedInitialDocument.data
  });

  const instancesTable = await createMetaGenInstancesSheet({
    container: instancesContainer.id,
    locale,
    logger,
    source: instancesSource,
    workbookId: instancesRuntimeNames.workbookId,
    workbookName: tableConfig.workbooks.displayNames.instances,
    sheetId: instancesRuntimeNames.sheetId,
    sheetName: instancesRuntimeNames.sheetName,
    tableConfig: tableConfig.tables.instances,
    hiddenMenuCommands: tableConfig.hiddenTableMenuCommands.instances,
    logMessages,
    instancesDocument: normalizedInitialDocument.instances
  });

  function buildDraftDocumentFromEditorState() {
    const draftDocument = {
      ...documentRecord.document,
      params: normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsTable?.extractDocumentValue?.() || sectionDefaults.params),
      data: dataTable?.extractDocumentValue?.() || sectionDefaults.data,
      instances: normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(
        instancesTable?.extractDocumentValue?.() || sectionDefaults.instances,
        tableConfig.tables.instances
      ),
      code: {
        ...(documentRecord.document?.code || sectionDefaults.code),
        text: codeTextarea.value
      }
    };

    return normalizeMetaGenDocumentForPersistence(draftDocument, tableConfig.tables);
  }

  function applyEditorValidationFeedback(validation) {
    const paramsErrors = validation?.errorsBySection?.[METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.params] || [];
    const dataErrors = validation?.errorsBySection?.[METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.data] || [];
    const instancesErrors = validation?.errorsBySection?.[METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.instances] || [];
    const codeErrors = validation?.errorsBySection?.[METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.code] || [];
    const allErrors = Array.isArray(validation?.errors) ? validation.errors : [];
    const guidance = resolveMetaGenValidationGuidance(validation);
    const paramsGuidance = resolveMetaGenValidationGuidanceForSection(validation, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.params);
    const dataGuidance = resolveMetaGenValidationGuidanceForSection(validation, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.data);
    const instancesGuidance = resolveMetaGenValidationGuidanceForSection(validation, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.instances);
    const codeGuidance = resolveMetaGenValidationGuidanceForSection(validation, METAGEN_VALIDATION_SECTIONS.code);

    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(paramsHeaderNode, paramsErrors, { tooltipText: paramsGuidance.message });
    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(dataHeaderNode, dataErrors, { tooltipText: dataGuidance.message });
    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(instancesHeaderNode, instancesErrors, { tooltipText: instancesGuidance.message });
    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(codeHeaderNode, codeErrors, { tooltipText: codeGuidance.message });
    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(codeTextarea, codeErrors, { tooltipText: codeGuidance.message });
    setValidationFeedbackTargetState(root, allErrors, { tooltipText: guidance.message });
  }

  const generationReadinessListeners = new Set();
  let generationReadinessState = {
    isReady: true,
    status: METAGEN_GENERATION_READINESS_STATUSES.ready,
    reason: '',
    validation: null
  };

  function emitGenerationReadiness(readiness) {
    generationReadinessState = readiness && typeof readiness === 'object'
      ? readiness
      : {
        isReady: true,
        status: METAGEN_GENERATION_READINESS_STATUSES.ready,
        reason: '',
        validation: null
      };

    for (const listener of generationReadinessListeners) {
      listener(generationReadinessState);
    }
  }

  function updateGenerationReadinessFromValidation(validation) {
    emitGenerationReadiness(resolveMetaGenGenerationReadinessFromValidation(validation, {
      invalidReasonPrefix: METAGEN_GENERATION_BLOCKED_REASON_PREFIX
    }));
  }

  function validateEditorDraft() {
    const validation = validateMetaGenDocumentDetailed(buildDraftDocumentFromEditorState());
    applyEditorValidationFeedback(validation);
    updateGenerationReadinessFromValidation(validation);
    return validation;
  }

  async function extractValue({ validateBeforeReturn = false } = {}) {
    await finishActiveTableEditing();

    const nextDocument = buildDraftDocumentFromEditorState();
    const validation = validateMetaGenDocumentDetailed(nextDocument);
    applyEditorValidationFeedback(validation);
    updateGenerationReadinessFromValidation(validation);

    if (validateBeforeReturn && !validation.isValid) {
      throw new Error(formatMetaGenValidationErrorMessage(validation));
    }

    const snapshot = cloneDocumentSnapshot(documentRecord, nextDocument);
    documentRecord.document = nextDocument;

    return snapshot;
  }

  function readParamsSnapshot() {
    return normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsTable?.extractDocumentValue?.() || sectionDefaults.params);
  }

  const paramsHistory = createMetaGenParamsHistoryController({
    maxDepth: tableConfig.tables.params.history?.maxDepth,
    initialSnapshot: readParamsSnapshot()
  });
  let isParamsReplayInProgress = false;
  let paramsSnapshotBaseline = safeSerialize(paramsHistory.getPresent());
  const paramsUndoRedoStateListeners = new Set();

  function getTargetTableContextId(target) {
    if (typeof Node !== 'undefined' && !(target instanceof Node)) {
      return null;
    }

    if (paramsContainer.contains(target)) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.params;
    }

    if (dataContainer.contains(target)) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.data;
    }

    if (instancesContainer.contains(target)) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.instances;
    }

    return null;
  }

  let lastTableContextId = null;

  function getFocusedTableContextId() {
    const activeElementContextId = getTargetTableContextId(document.activeElement);
    if (activeElementContextId) {
      return activeElementContextId;
    }

    const editingContextId = getEditingTableContextId();
    if (editingContextId) {
      return editingContextId;
    }

    return lastTableContextId;
  }

  function isParamsUndoRedoContextActive() {
    return getFocusedTableContextId() === tableConfig.contextIds.params;
  }

  function supportsParamsUndoRedo() {
    return Boolean(paramsTable && paramsHistory);
  }

  function canUndoParams() {
    return supportsParamsUndoRedo() && paramsHistory.canUndo();
  }

  function canRedoParams() {
    return supportsParamsUndoRedo() && paramsHistory.canRedo();
  }

  function getParamsUndoRedoState() {
    const isContextActive = isParamsUndoRedoContextActive();
    return {
      supported: supportsParamsUndoRedo(),
      canUndo: canUndoParams(),
      canRedo: canRedoParams(),
      isContextActive,
      isHotkeyContextActive: isContextActive,
      isParamsUndoRedoContextActive: isContextActive
    };
  }

  function emitParamsUndoRedoState() {
    const state = getParamsUndoRedoState();

    for (const listener of paramsUndoRedoStateListeners) {
      listener(state);
    }
  }

  let runtimeDirty = false;
  const tableDirtyDisposables = [];

  function markDirty() {
    runtimeDirty = true;
    onDirty?.();
  }

  tableDirtyDisposables.push(
    bindTableDirtyTracker(dataTable, () => dataTable?.extractDocumentValue?.(), markDirty, validateEditorDraft)
  );
  tableDirtyDisposables.push(
    bindTableDirtyTracker(instancesTable, () => instancesTable?.extractDocumentValue?.(), markDirty, validateEditorDraft)
  );

  if (typeof paramsTable?.workbook?.onCommandExecuted === 'function') {
    tableDirtyDisposables.push(paramsTable.workbook.onCommandExecuted(() => {
      if (isParamsReplayInProgress) {
        return;
      }

      const nextSnapshot = readParamsSnapshot();
      const nextSerialized = safeSerialize(nextSnapshot);

      if (nextSerialized === paramsSnapshotBaseline) {
        return;
      }

      paramsSnapshotBaseline = nextSerialized;
      paramsHistory.push(nextSnapshot);
      markDirty();
      validateEditorDraft();
      emitParamsUndoRedoState();
    }));
  }

  function buildTableContexts() {
    return [
      {
        contextId: tableConfig.contextIds.params,
        tableRuntime: paramsTable?.workbook
      },
      {
        contextId: tableConfig.contextIds.data,
        tableRuntime: dataTable?.workbook
      },
      {
        contextId: tableConfig.contextIds.instances,
        tableRuntime: instancesTable?.workbook
      }
    ];
  }

  let contextFinalizeInFlight = null;

  async function runContextLeaveFinalization({ reason, blockOnFailure = true } = {}) {
    if (contextFinalizeInFlight) {
      return contextFinalizeInFlight;
    }

    contextFinalizeInFlight = finalizeEditingOnContextLeave({
      tables: buildTableContexts(),
      logger,
      source: lifecycleSource,
      reason,
      blockOnFailure
    }).finally(() => {
      contextFinalizeInFlight = null;
    });

    return contextFinalizeInFlight;
  }

  function getEditingTableContextId() {
    if (paramsTable?.workbook?.isCellEditing?.()) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.params;
    }

    if (dataTable?.workbook?.isCellEditing?.()) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.data;
    }

    if (instancesTable?.workbook?.isCellEditing?.()) {
      return tableConfig.contextIds.instances;
    }

    return null;
  }

  function shouldFinalizeForContextTransfer(target) {
    const editingContextId = getEditingTableContextId();

    if (!editingContextId) {
      return false;
    }

    const targetContextId = getTargetTableContextId(target);
    return targetContextId !== editingContextId;
  }

  function bindContextLossFinalizer() {
    const handleContextTransfer = (event, reason) => {
      const targetContextId = getTargetTableContextId(event.target);
      if (targetContextId) {
        lastTableContextId = targetContextId;
      }

      if (!shouldFinalizeForContextTransfer(event.target)) {
        emitParamsUndoRedoState();
        return;
      }

      void runContextLeaveFinalization({
        reason,
        blockOnFailure: false
      });
      emitParamsUndoRedoState();
    };

    const onPointerDownCapture = (event) => {
      handleContextTransfer(event, tableConfig.transitionReasons.pointerContextSwitch);
    };

    const onFocusInCapture = (event) => {
      handleContextTransfer(event, tableConfig.transitionReasons.focusContextSwitch);
    };

    root.addEventListener('pointerdown', onPointerDownCapture, true);
    root.addEventListener('focusin', onFocusInCapture, true);

    return () => {
      root.removeEventListener('pointerdown', onPointerDownCapture, true);
      root.removeEventListener('focusin', onFocusInCapture, true);
    };
  }

  const disposeContextLossFinalizer = bindContextLossFinalizer();

  async function finishActiveTableEditing() {
    const result = await runContextLeaveFinalization({
      reason: tableConfig.transitionReasons.finishActiveEditing,
      blockOnFailure: false
    });

    return result.outcome;
  }

  async function replayParamsSnapshot(nextSnapshot, reason) {
    const currentEditingContext = getEditingTableContextId();
    if (currentEditingContext === tableConfig.contextIds.params) {
      await finishActiveTableEditing();
    }

    isParamsReplayInProgress = true;

    try {
      const currentSnapshot = readParamsSnapshot();
      const normalizedTargetSnapshot = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(nextSnapshot || sectionDefaults.params);
      const replayBounds = getParamsReplayRefreshBounds(currentSnapshot, normalizedTargetSnapshot);

      paramsTable?.beginReplayAutoStyleSuppression?.();
      try {
        paramsTable?.applyDocumentValue?.(normalizedTargetSnapshot, { refreshAutoStyle: false });
      } finally {
        paramsTable?.endReplayAutoStyleSuppression?.();
      }

      if (replayBounds) {
        paramsTable?.refreshReplayAutoStyleBounds?.(replayBounds);
      }
    } finally {
      isParamsReplayInProgress = false;
      paramsSnapshotBaseline = safeSerialize(readParamsSnapshot());
      validateEditorDraft();
      emitParamsUndoRedoState();
      logger?.info?.(loggerSource, 'MetaGen params replay completed', { reason });
    }
  }

  async function undoParams() {
    if (!canUndoParams()) {
      emitParamsUndoRedoState();
      return false;
    }

    const nextSnapshot = paramsHistory.undo();
    await replayParamsSnapshot(nextSnapshot, tableConfig.paramsUndoRedo.replayReasons.undo);
    return true;
  }

  async function redoParams() {
    if (!canRedoParams()) {
      emitParamsUndoRedoState();
      return false;
    }

    const nextSnapshot = paramsHistory.redo();
    await replayParamsSnapshot(nextSnapshot, tableConfig.paramsUndoRedo.replayReasons.redo);
    return true;
  }

  const disposeParamsHotkeys = bindMetaGenParamsUndoRedoHotkeys({
    root,
    hotkeysConfig: tableConfig.paramsUndoRedo.hotkeys,
    isContextActive: isParamsUndoRedoContextActive,
    handleUndo: undoParams,
    handleRedo: redoParams
  });

  async function trySave() {
    try {
      const nextRecord = await extractValue({ validateBeforeReturn: true });
      await onSave(nextRecord);
      runtimeDirty = false;
    } catch (error) {
      window.alert(`Ошибка сохранения: ${error?.message || String(error)}`);
    }
  }

  bindSaveShortcut(codeTextarea, trySave);
  codeTextarea.addEventListener('input', () => {
    markDirty();
    validateEditorDraft();
  });
  emitParamsUndoRedoState();
  validateEditorDraft();

  logger?.info(loggerSource, 'MetaGen табличный редактор инициализирован');

  return {
    paramsTable,
    dataTable,
    instancesTable,
    isDirty: () => runtimeDirty,
    finishActiveTableEditing,
    async finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave({ reason, blockOnFailure = true } = {}) {
      const result = await runContextLeaveFinalization({ reason, blockOnFailure });
      return {
        continued: result.flow !== TABLE_CONTEXT_FINALIZE_FLOW.BLOCKED,
        outcome: result.outcome,
        reason: result.reason
      };
    },
    async collectDocumentRecord() {
      return extractValue({ validateBeforeReturn: true });
    },
    isParamsUndoRedoContextActive,
    supportsParamsUndoRedo,
    getParamsUndoRedoState,
    getGenerationReadiness: () => ({ ...generationReadinessState }),
    canUndoParams,
    canRedoParams,
    undoParams,
    redoParams,
    subscribeParamsUndoRedoState(listener) {
      if (typeof listener !== 'function') {
        return () => {};
      }

      paramsUndoRedoStateListeners.add(listener);
      listener(getParamsUndoRedoState());

      return () => {
        paramsUndoRedoStateListeners.delete(listener);
      };
    },
    subscribeGenerationReadiness(listener) {
      if (typeof listener !== 'function') {
        return () => {};
      }

      generationReadinessListeners.add(listener);
      listener({ ...generationReadinessState });

      return () => {
        generationReadinessListeners.delete(listener);
      };
    },
    dispose() {
      generationReadinessListeners.clear();
      disposeParamsHotkeys?.();
      disposeContextLossFinalizer?.();
      tableDirtyDisposables.forEach((disposable) => disposable?.dispose?.());
      paramsTable?.dispose?.();
      dataTable?.dispose?.();
      instancesTable?.dispose?.();
      rightAreaSplit?.destroy?.();
      centerSplit?.destroy?.();
      outerSplit?.destroy?.();
      clearMountElement(mountElement);
    }
  };
}

import { PROJECT_CONFIG } from '../../../../shared/config/project-config.js';
import { UI_CONFIG } from '../../../config/ui-config.js';

const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE = '\u0422\u0438\u043f';
const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG = '\u0418\u043c\u044f \u043f\u0435\u0440\u0435\u043c\u0435\u043d\u043d\u043e\u0439';
const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE = '\u0417\u043d\u0430\u0447\u0435\u043d\u0438\u0435';
const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT = '\u041a\u043e\u043c\u043c\u0435\u043d\u0442\u0430\u0440\u0438\u0439';
const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF = 'Conf';

const METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONTRACT = {
  canonicalColumns: [
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF
  ],
  requiredColumns: [
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT,
    METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF
  ],
  requiredDisplayNames: {
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE]: 'Type',
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG]: 'Tag',
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE]: 'Value',
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT]: 'Comment',
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF]: 'Conf'
  },
  aliasesByCanonical: {
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE]: [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TYPE, 'Type', 'type'],
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG]: [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_TAG, 'Tag', 'tag'],
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE]: [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_VALUE, 'Value', 'value'],
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT]: [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT, 'Comment', 'comment'],
    [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF]: [METAGEN_DATA_COLUMN_CONF, 'Conf', 'conf']
  }
};

export const METAGEN_CONFIG = {
  moduleId: PROJECT_CONFIG.moduleIds.metagen,
  moduleName: PROJECT_CONFIG.moduleDisplayNames.metagen,

  documentKind: 'metagen.component',
  documentSchemaVersion: 1,
  defaultType: 'template',
  documentFormats: {
    headerPlusRows: 'header-plus-rows',
    table: 'table',
    list: 'list',
    templateText: 'template-text'
  },
  documentLanguages: {
    stTemplate: 'st-template'
  },
  bootstrapModes: {
    hydrate: 'hydrate',
    seed: 'seed'
  },

  commands: {
    createDocument: 'METAGEN_CREATE_DOCUMENT',
    generateCode: 'METAGEN_GENERATE_CODE',
    validateDocument: 'METAGEN_VALIDATE_DOCUMENT'
  },

  generation: {
    defaultEngine: 'python',
    defaultEntrypoint: 'gen_v2.py',
    defaultMode: 'external',
    defaultOutputLanguage: 'st'
  },

  editor: {
    saveShortcutKey: 's',
    containerIdPrefixes: {
      params: 'metagen-params-',
      data: 'metagen-data-',
      instances: 'metagen-instances-'
    },
    classNames: {
      centerStack: 'metagen-editor-center-stack'
    },
    layout: {
      outerSplit: {
        direction: 'horizontal',
        sizes: [30, 70],
        minSize: [260, 400],
        gutterSize: 4,
        cursor: 'col-resize'
      },

FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenDataContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

function normalizeAliasToken(value) {
  const normalized = String(value ?? '').trim();
  if (!normalized) {
    return '';
  }
  return /^[\x00-\x7F]+$/.test(normalized) ? normalized.toLowerCase() : normalized;
}

function normalizeContractColumns(columns, fallback = []) {
  if (!Array.isArray(columns) || columns.length === 0) {
    return [...fallback];
  }
  return columns.map((column) => String(column ?? '').trim()).filter((column) => column !== '');
}

function buildAliasToCanonical(aliasesByCanonical) {
  const index = new Map();

  Object.entries(aliasesByCanonical).forEach(([canonicalName, aliases]) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(aliases)) {
      return;
    }

    aliases.forEach((alias) => {
      const normalizedAlias = normalizeAliasToken(alias);
      if (!normalizedAlias || index.has(normalizedAlias)) {
        return;
      }
      index.set(normalizedAlias, canonicalName);
    });
  });

  return index;
}

export function resolveMetaGenDataContract(tableConfig = {}) {
  const configFromTable = tableConfig?.contract || {};
  const configuredColumns = normalizeContractColumns(configFromTable.canonicalColumns, tableConfig?.headers || []);
  const canonicalColumns = configuredColumns.length > 0
    ? configuredColumns
    : normalizeContractColumns(METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.tables.data.contract?.canonicalColumns, []);
  const requiredColumns = normalizeContractColumns(configFromTable.requiredColumns, canonicalColumns);

  const requiredDisplayNames = { ...(configFromTable.requiredDisplayNames || {}) };
  requiredColumns.forEach((canonicalName) => {
    if (!requiredDisplayNames[canonicalName]) {
      requiredDisplayNames[canonicalName] = canonicalName;
    }
  });

  const aliasesByCanonical = { ...(configFromTable.aliasesByCanonical || {}) };
  requiredColumns.forEach((canonicalName) => {
    if (!Array.isArray(aliasesByCanonical[canonicalName])) {
      aliasesByCanonical[canonicalName] = [canonicalName];
    } else if (!aliasesByCanonical[canonicalName].includes(canonicalName)) {
      aliasesByCanonical[canonicalName] = [canonicalName, ...aliasesByCanonical[canonicalName]];
    }
  });

  return {
    canonicalColumns,
    requiredColumns,
    requiredDisplayNames,
    aliasesByCanonical,
    aliasToCanonical: buildAliasToCanonical(aliasesByCanonical)
  };
}

export function canonicalizeMetaGenDataColumnName(columnName, tableConfig = {}) {
  const contract = resolveMetaGenDataContract(tableConfig);
  const normalizedAlias = normalizeAliasToken(columnName);
  if (!normalizedAlias) {
    return null;
  }
  return contract.aliasToCanonical.get(normalizedAlias) || null;
}

export function normalizeMetaGenDataColumns(columns, tableConfig = {}) {
  const contract = resolveMetaGenDataContract(tableConfig);
  const sourceColumns = Array.isArray(columns) ? columns : [];
  const columnIndexByCanonical = {};
  const duplicateRequiredColumns = [];
  const normalizedColumns = sourceColumns.map((columnName, columnIndex) => {
    const normalizedName = String(columnName ?? '').trim();
    const canonicalName = canonicalizeMetaGenDataColumnName(normalizedName, tableConfig);

    if (!canonicalName) {
      return normalizedName;
    }

    if (Object.hasOwn(columnIndexByCanonical, canonicalName)) {
      duplicateRequiredColumns.push({
        canonicalName,
        displayName: contract.requiredDisplayNames[canonicalName] || canonicalName,
        columnIndex
      });
      return canonicalName;
    }

    columnIndexByCanonical[canonicalName] = columnIndex;
    return canonicalName;
  });

  const missingRequiredColumns = contract.requiredColumns
    .filter((canonicalName) => !Object.hasOwn(columnIndexByCanonical, canonicalName))
    .map((canonicalName) => contract.requiredDisplayNames[canonicalName] || canonicalName);

  return {
    contract,
    normalizedColumns,
    columnIndexByCanonical,
    duplicateRequiredColumns,
    missingRequiredColumns
  };
}

function mapRowToCanonicalColumns(rowValues, canonicalColumns, columnIndexByCanonical) {
  return canonicalColumns.map((canonicalName, canonicalIndex) => {
    const sourceIndex = columnIndexByCanonical[canonicalName];
    if (Number.isInteger(sourceIndex) && sourceIndex >= 0) {
      return rowValues[sourceIndex] ?? '';
    }
    return rowValues[canonicalIndex] ?? '';
  });
}

export function normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const columnNormalization = normalizeMetaGenDataColumns(dataDocument?.columns, tableConfig);
  const canonicalColumns = [...columnNormalization.contract.canonicalColumns];
  const rows = Array.isArray(dataDocument?.rows)
    ? dataDocument.rows
      .map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row))
      .map((row) => mapRowToCanonicalColumns(row, canonicalColumns, columnNormalization.columnIndexByCanonical))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table,
    columns: canonicalColumns,
    rows
  };
}

export function validateMetaGenDataDocumentContract(dataDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const errors = [];

  if (!dataDocument || typeof dataDocument !== 'object' || Array.isArray(dataDocument)) {
    return {
      isValid: false,
      errors: ['data должен быть объектом'],
      analysis: null
    };
  }

  if (dataDocument.format != null && dataDocument.format !== METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table) {
    errors.push(`data.format должен быть ${METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.table}`);
  }

  if (!Array.isArray(dataDocument.columns)) {
    errors.push('data.columns должен быть массивом');
  }

  if (dataDocument.rows != null && !Array.isArray(dataDocument.rows)) {
    errors.push('data.rows должен быть массивом');
  }

  const analysis = normalizeMetaGenDataColumns(dataDocument.columns, tableConfig);
  const hasCanonicalPersistedColumns = Array.isArray(dataDocument.columns)
    && dataDocument.columns.length === analysis.contract.canonicalColumns.length
    && dataDocument.columns.every((columnName, columnIndex) => {
      const normalizedColumnName = String(columnName ?? '').trim();
      return normalizedColumnName === analysis.contract.canonicalColumns[columnIndex];
    });

  if (Array.isArray(dataDocument.columns) && !hasCanonicalPersistedColumns) {
    errors.push(`data.columns must match canonical persisted contract order ${JSON.stringify(analysis.contract.canonicalColumns)}`);
  }

  analysis.duplicateRequiredColumns.forEach((entry) => {
    errors.push(`Duplicate data column alias for '${entry.displayName}' at data.columns[${entry.columnIndex}]`);
  });

  if (analysis.missingRequiredColumns.length > 0) {
    errors.push(`Missing required data columns ${JSON.stringify([...analysis.missingRequiredColumns].sort())}`);
  }

  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors,
    analysis
  };
}


export function hasPersistedMetaGenDataShape(dataDocument) {
  if (!dataDocument || typeof dataDocument !== 'object') {
    return false;
  }

  const hasRows = Array.isArray(dataDocument.rows) && dataDocument.rows.length > 0;
  const hasColumns = Array.isArray(dataDocument.columns) && dataDocument.columns.length > 0;

  return hasRows || hasColumns;
}

export function getMetaGenDataRequiredDimensions(dataDocument, tableConfig = {}, options = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(dataDocument, tableConfig);
  const bootstrapRows = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1);
  const bootstrapColumns = Math.max(1, Array.isArray(tableConfig?.headers) ? tableConfig.headers.length : 0);

  const widestRow = normalized.rows.reduce(
    (maxValue, row) => Math.max(maxValue, Array.isArray(row) ? row.length : 0),
    0
  );

  // Runtime sheet semantics: always open at max(bootstrap seed, persisted payload shape).
  // Persisted payload itself stays compact via extract/save path.
  const payloadRows = normalized.rows.length || 1;
  const payloadColumns = Math.max(normalized.columns.length || 0, widestRow || 0, 1);

  return {
    rowCount: Math.max(bootstrapRows, payloadRows),
    columnCount: Math.max(bootstrapColumns, payloadColumns),
    normalized
  };
}

import { createDocumentGuid } from '../../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';
import { normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument } from './metagenParamsContract.js';
import { normalizeMetaGenDataDocument } from './metagenDataContract.js';
import { normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument } from './metagenInstancesContract.js';

export function createMetaGenDocumentSectionDefaults() {
  const tableConfig = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.tables;

  return {
    params: normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument({}),
    data: normalizeMetaGenDataDocument({}, tableConfig.data),
    instances: normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument({}, tableConfig.instances),
    code: {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.templateText,
      language: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentLanguages.stTemplate,
      text: ''
    }
  };
}

function normalizeMetaGenCodeText(value) {
  if (value == null) {
    return '';
  }

  if (typeof value === 'boolean') {
    return value ? 'true' : 'false';
  }

  return String(value);
}

export function normalizeMetaGenCodeDocument(codeDocument, fallbackCode = null) {
  const sectionDefaults = createMetaGenDocumentSectionDefaults();
  const baseCode = (fallbackCode && typeof fallbackCode === 'object' && !Array.isArray(fallbackCode))
    ? fallbackCode
    : sectionDefaults.code;
  const sourceCode = (codeDocument && typeof codeDocument === 'object' && !Array.isArray(codeDocument))
    ? codeDocument
    : {};

  return {
    ...baseCode,
    ...sourceCode,
    text: normalizeMetaGenCodeText(sourceCode.text)
  };
}

export function normalizeMetaGenDocumentForPersistence(document, tableConfig = METAGEN_CONFIG.tableRuntime.tables) {
  const sectionDefaults = createMetaGenDocumentSectionDefaults();
  const sourceDocument = (document && typeof document === 'object' && !Array.isArray(document))
    ? document
    : {};

  return {
    ...sourceDocument,
    params: normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(sourceDocument.params || sectionDefaults.params),
    data: normalizeMetaGenDataDocument(sourceDocument.data || sectionDefaults.data, tableConfig.data),
    instances: normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(sourceDocument.instances || sectionDefaults.instances, tableConfig.instances),
    code: normalizeMetaGenCodeDocument(sourceDocument.code, sectionDefaults.code)
  };
}

export function createMetaGenDocument({ name }) {
  const safeName = String(name || METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName).trim();
  const safeId = createDocumentGuid();
  const sectionDefaults = createMetaGenDocumentSectionDefaults();

  return {
    kind: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind,
    version: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentSchemaVersion,
    component: {
      id: safeId,
      name: safeName,
      type: METAGEN_CONFIG.defaultType,
      module: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleName,
      description: ''
    },
    params: sectionDefaults.params,
    data: sectionDefaults.data,
    instances: sectionDefaults.instances,
    code: sectionDefaults.code,
    generation: {
      engine: METAGEN_CONFIG.generation.defaultEngine,
      entrypoint: METAGEN_CONFIG.generation.defaultEntrypoint,
      mode: METAGEN_CONFIG.generation.defaultMode,
      output: {
        language: METAGEN_CONFIG.generation.defaultOutputLanguage,
        fileName: `${safeId}.st`
      }
    },
    meta: {
      author: '',
      importedFrom: '',
      importedSheet: ''
    }
  };
}

FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenGeneratorBridge.js
==================================================

export function createMetaGenGeneratorBridge({
  launchGenerate,
  resolveGenerationReadiness,
  preflightErrorCode = ''
} = {}) {
  if (typeof launchGenerate !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('MetaGen generator bridge requires launchGenerate(payload)');
  }

  const readGenerationReadiness = typeof resolveGenerationReadiness === 'function'
    ? resolveGenerationReadiness
    : () => null;

  function normalizeGenerationReadiness(readiness) {
    if (!readiness || typeof readiness !== 'object') {
      return { isReady: true, reason: '' };
    }

    return {
      isReady: readiness.isReady !== false,
      reason: String(readiness.reason || '').trim()
    };
  }

  function buildPreflightError(readiness) {
    const code = String(preflightErrorCode || '').trim();
    const message = readiness.reason || code;
    const error = new Error(message);
    error.code = code;
    error.readiness = readiness;
    return error;
  }

  return {
    async generate(payload = {}) {
      const readiness = normalizeGenerationReadiness(readGenerationReadiness());
      if (!readiness.isReady) {
        throw buildPreflightError(readiness);
      }

      return launchGenerate(payload);
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenInstancesContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

function normalizeInstancesRow(row, fixedColumnCount) {
  const normalizedRow = normalizeRowLike(row).slice(0, fixedColumnCount);

  while (normalizedRow.length < fixedColumnCount) {
    normalizedRow.push('');
  }

  return normalizedRow;
}

export function normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const fixedColumnCount = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.fixedColumnCount) || 1);
  const rows = Array.isArray(instancesDocument?.rows)
    ? instancesDocument.rows.map((row) => normalizeInstancesRow(row, fixedColumnCount))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list,
    rows
  };
}

export function validateMetaGenInstancesDocumentContract(instancesDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const errors = [];

  if (!instancesDocument || typeof instancesDocument !== 'object' || Array.isArray(instancesDocument)) {
    errors.push('instances должен быть объектом');
    return {
      isValid: false,
      errors
    };
  }

  if (instancesDocument.format != null && instancesDocument.format !== METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list) {
    errors.push(`instances.format должен быть ${METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.list}`);
  }

  if ('rows' in instancesDocument && !Array.isArray(instancesDocument.rows)) {
    errors.push('instances.rows должен быть массивом');
    return {
      isValid: false,
      errors
    };
  }

  const fixedColumnCount = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.fixedColumnCount) || 1);
  const rawRows = Array.isArray(instancesDocument.rows) ? instancesDocument.rows : [];

  rawRows.forEach((row, index) => {
    if (row == null) {
      return;
    }

    if (!Array.isArray(row)) {
      errors.push(`instances.rows[${index}] должен быть массивом`);
      return;
    }

    if (row.length > fixedColumnCount) {
      errors.push(
        `instances.rows[${index}] имеет ${row.length} элементов, ожидается не больше ${fixedColumnCount}`
      );
    }
  });

  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors
  };
}
export function getMetaGenInstancesRequiredDimensions(instancesDocument, tableConfig = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenInstancesDocument(instancesDocument, tableConfig);
  const bootstrapRows = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1);
  const fixedColumnCount = Math.max(1, Number(tableConfig?.fixedColumnCount) || 1);
  const payloadRows = normalized.rows.length || 1;

  return {
    rowCount: Math.max(bootstrapRows, payloadRows),
    columnCount: fixedColumnCount,
    normalized
  };
}

FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenModule.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/app-config.js';
import { createMetaGenDocument } from './metagenDocumentFactory.js';
import { formatMetaGenValidationErrorMessage, validateMetaGenDocument } from './metagenSchema.js';
import { createMetaGenEditor } from '../../editors/metagen/createMetaGenEditor.js';
import { slugifyDocumentName } from '../../runtime/naming.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

export function createMetaGenModule({ logger }) {
  return {
    id: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId,
    name: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleName,
    documentKinds: [METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind],

    getDefaultName() {
      return METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName;
    },

    createDefaultDocument({ name }) {
      return createMetaGenDocument({ name });
    },

    getFileName(document) {
      return `${slugifyDocumentName(document?.component?.name || METAGEN_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName)}${APP_CONFIG.project.fileExtensions.default}`;
    },

    validate(document) {
      return validateMetaGenDocument(document);
    },

    async openDocument({ documentRecord, mountElement, onDirty }) {
      return createMetaGenEditor({
        documentRecord,
        mountElement,
        logger,
        onDirty,
        onSave: async (nextRecord) => {
          const validation = validateMetaGenDocument(nextRecord.document);

          if (!validation.isValid) {
            logger.warn(METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId, 'Документ MetaGen не прошёл валидацию', validation.errors);
            throw new Error(formatMetaGenValidationErrorMessage(validation));
          }

          return true;
        }
      });
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsContract.js
==================================================

import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from './metagenConfig.js';

function normalizeRowLike(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((cell) => cell ?? '');
  }

  if (value == null) {
    return [];
  }

  return [value];
}

export function normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument) {
  if (Array.isArray(paramsDocument)) {
    const rows = paramsDocument.map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row));

    return {
      format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
      header: rows[0] || [],
      rows: rows.slice(1)
    };
  }

  const header = normalizeRowLike(paramsDocument?.header);
  const rows = Array.isArray(paramsDocument?.rows)
    ? paramsDocument.rows.map((row) => normalizeRowLike(row))
    : [];

  return {
    format: METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows,
    header,
    rows
  };
}

export function validateMetaGenParamsDocumentContract(paramsDocument) {
  const errors = [];

  if (!paramsDocument || typeof paramsDocument !== 'object' || Array.isArray(paramsDocument)) {
    errors.push('params должен быть объектом');
    return {
      isValid: false,
      errors
    };
  }

  if (paramsDocument.format != null && paramsDocument.format !== METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows) {
    errors.push(`params.format должен быть ${METAGEN_CONFIG.documentFormats.headerPlusRows}`);
  }

  if ('header' in paramsDocument && !Array.isArray(paramsDocument.header)) {
    errors.push('params.header должен быть массивом');
  }

  if ('rows' in paramsDocument && !Array.isArray(paramsDocument.rows)) {
    errors.push('params.rows должен быть массивом');
    return {
      isValid: false,
      errors
    };
  }

  const headerLength = Array.isArray(paramsDocument.header) ? paramsDocument.header.length : 0;
  const rawRows = Array.isArray(paramsDocument.rows) ? paramsDocument.rows : [];

  for (let index = 0; index < rawRows.length; index += 1) {
    const row = rawRows[index];

    if (row == null) {
      continue;
    }

    if (!Array.isArray(row)) {
      errors.push(`params.rows[${index}] должен быть массивом`);
      continue;
    }

    if (row.length > headerLength) {
      errors.push(
        `params.rows[${index}] имеет ${row.length} элементов, ожидается не больше ${headerLength}`
      );
    }
  }

  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors
  };
}
export function getMetaGenParamsRequiredDimensions(paramsDocument, tableConfig, options = {}) {
  const normalized = normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(paramsDocument);
  const rows = [normalized.header, ...normalized.rows];
  // Runtime sheet semantics: always open at max(bootstrap seed, persisted payload shape).
  // Persisted payload itself stays compact via extract/save path.
  const payloadRows = rows.length || 1;
  const requiredRows = Math.max(Number(tableConfig?.rows) || 1, payloadRows);
  const widestRow = rows.reduce((maxValue, row) => Math.max(maxValue, Array.isArray(row) ? row.length : 0), 0);
  const payloadColumns = widestRow || 1;
  const requiredColumns = Math.max(Number(tableConfig?.defaultColumns) || 1, payloadColumns);

  return {
    rowCount: requiredRows,
    columnCount: requiredColumns,
    normalized
  };
}




==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/modules/metagen/metagenParamsHistoryController.js
==================================================

import { normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument } from './metagenParamsContract.js';

function safeSerialize(snapshot) {
  try {
    return JSON.stringify(snapshot);
  } catch {
    return '';
  }
}

function toSemanticSnapshot(snapshot) {
  return normalizeMetaGenParamsDocument(snapshot);
}

function cloneSemanticSnapshot(snapshot) {
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(toSemanticSnapshot(snapshot)));
}

export function createMetaGenParamsHistoryController({ maxDepth = 100, initialSnapshot } = {}) {
  const safeMaxDepth = Math.max(1, Number(maxDepth) || 1);
  let past = [];
  let future = [];
  let present = cloneSemanticSnapshot(initialSnapshot || {});

  function reset(nextSnapshot) {
    past = [];
    future = [];
    present = cloneSemanticSnapshot(nextSnapshot || {});
    return present;
  }

  function push(nextSnapshot) {
    const normalizedNext = cloneSemanticSnapshot(nextSnapshot || {});

    if (safeSerialize(normalizedNext) === safeSerialize(present)) {
      return false;
    }

    past.push(present);
    if (past.length > safeMaxDepth) {
      past = past.slice(past.length - safeMaxDepth);
    }

    present = normalizedNext;
    future = [];
    return true;
  }

  function canUndo() {
    return past.length > 0;
  }

  function canRedo() {
    return future.length > 0;
  }

  function undo() {
    if (!canUndo()) {
      return present;
    }

    future.unshift(present);
    present = past.pop();
    return present;
  }

  function redo() {
    if (!canRedo()) {
      return present;
    }

    past.push(present);
    present = future.shift();
    return present;
  }

  function getPresent() {
    return cloneSemanticSnapshot(present);
  }

  function getState() {
    return {
      past: past.map((snapshot) => cloneSemanticSnapshot(snapshot)),
      present: getPresent(),
      future: future.map((snapshot) => cloneSemanticSnapshot(snapshot))
    };
  }

  return {
    reset,
    push,
    canUndo,
    canRedo,
    undo,
    redo,
    getPresent,
    getState
  };
}
