==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/adapters/createHttpRuntimeAdapter.js
==================================================

import { normalizeRuntimeRequest } from '../runtimeClientContract.js';
import { PLATFORM_CONFIG } from '../../../../shared/config/platform-config.js';

function normalizeBaseUrl(value) {
  return String(value || '').replace(/\/+$/, '');
}

function normalizePath(value) {
  const path = String(value || '').trim();
  if (!path) {
    throw new Error('Backend commands endpoint path is required');
  }
  return path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
}

function isPlainObject(value) {
  return Boolean(value) && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value);
}

const DEFAULT_ERROR_CODES = {
  internal: PLATFORM_CONFIG.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.internal
};
const DEFAULT_IMPORT_ENDPOINT_PATH = PLATFORM_CONFIG.backend.projectImportsEndpoint;
const DEFAULT_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = PLATFORM_CONFIG.backend.requestTimeoutMs;
const DEFAULT_IMPORT_ARCHIVE_FIELD_NAME = PLATFORM_CONFIG.backend.importContract.archiveFieldName;

function createTimeoutController(timeoutMs) {
  const abortController = typeof AbortController === 'function' ? new AbortController() : null;
  const timeoutId = abortController
    ? setTimeout(() => abortController.abort(), timeoutMs)
    : null;

  return {
    signal: abortController?.signal,
    clear: () => {
      if (timeoutId) {
        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      }
    }
  };
}

export function createHttpRuntimeAdapter({
  baseUrl,
  endpointPath,
  importEndpointPath = DEFAULT_IMPORT_ENDPOINT_PATH,
  timeoutMs = DEFAULT_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS,
  fetchImpl = fetch,
  errorCodes = DEFAULT_ERROR_CODES,
  importArchiveFieldName = DEFAULT_IMPORT_ARCHIVE_FIELD_NAME,
  defaultHeaders = {}
}) {
  if (typeof fetchImpl !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('fetch implementation is required');
  }

  const commandUrl = `${normalizeBaseUrl(baseUrl)}${normalizePath(endpointPath)}`;
  const importUrl = `${normalizeBaseUrl(baseUrl)}${normalizePath(importEndpointPath)}`;
  const normalizedBaseUrl = normalizeBaseUrl(baseUrl);

  function createInternalFailure({
    requestId = '',
    message = 'Unexpected runtime error',
    details = null
  } = {}) {
    return {
      ...(requestId ? { requestId } : {}),
      ok: false,
      error: {
        code: errorCodes.internal,
        message,
        ...(details == null ? {} : { details })
      }
    };
  }

  async function execute(request) {
    const normalizedRequest = normalizeRuntimeRequest(request);
    const timeoutController = createTimeoutController(timeoutMs);

    try {
      const response = await fetchImpl(commandUrl, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          ...defaultHeaders
        },
        body: JSON.stringify(normalizedRequest),
        signal: timeoutController.signal
      });

      let payload = null;
      try {
        payload = await response.json();
      } catch (error) {
        return createInternalFailure({
          requestId: normalizedRequest.requestId,
          message: 'Invalid runtime command response payload',
          details: {
            reason: error?.message || String(error),
            status: Number(response?.status || 0) || 0
          }
        });
      }

      if (isPlainObject(payload) && typeof payload.ok === 'boolean') {
        if (typeof payload.requestId !== 'string' || !payload.requestId.trim()) {
          payload.requestId = normalizedRequest.requestId;
        }
        return payload;
      }

      if (!response.ok) {
        return createInternalFailure({
          requestId: normalizedRequest.requestId,
          message: `Runtime command failed: HTTP ${response.status}`,
          details: {
            status: Number(response?.status || 0) || 0,
            statusText: String(response?.statusText || '').trim(),
            payload: isPlainObject(payload) ? payload : null
          }
        });
      }

      return createInternalFailure({
        requestId: normalizedRequest.requestId,
        message: 'Invalid runtime command response payload',
        details: {
          status: Number(response?.status || 0) || 0,
          payload: isPlainObject(payload) ? payload : null
        }
      });
    } catch (error) {
      return createInternalFailure({
        requestId: normalizedRequest.requestId,
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
    } finally {
      timeoutController.clear();
    }
  }

  async function downloadBinary(relativePath) {
    const downloadUrl = `${normalizedBaseUrl}${normalizePath(relativePath)}`;
    const timeoutController = createTimeoutController(timeoutMs);
    try {
      const response = await fetchImpl(downloadUrl, {
        method: 'GET',
        signal: timeoutController.signal
      });
      if (!response.ok) {
        throw new Error(`Export download failed: HTTP ${response.status}`);
      }
      return new Uint8Array(await response.arrayBuffer());
    } finally {
      timeoutController.clear();
    }
  }

  async function importProjectArchive(payload) {
    const fileName = String(payload?.fileName || '').trim();
    if (!fileName) {
      throw new Error('Import archive fileName is required');
    }

    const bytesInput = payload?.bytes;
    const bytes = Array.isArray(bytesInput)
      ? new Uint8Array(bytesInput)
      : bytesInput instanceof Uint8Array
        ? bytesInput
        : null;
    if (!bytes || !bytes.length) {
      throw new Error('Import archive bytes are required');
    }

    const timeoutController = createTimeoutController(timeoutMs);
    const formData = new FormData();
    formData.append(importArchiveFieldName, new Blob([bytes], { type: 'application/zip' }), fileName);

    try {
      const response = await fetchImpl(importUrl, {
        method: 'POST',
        body: formData,
        signal: timeoutController.signal
      });
      const responsePayload = await response.json();
      if (typeof responsePayload?.ok === 'boolean') {
        return responsePayload;
      }

      return {
        ok: false,
        error: {
          code: errorCodes.internal,
          message: 'Invalid import response payload'
        }
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        ok: false,
        error: {
          code: errorCodes.internal,
          message: error?.message || String(error)
        }
      };
    } finally {
      timeoutController.clear();
    }
  }

  return {
    execute,
    downloadBinary,
    importProjectArchive
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/appCloseCoordinator.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import {
  createLifecycleOutcome,
  normalizeLifecycleOutcome,
  resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses
} from './runtimeClientContract.js';

export function createAppCloseCoordinator({
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  hasDirtyProject,
  requestAppQuit,
  guardBrowserCloseDecision,
  allowBrowserClose
}) {
  const lifecycleStatuses = resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses();

  function normalizeConfirmSaveOutcome(decision) {
    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({ status: lifecycleStatuses.success });
    }
    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return createLifecycleOutcome({ status: lifecycleStatuses.cancelled });
    }

    return normalizeLifecycleOutcome(decision, {
      fallbackStatus: lifecycleStatuses.malformed,
      truthyStatus: lifecycleStatuses.success,
      falsyStatus: lifecycleStatuses.cancelled
    });
  }

  async function requestExit() {
    const confirmOutcome = normalizeConfirmSaveOutcome(await confirmSaveIfDirty());

    if (confirmOutcome.status !== lifecycleStatuses.success) {
      return confirmOutcome;
    }

    await requestAppQuit();
    return createLifecycleOutcome({ status: lifecycleStatuses.success });
  }

  function resolveBrowserCloseGuardDecision() {
    if (!hasDirtyProject()) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserCloseGuardDecisions.allow;
    }

    return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserCloseGuardDecisions.block;
  }

  function applyBrowserCloseGuardDecision(guardDecision) {
    if (guardDecision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserCloseGuardDecisions.block) {
      return guardBrowserCloseDecision();
    }

    return allowBrowserClose();
  }

  return {
    requestExit,
    resolveBrowserCloseGuardDecision,
    applyBrowserCloseGuardDecision
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.js
==================================================

import {
  createLifecycleOutcome,
  resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject,
  resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses,
  resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject,
  resolveBackendSessionPayloadFromRuntimeProject,
  resolveRuntimeCommandError
} from './runtimeClientContract.js';

export function buildBackendSavePayloadForSession({
  currentProject,
  backendSource,
  projectSnapshot
} = {}) {
  const projectId = resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });
  if (!projectId) {
    throw new Error('Backend project id is missing');
  }
  const lockToken = resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });
  if (!lockToken) {
    throw new Error('Backend lock token is missing');
  }
  if (!projectSnapshot || typeof projectSnapshot !== 'object') {
    throw new Error('Backend project snapshot is missing');
  }

  return {
    projectId,
    lockToken,
    projectSnapshot
  };
}

export function buildBackendSaveAsPayloadForSession({
  currentProject,
  backendSource,
  projectSnapshot,
  payloadFields = {},
  newName = '',
  comment = ''
} = {}) {
  const savePayload = buildBackendSavePayloadForSession({
    currentProject,
    backendSource,
    projectSnapshot
  });
  const saveAsNameField = String(payloadFields.saveProjectAsName || '').trim();
  const saveAsCommentField = String(payloadFields.projectComment || '').trim();
  const normalizedNewName = String(newName || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedNewName) {
    throw new Error('Backend save-as project name is required');
  }
  if (!saveAsNameField || !saveAsCommentField) {
    throw new Error('Backend save-as payload fields are missing');
  }

  return {
    ...savePayload,
    [saveAsNameField]: normalizedNewName,
    [saveAsCommentField]: String(comment || '').trim()
  };
}

export function resolveBackendLockReleaseBlockedMessage({
  releaseResult,
  releaseResultStates,
  text
}) {
  const state = String(releaseResult?.state || '').trim();
  if (state === String(releaseResultStates?.blockedActiveProcessBusy || '').trim()) {
    return text.backendLockReleaseBlockedActiveProcessBusy;
  }
  if (state === String(releaseResultStates?.blockedLostProjectLock || '').trim()) {
    return text.backendLockReleaseBlockedLostProjectLock;
  }
  return text.backendLockReleaseBlockedFailure;
}

export function logBackendLockReleaseBlockedTransition({
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  releaseResult,
  reason = '',
  releaseResultStates,
  text
}) {
  loggerWarn(
    loggerSource,
    resolveBackendLockReleaseBlockedMessage({
      releaseResult,
      releaseResultStates,
      text
    }),
    {
      reason: String(reason || '').trim(),
      state: String(releaseResult?.state || '').trim(),
      errorCode: String(releaseResult?.errorCode || '').trim()
    }
  );
}

export function resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation({
  errorCode,
  errorCodes,
  text
}) {
  const normalizedErrorCode = String(errorCode || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedErrorCode) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: '',
      warningText: text.backendCommandFailed
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.projectLocked) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: errorCodes.projectLocked,
      warningText: text.backendProjectLocked
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.lostProjectLock) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: errorCodes.lostProjectLock,
      warningText: text.backendProjectLockLost
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.activeProcessBusy) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: '',
      warningText: text.backendActiveProcessBusy
    };
  }

  return {
    lockErrorCode: '',
    warningText: text.backendCommandFailed
  };
}

export function createBackendCommandSessionOrchestrator({
  backendRuntimeClient,
  nextBackendRequestId,
  getProjectManager,
  resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation,
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  backendText,
  commandModuleId,
  backendCommands,
  backendErrorCodes,
  backendSource,
  backendLockReleaseStates,
  backendHeartbeatIntervalMs,
  backendHeartbeatFailedText,
  backendHeartbeatStopReasonLost,
  backendHeartbeatStopReasonSwitch,
  setIntervalFn = setInterval,
  clearIntervalFn = clearInterval
}) {
  const lifecycleStatuses = resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses();
  let backendHeartbeatTimerId = null;
  let backendHeartbeatInFlight = false;

  function getProjectManagerOrNull() {
    return getProjectManager?.() || null;
  }

  function stopBackendHeartbeat(_reason = '') {
    if (backendHeartbeatTimerId) {
      clearIntervalFn(backendHeartbeatTimerId);
      backendHeartbeatTimerId = null;
    }
    backendHeartbeatInFlight = false;
  }

  function resolveBackendLockErrorCode(errorCode) {
    const normalized = String(errorCode || '').trim();
    if (!normalized) {
      return '';
    }
    if (normalized === backendErrorCodes.projectLocked) {
      return backendErrorCodes.projectLocked;
    }
    if (normalized === backendErrorCodes.lostProjectLock) {
      return backendErrorCodes.lostProjectLock;
    }
    return '';
  }

  function handleLostBackendProjectLock() {
    stopBackendHeartbeat(backendHeartbeatStopReasonLost);
    const projectManager = getProjectManagerOrNull();
    projectManager?.setBackendProjectLockToken?.('');
  }

  function normalizeBackendCommandFailureOutcome({
    error,
    fallbackErrorCode = '',
    fallbackErrorMessage = '',
    fallbackErrorDetails = null
  } = {}) {
    const normalizedError = resolveRuntimeCommandError(error, {
      fallbackCode: fallbackErrorCode,
      fallbackMessage: fallbackErrorMessage,
      fallbackDetails: fallbackErrorDetails
    });
    const errorCode = String(normalizedError?.code || '').trim();
    const errorMessage = String(normalizedError?.message || '').trim();
    const errorDetails = normalizedError?.details ?? normalizedError?.errorDetails ?? null;

    return {
      ok: false,
      result: null,
      errorCode,
      errorMessage,
      errorDetails,
      details: errorDetails,
      error: {
        ...(normalizedError || {}),
        code: errorCode,
        message: errorMessage,
        ...(errorDetails === null ? {} : { details: errorDetails, errorDetails })
      }
    };
  }

  function normalizeBackendCommandSuccessOutcome(result = {}) {
    const normalizedResult = (result && typeof result === 'object' && !Array.isArray(result))
      ? result
      : {};
    return {
      ok: true,
      result: normalizedResult,
      errorCode: '',
      errorMessage: '',
      errorDetails: null,
      details: null,
      error: null
    };
  }

  async function executeBackendCommand(command, payload = {}) {
    let response = null;
    try {
      response = await backendRuntimeClient.execute({
        requestId: nextBackendRequestId(),
        module: commandModuleId,
        command,
        payload
      });
    } catch (error) {
      const runtimeFailure = normalizeBackendCommandFailureOutcome({
        error,
        fallbackErrorCode: backendErrorCodes.internal,
        fallbackErrorMessage: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      loggerWarn(
        loggerSource,
        backendText.backendCommandFailed,
        { command, ...(runtimeFailure.error || {}) }
      );
      return runtimeFailure;
    }

    if (!response.ok) {
      const responseFailure = normalizeBackendCommandFailureOutcome({
        error: response
      });
      const failurePresentation = resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation({
        errorCode: responseFailure.errorCode,
        errorCodes: backendErrorCodes,
        text: backendText
      });
      const lockErrorCode = resolveBackendLockErrorCode(failurePresentation.lockErrorCode);
      loggerWarn(
        loggerSource,
        failurePresentation.warningText,
        { command, ...(responseFailure.error || {}) }
      );
      if (lockErrorCode === backendErrorCodes.lostProjectLock) {
        handleLostBackendProjectLock();
      }
      return normalizeBackendCommandFailureOutcome({
        error: responseFailure.error,
        fallbackErrorCode: failurePresentation.lockErrorCode || responseFailure.errorCode,
        fallbackErrorMessage: responseFailure.errorMessage,
        fallbackErrorDetails: responseFailure.errorDetails
      });
    }

    return normalizeBackendCommandSuccessOutcome(response.result);
  }

  async function releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason = '' } = {}) {
    const projectManager = getProjectManagerOrNull();
    const currentProject = projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.();
    const isBackendProject = currentProject?.source === backendSource;
    if (!isBackendProject) {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(reason);
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.success,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.noBackendProject,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: true
      };
    }

    const lockToken = resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject({
      currentProject,
      backendSource
    });
    if (!lockToken) {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(reason);
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.success,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.noLockToken,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: true
      };
    }

    const closePayload = resolveBackendSessionPayloadFromRuntimeProject({
      currentProject,
      backendSource
    });
    if (!closePayload) {
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.malformed,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.noClosePayload,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: false
      };
    }

    const closeResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      backendCommands.closeProject,
      closePayload
    );
    if (closeResult?.ok) {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(reason);
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.success,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.released,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: true
      };
    }

    const errorCode = String(
      closeResult?.errorCode
      || closeResult?.error?.code
      || ''
    ).trim();
    if (errorCode === backendErrorCodes.activeProcessBusy) {
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.blocked,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.blockedActiveProcessBusy,
          errorCode,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: false
      };
    }
    if (errorCode === backendErrorCodes.lostProjectLock) {
      return {
        ...createLifecycleOutcome({
          status: lifecycleStatuses.blocked,
          state: backendLockReleaseStates.blockedLostProjectLock,
          errorCode,
          reason
        }),
        canContinue: false
      };
    }

    return {
      ...createLifecycleOutcome({
        status: lifecycleStatuses.failed,
        state: backendLockReleaseStates.blockedFailure,
        errorCode,
        reason
      }),
      canContinue: false
    };
  }

  async function sendBackendHeartbeat() {
    if (backendHeartbeatInFlight) {
      return;
    }

    const projectManager = getProjectManagerOrNull();
    const currentProject = projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null;
    const heartbeatPayload = resolveBackendSessionPayloadFromRuntimeProject({
      currentProject,
      backendSource
    });

    if (!heartbeatPayload) {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(backendHeartbeatStopReasonSwitch);
      return;
    }

    backendHeartbeatInFlight = true;
    try {
      const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
        backendCommands.projectHeartbeat,
        heartbeatPayload
      );

      const hasLockToken = Boolean(resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject({
        currentProject,
        backendSource
      }));
      if (!commandResult?.ok && hasLockToken) {
        loggerWarn(
          loggerSource,
          backendHeartbeatFailedText
        );
      }
    } finally {
      backendHeartbeatInFlight = false;
    }
  }

  function startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(_reason = '') {
    stopBackendHeartbeat();

    const projectManager = getProjectManagerOrNull();
    const currentProject = projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null;
    const heartbeatPayload = resolveBackendSessionPayloadFromRuntimeProject({
      currentProject,
      backendSource
    });

    if (!heartbeatPayload) {
      return;
    }

    backendHeartbeatTimerId = setIntervalFn(() => {
      void sendBackendHeartbeat();
    }, backendHeartbeatIntervalMs);
  }

  return {
    executeBackendCommand,
    releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
    resolveBackendLockErrorCode,
    handleLostBackendProjectLock,
    stopBackendHeartbeat,
    sendBackendHeartbeat,
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/backendProjectExportFlow.js
==================================================

import { buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields } from './runtimeClientContract.js';

export async function runBackendProjectExport({
  project,
  exportCommandId,
  executeBackendCommand,
  downloadBinary,
  saveBinaryFileAsDialog,
  dialogs,
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  downloadFailedText,
  backendCommandFailedText
}) {
  const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
  if (!projectId) {
    return false;
  }

  const commandOutcome = await executeBackendCommand(exportCommandId, { projectId });
  const commandFailedWarningText = String(
    backendCommandFailedText
    || downloadFailedText
    || ''
  ).trim();

  if (commandOutcome?.ok !== true) {
    if (commandFailedWarningText) {
      loggerWarn(
        loggerSource,
        commandFailedWarningText,
        {
          projectId,
          ...buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields(commandOutcome)
        }
      );
    }
    return false;
  }

  const result = commandOutcome?.result;
  const downloadUrl = String(result?.downloadUrl || '').trim();
  if (!downloadUrl) {
    if (commandFailedWarningText) {
      loggerWarn(
        loggerSource,
        commandFailedWarningText,
        {
          projectId,
          ...buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields({
            error: {
              message: commandFailedWarningText,
              details: {
                result: result ?? null
              }
            }
          })
        }
      );
    }
    return false;
  }

  try {
    const bytes = Array.from(await downloadBinary(downloadUrl));
    const defaultFileName = String(result?.fileName || `${project?.slug || projectId}.zip`).trim();
    await saveBinaryFileAsDialog({
      title: dialogs.exportProjectArchiveTitle,
      buttonLabel: dialogs.exportButtonLabel,
      defaultPath: defaultFileName,
      filters: [
        {
          name: dialogs.zipFilterName,
          extensions: dialogs.zipFilterExtensions
        }
      ],
      bytes
    });
  } catch (error) {
    loggerWarn(
      loggerSource,
      downloadFailedText,
      { message: error?.message || String(error), projectId }
    );
  }

  return true;
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/browserShellAdapter.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { createRendererShellContract } from './shellContract.js';

const FALLBACK_BINARY_MIME_TYPE = 'application/octet-stream';
const BROWSER_CLOSE_EVENT = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserClose.eventName;
const BROWSER_CLOSE_NATIVE_DIALOG_RETURN_VALUE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.browserClose.nativeDialogReturnValue;
const FILE_DIALOG_TYPE = 'file';
const FILE_DIALOG_ACCEPT = '.zip';
const FILE_DIALOG_CHANGE_EVENT = 'change';
const FILE_DIALOG_CANCEL_EVENT = 'cancel';
const WINDOW_FOCUS_EVENT = 'focus';

function toUint8Array(bytes) {
  if (bytes instanceof Uint8Array) {
    return bytes;
  }
  if (Array.isArray(bytes)) {
    return Uint8Array.from(bytes);
  }
  return new Uint8Array(0);
}

function resolveDownloadFileName(defaultPath) {
  const normalized = String(defaultPath || '').trim();
  return normalized || 'download.bin';
}

function createImportDialogRequest({ globalObject }) {
  const documentRef = globalObject?.document;
  if (!documentRef?.createElement) {
    return Promise.resolve(null);
  }

  const input = documentRef.createElement('input');
  if (!input) {
    return Promise.resolve(null);
  }
  input.type = FILE_DIALOG_TYPE;
  input.accept = FILE_DIALOG_ACCEPT;
  if (input.style && typeof input.style === 'object') {
    input.style.display = 'none';
  }

  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    let settled = false;

    const cleanup = () => {
      input.removeEventListener?.(FILE_DIALOG_CHANGE_EVENT, handleChange);
      input.removeEventListener?.(FILE_DIALOG_CANCEL_EVENT, handleCancel);
      globalObject?.removeEventListener?.(WINDOW_FOCUS_EVENT, handleWindowFocus);
      input.remove?.();
    };

    const finish = (value) => {
      if (settled) {
        return;
      }
      settled = true;
      cleanup();
      resolve(value);
    };

    const handleCancel = () => {
      finish(null);
    };

    const handleWindowFocus = () => {
      queueMicrotask(() => {
        if (settled) {
          return;
        }
        const hasFile = Boolean(input.files?.[0]);
        if (!hasFile) {
          finish(null);
        }
      });
    };

    const handleChange = async () => {
      const selectedFile = input.files?.[0] || null;
      if (!selectedFile) {
        finish(null);
        return;
      }

      try {
        const bytes = new Uint8Array(await selectedFile.arrayBuffer());
        finish({
          fileName: String(selectedFile.name || '').trim(),
          filePath: String(selectedFile.name || '').trim(),
          bytes
        });
      } catch (_error) {
        finish(null);
      }
    };

    input.addEventListener(FILE_DIALOG_CHANGE_EVENT, handleChange);
    input.addEventListener(FILE_DIALOG_CANCEL_EVENT, handleCancel);
    globalObject?.addEventListener?.(WINDOW_FOCUS_EVENT, handleWindowFocus);
    documentRef.body?.appendChild?.(input);

    if (typeof input.click === 'function') {
      input.click();
      return;
    }

    finish(null);
  });
}

function createBinarySaveRequest({ globalObject, options }) {
  const documentRef = globalObject?.document;
  const urlApi = globalObject?.URL;
  const BlobCtor = globalObject?.Blob;
  if (!documentRef?.createElement || typeof urlApi?.createObjectURL !== 'function' || typeof BlobCtor !== 'function') {
    return Promise.resolve({ saved: false, filePath: null });
  }

  const bytes = toUint8Array(options?.bytes);
  const filePath = resolveDownloadFileName(options?.defaultPath);
  const blob = new BlobCtor([bytes], { type: options?.mimeType || FALLBACK_BINARY_MIME_TYPE });
  const objectUrl = urlApi.createObjectURL(blob);

  try {
    const link = documentRef.createElement('a');
    if (!link) {
      return Promise.resolve({ saved: false, filePath: null });
    }
    link.href = objectUrl;
    link.download = filePath;
    link.rel = 'noopener';
    link.style.display = 'none';

    if (documentRef.body?.appendChild) {
      documentRef.body.appendChild(link);
    }
    link.click?.();
    link.remove?.();

    return Promise.resolve({
      saved: true,
      filePath
    });
  } finally {
    urlApi.revokeObjectURL?.(objectUrl);
  }
}

export function createBrowserShellAdapter({ globalObject = globalThis } = {}) {
  let pendingCloseEvent = null;

  return createRendererShellContract({
    adapterId: APP_CONFIG.platform.runtime.shell.adapterId,
    requestProjectImportArchive: () => createImportDialogRequest({ globalObject }),
    requestBinarySaveAs: (options) => createBinarySaveRequest({ globalObject, options }),
    requestApplicationExit: async () => {
      globalObject?.close?.();
      return true;
    },
    approveCloseIntent: async () => {
      pendingCloseEvent = null;
      return true;
    },
    cancelCloseIntent: async () => {
      const closeEvent = pendingCloseEvent;
      pendingCloseEvent = null;

      if (closeEvent && typeof closeEvent.preventDefault === 'function') {
        closeEvent.preventDefault();
      }
      if (closeEvent && 'returnValue' in closeEvent) {
        closeEvent.returnValue = BROWSER_CLOSE_NATIVE_DIALOG_RETURN_VALUE;
      }
      return true;
    },
    subscribeToCloseIntent: (listener) => {
      if (typeof globalObject?.addEventListener !== 'function') {
        return () => {};
      }

      const handler = (event) => {
        pendingCloseEvent = event || null;
        listener?.(event);
      };
      globalObject.addEventListener(BROWSER_CLOSE_EVENT, handler);
      return () => {
        pendingCloseEvent = null;
        globalObject?.removeEventListener?.(BROWSER_CLOSE_EVENT, handler);
      };
    }
  });
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { createBrowserShellAdapter } from './browserShellAdapter.js';

export function createShellAdapter({
  adapterId = APP_CONFIG.platform.runtime.shell.adapterId,
  globalObject = globalThis
} = {}) {
  if (adapterId === APP_CONFIG.platform.runtime.shell.adapterId) {
    return createBrowserShellAdapter({ globalObject });
  }

  throw new Error(`Unsupported shell adapter: ${String(adapterId || '')}`);
}

import YAML from 'yaml';

export function createDocumentLoader({ fileSystem }) {
  // YAML file IO helper used by compatibility/file adapters only.
  // Backend catalog project lifecycle does not depend on this helper.
  return {
    async loadYaml(targetPath) {
      const text = await fileSystem.readText(targetPath);
      return {
        rawText: text,
        data: YAML.parse(text)
      };
    },

    async saveYaml(targetPath, value) {
      const text = YAML.stringify(value);
      await fileSystem.writeText(targetPath, text);
      return text;
    }
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';

const UUID_REGEX = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[1-8][0-9a-f]{3}-[89ab][0-9a-f]{3}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i;

function fallbackUuidV4() {
  return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, (token) => {
    const random = Math.floor(Math.random() * 16);
    const value = token === 'x' ? random : ((random & 0x3) | 0x8);
    return value.toString(16);
  });
}

export function createDocumentGuid() {
  if (globalThis.crypto?.randomUUID) {
    return globalThis.crypto.randomUUID();
  }

  return fallbackUuidV4();
}

export function normalizeDocumentName(name) {
  return String(name ?? '').trim();
}

export function getDocumentName(documentRecord) {
  const componentName = normalizeDocumentName(documentRecord?.document?.component?.name || '');
  if (componentName) {
    return componentName;
  }

  const scenarioName = normalizeDocumentName(documentRecord?.document?.scenario?.name || '');
  if (scenarioName) {
    return scenarioName;
  }

  const screenName = normalizeDocumentName(documentRecord?.document?.screen?.name || '');
  if (screenName) {
    return screenName;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.kind === METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind) {
    return '';
  }

  return normalizeDocumentName(documentRecord?.document?.name || '');
}

function getDocumentIdentityContainer(documentRecord) {
  if (documentRecord?.document?.component) {
    return documentRecord.document.component;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.scenario) {
    return documentRecord.document.scenario;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.screen) {
    return documentRecord.document.screen;
  }

  return documentRecord?.document || null;
}

export function getDocumentId(documentRecord) {
  const value = getDocumentIdentityContainer(documentRecord)?.id;
  return typeof value === 'string' ? value.trim() : '';
}

export function isValidDocumentGuid(value) {
  return UUID_REGEX.test(String(value || '').trim());
}

export function ensureDocumentId(documentRecord, { force = false } = {}) {
  const container = getDocumentIdentityContainer(documentRecord);

  if (!container) {
    return '';
  }

  const currentId = getDocumentId(documentRecord);

  if (!force && isValidDocumentGuid(currentId)) {
    return currentId;
  }

  const nextId = createDocumentGuid();
  container.id = nextId;
  return nextId;
}

export function getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord) {
  const documentId = ensureDocumentId(documentRecord);
  return documentId ? `${APP_CONFIG.project.identity.documentPrefix}${documentId}` : '';
}

export function setDocumentName(documentRecord, nextName) {
  const value = normalizeDocumentName(nextName);

  if (documentRecord?.document?.component) {
    documentRecord.document.component.name = value;
    return value;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.scenario) {
    documentRecord.document.scenario.name = value;
    return value;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.screen) {
    documentRecord.document.screen.name = value;
    return value;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document?.kind === METAGEN_CONFIG.documentKind) {
    return value;
  }

  if (documentRecord?.document) {
    documentRecord.document.name = value;
  }

  return value;
}

function isObjectRecord(value) {
  return Boolean(value) && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value);
}

export function getMetaGenNameSurfaceStatus(documentRecord) {
  if (documentRecord?.moduleId !== APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen) {
    return 'not-metagen-module';
  }

  if (!isObjectRecord(documentRecord?.document?.component)) {
    return 'legacy-missing-component';
  }

  return 'canonical-component';
}

export function getDocumentLabel(documentRecord) {
  return getDocumentName(documentRecord) || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;
}

export function isUnsavedDocumentPath(targetPath) {
  return String(targetPath || '').startsWith(APP_CONFIG.project.unsavedDocumentPathPrefix);
}

FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/documentSnapshot.js
==================================================

function stableSortObject(value) {
  if (Array.isArray(value)) {
    return value.map((entry) => stableSortObject(entry));
  }

  if (value && typeof value === 'object') {
    const entries = Object.entries(value)
      .filter(([, nested]) => nested !== undefined)
      .sort(([left], [right]) => left.localeCompare(right));

    return entries.reduce((accumulator, [key, nested]) => {
      accumulator[key] = stableSortObject(nested);
      return accumulator;
    }, {});
  }

  return value;
}

export function normalizeDocumentSnapshot(documentRecord) {
  return stableSortObject({
    moduleId: documentRecord?.moduleId || '',
    document: documentRecord?.document || null
  });
}

export function areDocumentSnapshotsSemanticallyEqual(leftRecord, rightRecord) {
  return JSON.stringify(normalizeDocumentSnapshot(leftRecord)) === JSON.stringify(normalizeDocumentSnapshot(rightRecord));
}

export function slugifyDocumentName(name) {
  return String(name ?? '')
    .trim()
    .replace(/\s+/g, '_')
    .replace(/[^\w\-А-Яа-яЁё]/g, '')
    .toLowerCase();
}

==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/processExecutionOrchestrator.js
==================================================

import { createProcessPollingLifecycle } from './processPollingLifecycle.js';
import { resolveRuntimeCommandError } from './runtimeClientContract.js';

function cloneProcessSnapshot(snapshot) {
  return {
    process: snapshot.process ? { ...snapshot.process } : null,
    commandFailure: snapshot.commandFailure ? { ...snapshot.commandFailure } : null,
    outputChunks: snapshot.outputChunks.map((chunk) => ({ ...chunk })),
    afterChunkId: snapshot.afterChunkId
  };
}

export function createProcessExecutionOrchestrator({
  executeBackendCommand,
  commandIds,
  terminalStatuses,
  pollingIntervalMs,
  onUpdate
}) {
  if (typeof executeBackendCommand !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Process execution orchestrator requires executeBackendCommand()');
  }

  const terminalStatusSet = new Set(Array.isArray(terminalStatuses) ? terminalStatuses : []);
  const notify = typeof onUpdate === 'function' ? onUpdate : () => {};

  const state = {
    process: null,
    commandFailure: null,
    outputChunks: [],
    afterChunkId: 0,
    hasSeenTerminal: false
  };

  function normalizeProcessCommandFailure(commandOutcomeOrError, command, fallbackMessage = '') {
    const commandLabel = String(command || '').trim();
    const normalizedFallbackMessage = String(fallbackMessage || '').trim() || commandLabel;
    const error = resolveRuntimeCommandError(commandOutcomeOrError, {
      fallbackMessage: normalizedFallbackMessage
    });

    if (error) {
      return error;
    }

    return {
      code: '',
      message: normalizedFallbackMessage
    };
  }

  function normalizeCommandOutcome(commandOutcome, command = '') {
    if (commandOutcome && typeof commandOutcome === 'object' && typeof commandOutcome.ok === 'boolean') {
      const error = commandOutcome.ok
        ? null
        : normalizeProcessCommandFailure(commandOutcome, command);
      return {
        ok: commandOutcome.ok,
        result: commandOutcome.ok && commandOutcome.result && typeof commandOutcome.result === 'object'
          ? commandOutcome.result
          : null,
        error
      };
    }

    return {
      ok: false,
      result: null,
      error: normalizeProcessCommandFailure(commandOutcome, command)
    };
  }

  async function executeProcessCommand(command, payload = {}) {
    try {
      const commandOutcome = await executeBackendCommand(command, payload);
      return normalizeCommandOutcome(commandOutcome, command);
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        ok: false,
        result: null,
        error: normalizeProcessCommandFailure(
          error,
          command,
          String(error?.message || String(error)).trim()
        )
      };
    }
  }

  function updateState(nextProcess = state.process) {
    if (nextProcess) {
      state.process = { ...nextProcess };
      if (terminalStatusSet.has(String(nextProcess.status || '').trim())) {
        state.hasSeenTerminal = true;
      }
    } else if (!state.hasSeenTerminal) {
      state.process = null;
    }
    notify(cloneProcessSnapshot(state));
  }

  function appendChunks(chunks) {
    if (!Array.isArray(chunks) || chunks.length === 0) {
      return 0;
    }

    for (const chunk of chunks) {
      state.outputChunks.push(chunk);
      const chunkId = Number(chunk?.chunkId || 0);
      if (chunkId > state.afterChunkId) {
        state.afterChunkId = chunkId;
      }
    }
    return chunks.length;
  }

  async function pollTick() {
    const stateOutcome = await executeProcessCommand(commandIds.processGetState, {});
    const activeProcess = stateOutcome.ok
      ? (stateOutcome.result?.process || null)
      : null;

    const outputOutcome = await executeProcessCommand(
      commandIds.processReadOutput,
      { afterChunkId: state.afterChunkId }
    );
    const latestProcess = outputOutcome.ok
      ? (outputOutcome.result?.process || null)
      : null;
    const readChunks = outputOutcome.ok && Array.isArray(outputOutcome.result?.chunks)
      ? outputOutcome.result.chunks
      : [];
    const chunkCount = appendChunks(readChunks);

    const effectiveProcess = latestProcess || activeProcess || state.process;
    if (effectiveProcess) {
      state.commandFailure = null;
    }
    updateState(effectiveProcess);

    if (!activeProcess && !latestProcess && !state.hasSeenTerminal) {
      return false;
    }

    if (state.hasSeenTerminal && !activeProcess && chunkCount === 0) {
      return false;
    }

    return true;
  }

  const pollingLifecycle = createProcessPollingLifecycle({
    intervalMs: pollingIntervalMs,
    tick: pollTick
  });

  function clearSnapshot() {
    pollingLifecycle.stop();
    state.process = null;
    state.commandFailure = null;
    state.outputChunks = [];
    state.afterChunkId = 0;
    state.hasSeenTerminal = false;
    notify(cloneProcessSnapshot(state));
  }

  async function syncActiveProcess() {
    const commandOutcome = await executeProcessCommand(commandIds.processGetState, {});
    const process = commandOutcome.ok ? (commandOutcome.result?.process || null) : null;
    if (process) {
      state.commandFailure = null;
    }
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  async function launchGenerate(payload = {}) {
    clearSnapshot();

    const commandOutcome = await executeProcessCommand(commandIds.metagenGenerate, payload);
    const process = commandOutcome.ok ? (commandOutcome.result?.process || null) : null;
    if (!commandOutcome.ok) {
      const errorDetails = commandOutcome.error?.details ?? commandOutcome.error?.errorDetails ?? null;
      state.commandFailure = {
        command: String(commandIds.metagenGenerate || '').trim(),
        code: String(commandOutcome.error?.code || '').trim(),
        message: String(commandOutcome.error?.message || '').trim(),
        ...(errorDetails === null ? {} : { details: errorDetails, errorDetails })
      };
    } else if (!process) {
      const command = String(commandIds.metagenGenerate || '').trim();
      const details = {
        result: commandOutcome.result ?? null
      };
      state.commandFailure = {
        command,
        code: '',
        message: command,
        details,
        errorDetails: details
      };
    } else {
      state.commandFailure = null;
    }
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  async function stopProcess() {
    const commandOutcome = await executeProcessCommand(commandIds.processStop, {});
    const process = commandOutcome.ok ? (commandOutcome.result?.process || null) : null;
    if (process) {
      state.commandFailure = null;
    }
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  function dispose() {
    pollingLifecycle.dispose();
  }

  return {
    syncActiveProcess,
    launchGenerate,
    stopProcess,
    clearSnapshot,
    dispose,
    isPollingActive: () => pollingLifecycle.isActive(),
    getSnapshot: () => cloneProcessSnapshot(state)
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/processPollingLifecycle.js
==================================================

export function createProcessPollingLifecycle({
  intervalMs,
  tick,
  setIntervalFn = setInterval,
  clearIntervalFn = clearInterval
}) {
  if (typeof tick !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Process polling lifecycle requires tick()');
  }

  let timerId = null;
  let tickInFlight = false;

  async function runTickOnce() {
    if (tickInFlight) {
      return true;
    }

    tickInFlight = true;
    try {
      const shouldContinue = await tick();
      if (shouldContinue === false) {
        stop();
        return false;
      }
      return true;
    } finally {
      tickInFlight = false;
    }
  }

  function start() {
    if (timerId !== null) {
      return false;
    }

    timerId = setIntervalFn(() => {
      void runTickOnce();
    }, intervalMs);
    return true;
  }

  function stop() {
    if (timerId === null) {
      return false;
    }

    clearIntervalFn(timerId);
    timerId = null;
    return true;
  }

  function dispose() {
    stop();
  }

  return {
    start,
    stop,
    dispose,
    runTickOnce,
    isActive: () => timerId !== null,
    isTickInFlight: () => tickInFlight
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/runtimeClient.js
==================================================

import { normalizeImportResponse, normalizeRuntimeRequest, normalizeRuntimeResponse } from './runtimeClientContract.js';

export function createRuntimeClient({ adapter }) {
  if (!adapter || typeof adapter.execute !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with execute(request) is required');
  }

  async function execute(request) {
    const normalizedRequest = normalizeRuntimeRequest(request);
    const response = await adapter.execute(normalizedRequest);
    return normalizeRuntimeResponse(response, normalizedRequest.requestId);
  }

  async function downloadBinary(relativePath) {
    if (typeof adapter.downloadBinary !== 'function') {
      throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with downloadBinary(relativePath) is required');
    }
    return adapter.downloadBinary(relativePath);
  }

  async function importProjectArchive(payload) {
    if (typeof adapter.importProjectArchive !== 'function') {
      throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with importProjectArchive(payload) is required');
    }

    const response = await adapter.importProjectArchive(payload);
    return normalizeImportResponse(response);
  }

  return {
    execute,
    downloadBinary,
    importProjectArchive
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/runtimeClientContract.js
==================================================

const REQUIRED_STRING_FIELDS = ['requestId', 'module', 'command'];
const LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES = Object.freeze({
  success: 'success',
  cancelled: 'cancelled',
  blocked: 'blocked',
  failed: 'failed',
  malformed: 'malformed'
});

function isPlainObject(value) {
  return Boolean(value) && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value);
}

function hasOwnField(source, field) {
  return Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(source, field);
}

function normalizeRuntimeError(error, label) {
  if (!isPlainObject(error)) {
    throw new Error(`${label} must include error object`);
  }

  const code = String(error.code || '').trim();
  const message = String(error.message || '').trim();
  if (!code) {
    throw new Error(`${label} error field is required: code`);
  }
  if (!message) {
    throw new Error(`${label} error field is required: message`);
  }

  const details = error.details ?? error.errorDetails ?? null;
  return {
    ...error,
    code,
    message,
    ...(details === null ? {} : { details, errorDetails: details })
  };
}

function normalizeRuntimeErrorCode(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim();
}

function normalizeRuntimeErrorMessage(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim();
}

function normalizeLifecycleOutcomeStatus(status) {
  const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
  return Object.values(LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES).includes(normalizedStatus)
    ? normalizedStatus
    : '';
}

export function resolveLifecycleOutcomeStatuses() {
  return LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES;
}

export function createLifecycleOutcome({
  status = LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES.malformed,
  state = '',
  reason = '',
  errorCode = '',
  details = null
} = {}) {
  const normalizedStatus = normalizeLifecycleOutcomeStatus(status) || LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES.malformed;
  const normalizedState = String(state || '').trim();
  const normalizedReason = String(reason || '').trim();
  const normalizedErrorCode = String(errorCode || '').trim();
  const normalizedDetails = details ?? null;

  return {
    status: normalizedStatus,
    state: normalizedState,
    reason: normalizedReason,
    errorCode: normalizedErrorCode,
    details: normalizedDetails
  };
}

export function normalizeLifecycleOutcome(input, {
  fallbackStatus = LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES.malformed,
  truthyStatus = LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES.success,
  falsyStatus = LIFECYCLE_OUTCOME_STATUSES.failed
} = {}) {
  const fallback = createLifecycleOutcome({ status: fallbackStatus });

  if (input && typeof input === 'object' && !Array.isArray(input)) {
    const status = normalizeLifecycleOutcomeStatus(input.status);
    if (!status) {
      return fallback;
    }

    return createLifecycleOutcome({
      status,
      state: input.state,
      reason: input.reason,
      errorCode: input.errorCode,
      details: input.details
    });
  }

  if (input === true) {
    return createLifecycleOutcome({ status: truthyStatus });
  }

  if (input === false) {
    return createLifecycleOutcome({ status: falsyStatus });
  }

  return fallback;
}

export function resolveRuntimeCommandError(commandOutcomeOrError, {
  fallbackCode = '',
  fallbackMessage = '',
  fallbackDetails = null
} = {}) {
  const source = isPlainObject(commandOutcomeOrError) ? commandOutcomeOrError : {};
  const nestedError = isPlainObject(source.error) ? source.error : null;
  const error = nestedError || source;

  const code = normalizeRuntimeErrorCode(
    error.code
    ?? source.errorCode
    ?? fallbackCode
  );
  const message = normalizeRuntimeErrorMessage(
    error.message
    ?? source.errorMessage
    ?? fallbackMessage
  );
  const details = error.details
    ?? error.errorDetails
    ?? source.errorDetails
    ?? source.details
    ?? fallbackDetails
    ?? null;

  if (!code && !message && details === null) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    ...error,
    code,
    message,
    ...(details === null ? {} : { details, errorDetails: details })
  };
}

export function buildRuntimeCommandFailureFields(commandOutcomeOrError) {
  const error = resolveRuntimeCommandError(commandOutcomeOrError);
  const errorCode = String(error?.code || '').trim();
  const errorMessage = String(error?.message || '').trim();
  const errorDetails = error?.details ?? error?.errorDetails ?? null;

  return {
    ...(errorCode ? { errorCode } : {}),
    ...(errorMessage ? { errorMessage } : {}),
    ...(errorDetails === null ? {} : { errorDetails, details: errorDetails })
  };
}

function resolveRuntimeProjectBackendSource(currentProject, backendSource) {
  if (!currentProject || currentProject.source !== backendSource) {
    return null;
  }
  return currentProject;
}

export function resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource,
  includeBackendEntityId = false
} = {}) {
  const backendProjectRuntime = resolveRuntimeProjectBackendSource(currentProject, backendSource);
  if (!backendProjectRuntime) {
    return '';
  }

  return String(
    (includeBackendEntityId ? backendProjectRuntime.backendProject?.id : '')
    || backendProjectRuntime.backendProject?.projectId
    || backendProjectRuntime.project?.id
    || ''
  ).trim();
}

export function resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource
} = {}) {
  const backendProjectRuntime = resolveRuntimeProjectBackendSource(currentProject, backendSource);
  if (!backendProjectRuntime) {
    return '';
  }

  return String(backendProjectRuntime.backendProject?.lockToken || '').trim();
}

export function resolveBackendSessionPayloadFromRuntimeProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource
} = {}) {
  const projectId = resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });
  const lockToken = resolveBackendProjectLockTokenFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });

  if (!projectId || !lockToken) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    projectId,
    lockToken
  };
}

export function resolveBackendProjectForExportFromRuntimeProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource
} = {}) {
  const backendProjectRuntime = resolveRuntimeProjectBackendSource(currentProject, backendSource);
  if (!backendProjectRuntime) {
    return null;
  }

  const projectId = resolveBackendProjectIdFromRuntimeProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource,
    includeBackendEntityId: true
  });
  if (!projectId) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    ...(isPlainObject(backendProjectRuntime.backendProject) ? backendProjectRuntime.backendProject : {}),
    id: projectId
  };
}

export function resolveBackendProjectDisplayFieldsFromRuntimeProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource,
  fallbackName = ''
} = {}) {
  const backendProjectRuntime = resolveRuntimeProjectBackendSource(currentProject, backendSource);
  if (!backendProjectRuntime) {
    return null;
  }

  const backendProject = isPlainObject(backendProjectRuntime.backendProject)
    ? backendProjectRuntime.backendProject
    : {};
  const project = isPlainObject(backendProjectRuntime.project)
    ? backendProjectRuntime.project
    : {};
  const resolvedFallbackName = String(fallbackName || '').trim();
  const hasComment = hasOwnField(backendProject, 'comment') || hasOwnField(project, 'comment');

  return {
    name: String(
      backendProject.name
      || project.name
      || resolvedFallbackName
    ).trim() || resolvedFallbackName,
    hasComment,
    comment: hasComment
      ? String(backendProject.comment ?? project.comment ?? '').trim()
      : ''
  };
}

export function normalizeRuntimeRequest(input) {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command request must be an object');
  }

  for (const field of REQUIRED_STRING_FIELDS) {
    const value = String(input[field] || '').trim();
    if (!value) {
      throw new Error(`Runtime command request field is required: ${field}`);
    }
  }

  const payload = input.payload;

  return {
    requestId: String(input.requestId).trim(),
    module: String(input.module).trim(),
    command: String(input.command).trim(),
    payload: isPlainObject(payload) ? payload : {}
  };
}

export function normalizeRuntimeResponse(input, fallbackRequestId = '') {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response must be an object');
  }

  const requestId = String(input.requestId || fallbackRequestId || '').trim();
  if (!requestId) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response field is required: requestId');
  }

  if (input.ok !== true && input.ok !== false) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response field is required: ok(boolean)');
  }

  const ok = input.ok === true;

  if (ok) {
    if (input.error != null) {
      throw new Error('Runtime command response cannot include error when ok=true');
    }
    if (!hasOwnField(input, 'result')) {
      throw new Error('Runtime command response must include result when ok=true');
    }
    if (!isPlainObject(input.result)) {
      throw new Error('Runtime command response result must be an object when ok=true');
    }

    return {
      requestId,
      ok: true,
      result: input.result,
      error: null
    };
  }

  if (input.error == null) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response must include error when ok=false');
  }

  if (input.result != null) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response cannot include result when ok=false');
  }

  return {
    requestId,
    ok: false,
    result: null,
    error: normalizeRuntimeError(input.error, 'Runtime command response')
  };
}

export function normalizeImportResponse(input) {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Import response must be an object');
  }

  if (input.ok !== true && input.ok !== false) {
    throw new Error('Import response field is required: ok(boolean)');
  }

  const ok = input.ok === true;

  if (ok) {
    if (input.error != null) {
      throw new Error('Import response cannot include error when ok=true');
    }
    if (!hasOwnField(input, 'result')) {
      throw new Error('Import response must include result when ok=true');
    }
    if (!isPlainObject(input.result)) {
      throw new Error('Import response result must be an object when ok=true');
    }

    return {
      ok: true,
      result: input.result,
      error: null
    };
  }

  if (input.error == null) {
    throw new Error('Import response must include error when ok=false');
  }

  if (input.result != null) {
    throw new Error('Import response cannot include result when ok=false');
  }

  return {
    ok: false,
    result: null,
    error: normalizeRuntimeError(input.error, 'Import response')
  };
}

function assertShellOperation(operation, operationName) {
  if (typeof operation !== 'function') {
    throw new Error(`Shell operation "${operationName}" must be a function`);
  }
}

function toUnsubscribe(handle) {
  return typeof handle === 'function' ? handle : () => {};
}

export function createRendererShellContract({
  adapterId = '',
  requestProjectImportArchive,
  requestBinarySaveAs,
  requestApplicationExit,
  approveCloseIntent,
  cancelCloseIntent,
  subscribeToCloseIntent
}) {
  assertShellOperation(requestProjectImportArchive, 'requestProjectImportArchive');
  assertShellOperation(requestBinarySaveAs, 'requestBinarySaveAs');
  assertShellOperation(requestApplicationExit, 'requestApplicationExit');
  assertShellOperation(approveCloseIntent, 'approveCloseIntent');
  assertShellOperation(cancelCloseIntent, 'cancelCloseIntent');
  assertShellOperation(subscribeToCloseIntent, 'subscribeToCloseIntent');

  return Object.freeze({
    adapterId: String(adapterId || '').trim(),
    requestProjectImportArchive,
    requestBinarySaveAs,
    requestApplicationExit,
    approveCloseIntent,
    cancelCloseIntent,
    subscribeToCloseIntent: (listener) => toUnsubscribe(subscribeToCloseIntent(listener))
  });
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

export function applyStaticText() {
  const titleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.titleSelector);
  const topPanelTitleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.topPanelTitleSelector);
  const paramsUndoButton = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsUndoButtonSelector);
  const paramsRedoButton = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsRedoButtonSelector);
  const logsHeaderNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.logsPanelHeaderSelector);

  if (titleNode) {
    titleNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.title;
  }

  if (topPanelTitleNode) {
    topPanelTitleNode.innerHTML = '';

    const textNode = document.createElement('span');
    textNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.topPanelTitleText);
    textNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.topPanelTitle;
    topPanelTitleNode.appendChild(textNode);
  }

  if (logsHeaderNode) {
    logsHeaderNode.innerHTML = '';

    const iconHost = document.createElement('span');
    iconHost.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.iconHost);
    const iconImage = document.createElement('img');
    iconImage.src = APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.logs;
    iconImage.alt = '';
    iconImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
    iconImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
    iconImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
    iconImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
    iconImage.decoding = 'async';
    iconImage.loading = 'eager';
    iconImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    iconHost.appendChild(iconImage);
    logsHeaderNode.appendChild(iconHost);

    const textNode = document.createElement('span');
    textNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.panelHeaderText);
    textNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.logs;
    logsHeaderNode.appendChild(textNode);
  }

  if (paramsUndoButton) {
    paramsUndoButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.paramsUndoButton;
  }

  if (paramsRedoButton) {
    paramsRedoButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.paramsRedoButton;
  }
}
