import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';
import { METALAB_CONFIG } from '../modules/metalab/metalabConfig.js';
import { METAVIEW_CONFIG } from '../modules/metaview/metaviewConfig.js';
import {
  TREE_NODE_TYPES,
  buildProjectTreeNodes,
  createTreeBehaviorConfig,
  createTreeInteractionController,
  getNodeActions,
  getNodeRowClassNames
} from './projectTree/treeAdapter.js';

const TREE_CLASSNAMES = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames;

function normalizeClassNames(classNames = []) {
  const normalizedClassNames = Array.isArray(classNames) ? classNames : [classNames];

  return normalizedClassNames.filter(Boolean).map((className) => {
    if (/\s/.test(className)) {
      throw new TypeError(
        `Invalid class token "${className}". Pass class names as separate tokens.`
      );
    }

    return className;
  });
}

function createElement(tagName, classNames = []) {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);
  normalizeClassNames(classNames).forEach((className) => node.classList.add(className));
  return node;
}

function resolveNodeIconAssetPath(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project) {
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.project;
  }

  if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.moduleById[nodeData.moduleId];
  }

  return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.documentById[nodeData.moduleId];
}

export function createProjectTree({
  logger,
  projectManager,
  tabs,
  onCreateComponentRequest,
  onDeleteComponentRequest
}) {
  const treeRoot = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectTreeId);
  const projectPanelTitleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectPanelTitleSelector);

  const moduleSections = [
    {
      moduleId: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => projectManager.getNextMetaGenDefaultName()
    },
    {
      moduleId: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => METALAB_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName
    },
    {
      moduleId: METAVIEW_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METAVIEW_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => METAVIEW_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName
    }
  ];

  const behaviorConfig = createTreeBehaviorConfig();
  const treeSelectionState = {
    selectedNodeId: null
  };
  const moduleExpandState = new Map();

  function getProjectPanelTitle(project) {
    if (!project) {
      return '';
    }

    const projectName = String(project.project?.name || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled).trim() || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;
    return project.isDirty ? `${projectName} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.dirtyMarker}` : projectName;
  }

  function renderProjectPanelTitle(project) {
    if (!projectPanelTitleNode) {
      return;
    }

    if (!project) {
      projectPanelTitleNode.innerHTML = '';
      return;
    }

    projectPanelTitleNode.innerHTML = '';

    const textNode = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.panelHeaderText]);
    textNode.textContent = getProjectPanelTitle(project);
    projectPanelTitleNode.appendChild(textNode);
  }

  function isModuleExpanded(moduleId) {
    if (!moduleExpandState.has(moduleId)) {
      moduleExpandState.set(moduleId, true);
    }

    return moduleExpandState.get(moduleId);
  }

  function toggleModuleExpanded(moduleId) {
    moduleExpandState.set(moduleId, !isModuleExpanded(moduleId));
  }

  async function startDocumentCreation(sectionConfig) {
    await tabs.startTemporaryDocumentCreation({
      moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
      defaultName: sectionConfig.getDefaultName(),
      onCommit: async ({ moduleId, confirmedName }) => {
        return projectManager.createDocument(moduleId, confirmedName);
      }
    });
  }

  const interactionController = createTreeInteractionController({
    tabs,
    onCreateComponentRequest: onCreateComponentRequest || (async (moduleId, nodeData) => {
      const sectionConfig = moduleSections.find((section) => section.moduleId === moduleId);

      if (!sectionConfig) {
        logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Не найден модуль для создания компонента', {
          moduleId,
          nodeData
        });
        return;
      }

      await startDocumentCreation(sectionConfig);
    }),
    onDeleteComponentRequest: onDeleteComponentRequest || (async (documentRecord, nodeData) => {
      const documentIdentity = nodeData?.id || documentRecord;
      await projectManager.deleteDocument(documentIdentity);
      await tabs.closeTab(documentIdentity, { reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.deleteDocument });
    })
  });

  function renderNodeRow(nodeData, rowClassNames = [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow]) {
    const row = createElement('div', [...rowClassNames, ...getNodeRowClassNames(nodeData)]);
    row.dataset.nodeType = nodeData.nodeType;
    row.dataset.nodeId = nodeData.id;

    const label = createElement('button', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeLabel]);
    label.type = 'button';

    const disclosureHost = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDisclosure]);
    if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
      const disclosureIconAssetPath = isModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId)
        ? APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.disclosure.expanded
        : APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.disclosure.collapsed;
      const disclosureIconHost = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.iconHost, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeIcon]);
      const disclosureImage = document.createElement('img');
      disclosureImage.src = disclosureIconAssetPath;
      disclosureImage.alt = '';
      disclosureImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
      disclosureImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
      disclosureImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
      disclosureImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
      disclosureImage.decoding = 'async';
      disclosureImage.loading = 'eager';
      disclosureImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      disclosureIconHost.appendChild(disclosureImage);
      disclosureHost.appendChild(disclosureIconHost);
    } else {
      disclosureHost.classList.add(TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDisclosureSpacer);
    }

    label.appendChild(disclosureHost);
    const nodeIconHost = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.iconHost, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeIcon]);
    const nodeIconImage = document.createElement('img');
    nodeIconImage.src = resolveNodeIconAssetPath(nodeData);
    nodeIconImage.alt = '';
    nodeIconImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
    nodeIconImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon;
    nodeIconImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
    nodeIconImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon));
    nodeIconImage.decoding = 'async';
    nodeIconImage.loading = 'eager';
    nodeIconImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    nodeIconHost.appendChild(nodeIconImage);
    label.appendChild(nodeIconHost);

    const labelText = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeLabelText]);
    labelText.textContent = nodeData.label;
    label.appendChild(labelText);

    label.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      treeSelectionState.selectedNodeId = nodeData.id;

      if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
        toggleModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId);
        await render();
        return;
      }

      await interactionController.onNodePrimaryClick(nodeData);
      await render();
    });

    row.appendChild(label);

    const actions = getNodeActions(nodeData);

    if (actions.length > 0) {
      const actionsContainer = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActions]);

      for (const action of actions) {
        if (!action.visible) {
          continue;
        }

        const actionButton = createElement('button', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActionButton]);
        actionButton.type = 'button';
        actionButton.title = action.title;
        actionButton.setAttribute('aria-label', action.title);
        const actionIconHost = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.iconHost, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActionIcon]);
        const actionIconImage = document.createElement('img');
        actionIconImage.src = action.iconAssetPath;
        actionIconImage.alt = '';
        actionIconImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
        actionIconImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
        actionIconImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
        actionIconImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
        actionIconImage.decoding = 'async';
        actionIconImage.loading = 'eager';
        actionIconImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
        actionIconHost.appendChild(actionIconImage);
        actionButton.appendChild(actionIconHost);

        actionButton.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
          await interactionController.onNodeActionClick({
            actionId: action.id,
            nodeData,
            event
          });
        });

        actionsContainer.appendChild(actionButton);
      }

      row.appendChild(actionsContainer);
    }

    if (treeSelectionState.selectedNodeId === nodeData.id) {
      row.classList.add(TREE_CLASSNAMES.selected);
    }

    return row;
  }

  async function render() {
    const project = projectManager.getCurrentProject();

    treeRoot.innerHTML = '';
    renderProjectPanelTitle(project);

    if (!project) {
      return;
    }

    const treeNodes = buildProjectTreeNodes({
      project,
      moduleSections,
      getDocumentsByModule: (moduleId) => projectManager.getDocumentsByModule(moduleId)
    });

    const projectNode = treeNodes.find((node) => node.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project);

    if (projectNode) {
      const projectRootNode = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.projectNode]);
      projectRootNode.appendChild(renderNodeRow(projectNode, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow]));
      treeRoot.appendChild(projectRootNode);
    }

    for (const nodeData of treeNodes) {
      if (nodeData.nodeType !== TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
        continue;
      }

      const moduleBlock = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeModuleBlock]);
      moduleBlock.appendChild(
        renderNodeRow(nodeData, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeSectionHeader, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow])
      );

      const documentsContainer = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeModuleChildren]);

      if (isModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId)) {
        for (const documentNode of nodeData.children || []) {
          const item = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeItem]);
          item.appendChild(
            renderNodeRow(documentNode, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDocumentRow])
          );
          documentsContainer.appendChild(item);
        }
      }

      moduleBlock.appendChild(documentsContainer);
      treeRoot.appendChild(moduleBlock);
    }

    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Дерево проекта обновлено', {
      inlineRenameEnabled: behaviorConfig.inlineRenameEnabled,
      slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled: behaviorConfig.slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled
    });
  }

  async function renderSafely() {
    try {
      await render();
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Ошибка рендера дерева проекта', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
    }
  }

  return { render, renderSafely, getProjectPanelTitle };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/ui/createWorkbenchTabs.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch } from './tabEditLifecycle.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition } from './editorContextLifecycle.js';
import { getDocumentLabel, getDocumentIdentityKey } from '../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';

function createElement(tagName, classNames = []) {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);
  classNames.forEach((className) => node.classList.add(className));
  return node;
}

function normalizeName(name) {
  return String(name ?? '').trim();
}

function buildTabTitleNode(title) {
  const titleNode = createElement('span', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle]);
  titleNode.textContent = title;
  return titleNode;
}

function buildCloseButtonNode(label) {
  const closeButtonNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabClose]);
  closeButtonNode.type = 'button';
  const iconHost = createElement('span', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.iconHost]);
  const iconImage = document.createElement('img');
  iconImage.src = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.tabs.close;
  iconImage.alt = '';
  iconImage.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
  iconImage.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
  iconImage.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
  iconImage.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
  iconImage.decoding = 'async';
  iconImage.loading = 'eager';
  iconImage.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  iconHost.appendChild(iconImage);
  closeButtonNode.appendChild(iconHost);
  closeButtonNode.tabIndex = -1;
  closeButtonNode.setAttribute('aria-label', `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.closeAriaPrefix} ${label}`);
  return closeButtonNode;
}

export function createWorkbenchTabs({
  logger,
  openEditor,
  onActiveEntryChanged,
  onRenameDocument,
  onSyncDocumentRecord
}) {
  const tabsList = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.tabsListId);
  const editorHost = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.editorHostId);
  const tabs = new Map();
  let activeTabId = null;
  let temporaryCounter = 0;
  const renameDocument = typeof onRenameDocument === 'function' ? onRenameDocument : async () => null;
  const syncDocumentRecord = typeof onSyncDocumentRecord === 'function' ? onSyncDocumentRecord : async () => null;


  async function finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({ reason, blockOnFailure = true } = {}) {
    const currentEntry = activeTabId && tabs.has(activeTabId) ? tabs.get(activeTabId) : null;
    const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
      activeEntry: currentEntry,
      logger,
      source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
      reason,
      blockOnFailure
    });

    return result;
  }

  async function activateTab(tabId) {
    const currentEntry = activeTabId && tabs.has(activeTabId) ? tabs.get(activeTabId) : null;
    const canActivate = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
      activeEntry: currentEntry,
      nextTabId: tabId,
      logger
    });

    if (!canActivate) {
      return false;
    }

    activeTabId = tabId;
    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      entry.tabNode.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabActive, entry.tabId === tabId);
      entry.pageNode.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.pageActive, entry.tabId === tabId);
    }

    onActiveEntryChanged?.(tabs.get(tabId) || null);

    return true;
  }

  function updateTabTitle(entry) {
    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);
    if (titleNode) {
      titleNode.textContent = getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord);
    }
  }


  async function collectEntryDocumentRecord(entry) {
    if (!entry) {
      return null;
    }

    let nextRecord = entry.documentRecord;

    if (typeof entry.runtime?.collectDocumentRecord === 'function') {
      nextRecord = await entry.runtime.collectDocumentRecord();

      if (nextRecord?.moduleId && nextRecord?.path && nextRecord?.document) {
        entry.documentRecord = nextRecord;
      } else {
        nextRecord = entry.documentRecord;
      }
    }

    return nextRecord;
  }

  async function syncEntryDocumentRecord(entry, options = {}) {
    const nextRecord = await collectEntryDocumentRecord(entry);

    if (nextRecord?.moduleId && nextRecord?.path && nextRecord?.document) {
      await syncDocumentRecord(nextRecord, {
        tabId: entry?.tabId || '',
        reason: options.reason || APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.tabClose,
        isTemporary: Boolean(entry?.isTemporary)
      });
    }

    return nextRecord;
  }

  function resolveTabId(targetIdentity) {
    if (tabs.has(targetIdentity)) {
      return targetIdentity;
    }

    const identityKeyFromRecord = targetIdentity && typeof targetIdentity === 'object'
      ? getDocumentIdentityKey(targetIdentity)
      : '';

    for (const [candidateTabId, candidateEntry] of tabs.entries()) {
      const candidateIdentityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(candidateEntry.documentRecord);

      if (identityKeyFromRecord && candidateIdentityKey === identityKeyFromRecord) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

      if (candidateIdentityKey && candidateIdentityKey === targetIdentity) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

      if (candidateEntry.documentRecord === targetIdentity) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

    }

    return null;
  }


  async function closeTab(tabId, options = {}) {
    const resolvedTabId = resolveTabId(tabId);
    const entry = resolvedTabId ? tabs.get(resolvedTabId) : null;

    if (!entry) {
      return;
    }

    const orderedEntries = Array.from(tabs.values());
    const index = orderedEntries.findIndex((tabEntry) => tabEntry.tabId === resolvedTabId);

    await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
      activeEntry: entry,
      logger,
      source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
      reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.tabClose,
      blockOnFailure: false
    });

    try {
      await syncEntryDocumentRecord(entry, options);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Ошибка синхронизации snapshot перед закрытием вкладки', {
        tabId: resolvedTabId,
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
    }

    entry.runtime?.dispose?.();
    entry.pageNode.remove();
    entry.tabNode.remove();
    tabs.delete(resolvedTabId);

    if (activeTabId === resolvedTabId) {
      activeTabId = null;
    }

    const fallback = orderedEntries[index + 1] || orderedEntries[index - 1];

    if (fallback && tabs.has(fallback.tabId)) {
      await activateTab(fallback.tabId);
    } else {
      onActiveEntryChanged?.(null);
    }
  }

  function createTemporaryTabEntry({ tabId, initialTitle }) {
    const tabNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tab]);
    tabNode.type = 'button';

    const titleNode = buildTabTitleNode(initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled);
    tabNode.appendChild(titleNode);

    const closeButton = buildCloseButtonNode(initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled);
    closeButton.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeTab(tabId);
    });
    tabNode.appendChild(closeButton);

    const pageNode = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.page]);
    pageNode.dataset.tabId = tabId;
    editorHost.appendChild(pageNode);

    const entry = {
      tabId,
      tabNode,
      pageNode,
      runtime: null,
      documentRecord: {
        moduleId: APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.temporary,
        path: tabId,
        document: { name: initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled }
      },
      isTemporary: true
    };

    tabNode.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      await activateTab(entry.tabId);
    });
    tabsList.appendChild(tabNode);
    tabs.set(tabId, entry);
    void activateTab(tabId);

    return entry;
  }

  async function startTemporaryDocumentCreation({ moduleId, defaultName = '', onCommit }) {
    const tabId = `${APP_CONFIG.project.temporaryDocumentPathPrefix}${moduleId}/${++temporaryCounter}`;
    const entry = createTemporaryTabEntry({ tabId, initialTitle: defaultName || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled });

    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);

    if (!titleNode) {
      return null;
    }

    const input = createElement('input', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.inlineRenameInput]);
    input.type = 'text';
    input.value = defaultName;
    titleNode.replaceWith(input);
    input.focus();
    input.select();

    let finalized = false;

    const cancel = () => {
      if (finalized) {
        return null;
      }

      finalized = true;
      closeTab(tabId);
      return null;
    };

    const commit = async () => {
      if (finalized) {
        return null;
      }

      const nextName = normalizeName(input.value);

      if (!nextName) {
        return cancel();
      }

      const created = await onCommit?.({ moduleId, confirmedName: nextName });

      if (!created) {
        logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Создание документа отклонено', { moduleId, name: nextName });
        input.focus();
        input.select();
        return null;
      }

      finalized = true;
      closeTab(tabId);
      await openDocument(created);
      return created;
    };

    input.addEventListener('keydown', async (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        await commit();
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancel();
      }
    });

    input.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
      if (!normalizeName(input.value)) {
        cancel();
        return;
      }

      await commit();
    });

    return entry;
  }

  async function closeAllTabs(options = {}) {
    for (const tabId of Array.from(tabs.keys())) {
      await closeTab(tabId, options);
    }
  }

  function getActiveDocumentRecord() {
    if (!activeTabId || !tabs.has(activeTabId)) {
      return null;
    }

    return tabs.get(activeTabId).documentRecord;
  }

  function getActiveRuntime() {
    if (!activeTabId || !tabs.has(activeTabId)) {
      return null;
    }

    return tabs.get(activeTabId).runtime || null;
  }

  async function startRename(tabId) {
    const entry = tabs.get(tabId);

    if (!entry) {
      return false;
    }

    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);

    if (!titleNode || titleNode.dataset.renaming === '1') {
      return false;
    }

    titleNode.dataset.renaming = '1';

    const previousName = getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord);
    const input = createElement('input', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.inlineRenameInput]);
    input.type = 'text';
    input.value = previousName;

    titleNode.replaceWith(input);
    input.focus();
    input.select();

    let finalized = false;

    const finalize = async (commit) => {
      if (finalized) {
        return false;
      }

      finalized = true;
      const nextName = normalizeName(input.value);
      let updatedTabId = tabId;

      if (commit) {
        if (!nextName) {
          logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Пустое имя отклонено');
        } else {
          const renamed = await renameDocument(getDocumentIdentityKey(entry.documentRecord), nextName);

          if (!renamed) {
            logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Переименование отклонено', { name: nextName });
          } else {
            if (renamed.nextPath !== renamed.previousPath) {
              entry.documentRecord.path = renamed.nextPath;
            }

            updatedTabId = entry.tabId;
            entry.pageNode.dataset.tabId = entry.tabId;
            updateTabTitle(entry);
          }
        }
      }

      const restoredTitle = buildTabTitleNode(getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord));
      restoredTitle.dataset.renaming = '0';
      input.replaceWith(restoredTitle);

      return updatedTabId;
    };

    input.addEventListener('keydown', async (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        const updatedTabId = await finalize(true);
        if (updatedTabId) {
          await activateTab(updatedTabId);
        }
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        const updatedTabId = await finalize(false);
        if (updatedTabId) {
          await activateTab(updatedTabId);
        }
      }
    });

    input.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
      const updatedTabId = await finalize(true);
      if (updatedTabId) {
        await activateTab(updatedTabId);
      }
    });

    return true;
  }


  function findTabByDocument(documentRecord) {
    const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);

    if (!identityKey) {
      return null;
    }

    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      if (getDocumentIdentityKey(entry.documentRecord) === identityKey) {
        return entry;
      }
    }

    return null;
  }

  async function openOrActivateDocument(documentRecord, options = {}) {
    const existingEntry = findTabByDocument(documentRecord);

    if (existingEntry) {
      await activateTab(existingEntry.tabId);
      return existingEntry;
    }

    return openDocument(documentRecord, options);
  }

  async function openDocument(documentRecord, { startRenameMode = false } = {}) {
    const tabId = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);

    const existingEntry = tabs.get(tabId) || findTabByDocument(documentRecord);
    if (existingEntry) {
      void activateTab(existingEntry.tabId);
      if (startRenameMode) {
        await startRename(existingEntry.tabId);
      }
      return existingEntry;
    }

    const tabNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tab]);
    tabNode.type = 'button';

    const tabTitle = getDocumentLabel(documentRecord);
    tabNode.appendChild(buildTabTitleNode(tabTitle));

    const closeButton = buildCloseButtonNode(tabTitle);
    closeButton.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeTab(tabId);
    });
    tabNode.appendChild(closeButton);

    const pageNode = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.page]);
    pageNode.dataset.tabId = tabId;
    editorHost.appendChild(pageNode);

    const runtime = await openEditor({
      documentRecord,
      mountElement: pageNode
    });

    const entry = { tabId, tabNode, pageNode, runtime, documentRecord };
    tabs.set(tabId, entry);

    tabNode.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      await activateTab(entry.tabId);
    });
    tabNode.addEventListener('dblclick', async (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      await startRename(entry.tabId);
    });

    tabsList.appendChild(tabNode);
    void activateTab(tabId);

    if (startRenameMode) {
      await startRename(entry.tabId);
    }

    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Открыта вкладка', { tabId });
    return entry;
  }

  async function collectOpenDocumentRecords() {
    const output = [];

    await finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({
      reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.collectOpenDocumentRecords,
      blockOnFailure: false
    });

    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      try {
        const nextRecord = await collectEntryDocumentRecord(entry);
        output.push(nextRecord || entry.documentRecord);
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Ошибка синхронизации snapshot открытого документа', {
          tabId: entry.tabId,
          message: error?.message || String(error)
        });
        output.push(entry.documentRecord);
      }
    }

    return output;
  }

  function updateTabPaths(pathMap) {
    if (!pathMap || typeof pathMap.entries !== 'function') {
      return;
    }

    for (const [identityKey, nextPath] of pathMap.entries()) {
      if (!tabs.has(identityKey)) {
        continue;
      }

      const entry = tabs.get(identityKey);
      entry.documentRecord.path = nextPath;
      entry.pageNode.dataset.tabId = identityKey;
    }
  }

  return {
    openDocument,
    openOrActivateDocument,
    findTabByDocument,
    activateTab,
    closeTab,
    closeAllTabs,
    getActiveDocumentRecord,
    getActiveRuntime,
    collectOpenDocumentRecords,
    startRename,
    updateTabPaths,
    startTemporaryDocumentCreation,
    finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/ui/dialogs.js

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

function createElement(tagName, className = '') {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);

  if (className) {
    node.className = className;
  }

  return node;
}

function normalizeUserId(value) {
  return String(value || '').trim().toLocaleLowerCase();
}

export function normalizeProjectSaveAsDialogResult(dialogResult, {
  resultIds = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.resultIds,
  fieldNames = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.fieldNames
} = {}) {
  const cancelResultId = String(resultIds?.cancel || '').trim();
  const confirmResultId = String(resultIds?.confirm || '').trim();
  const resultId = String(dialogResult?.resultId || '').trim();

  if (!resultId) {
    return {
      isMalformed: true,
      isCancelled: false,
      isConfirmed: false,
      name: '',
      comment: ''
    };
  }

  if (resultId === cancelResultId) {
    return {
      isMalformed: false,
      isCancelled: true,
      isConfirmed: false,
      name: '',
      comment: ''
    };
  }

  if (resultId !== confirmResultId) {
    return {
      isMalformed: true,
      isCancelled: false,
      isConfirmed: false,
      name: '',
      comment: ''
    };
  }

  const name = String(dialogResult?.[fieldNames?.name] || '').trim();
  const comment = String(dialogResult?.[fieldNames?.comment] || '').trim();
  if (!name) {
    return {
      isMalformed: true,
      isCancelled: false,
      isConfirmed: false,
      name: '',
      comment: ''
    };
  }

  return {
    isMalformed: false,
    isCancelled: false,
    isConfirmed: true,
    name,
    comment
  };
}

export function normalizeSaveChangesDialogResult(decision, {
  dialogResults = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults
} = {}) {
  const normalizedDecision = String(decision || '').trim();

  return {
    isCancel: normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.cancel || '').trim(),
    isDiscard: normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.discard || '').trim(),
    isSave: normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.save || '').trim(),
    isMalformed: !normalizedDecision
      || !(
        normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.cancel || '').trim()
        || normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.discard || '').trim()
        || normalizedDecision === String(dialogResults?.save || '').trim()
      )
  };
}

function appendDialogCloseButton({ headerNode, onClose }) {
  const closeButton = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogCloseButton);
  closeButton.type = 'button';
  closeButton.title = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.dialogCloseAriaLabel;
  closeButton.setAttribute('aria-label', APP_CONFIG.ui.text.dialogCloseAriaLabel);
  closeButton.addEventListener('click', () => onClose?.());

  const closeIcon = createElement('img', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogCloseIcon);
  closeIcon.src = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.dialog.close;
  closeIcon.alt = '';
  closeIcon.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
  closeIcon.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
  closeIcon.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
  closeIcon.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
  closeIcon.decoding = 'async';
  closeIcon.loading = 'eager';
  closeIcon.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  closeButton.appendChild(closeIcon);
  headerNode.appendChild(closeButton);
}

function createDialogHeader({ title, onClose, titleClassName = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogTitle, titlePrefixNode = null }) {
  const headerNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogHeader);
  const titleRowNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogHeaderRow);
  if (titlePrefixNode) {
    titleRowNode.appendChild(titlePrefixNode);
  }
  const titleNode = createElement('div', titleClassName);
  titleNode.textContent = title;
  titleRowNode.appendChild(titleNode);
  headerNode.appendChild(titleRowNode);
  appendDialogCloseButton({ headerNode, onClose });
  return { headerNode, titleNode, titleRowNode };
}

export function isBackendProjectLocked(project) {
  const lockOwnerDisplayName = String(project?.lockedBy?.displayName || '').trim();
  const lockOwnerUserId = String(project?.lockedBy?.userId || '').trim();
  return Boolean(lockOwnerDisplayName || lockOwnerUserId);
}

export function resolveBackendProjectPickerStatusText({
  statusId,
  loadingStatusId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.loading,
  readyStatusId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.ready,
  emptyStatusId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.empty,
  errorStatusId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.error,
  loadingText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerLoading,
  readyText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerReady,
  emptyText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerEmpty,
  errorText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerError
}) {
  if (statusId === loadingStatusId) {
    return loadingText;
  }
  if (statusId === readyStatusId) {
    return readyText;
  }
  if (statusId === emptyStatusId) {
    return emptyText;
  }
  if (statusId === errorStatusId) {
    return errorText;
  }
  return '';
}

export function resolveBackendProjectPickerProjectEntry(
  project,
  {
    currentUserId = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.userId,
    lockedBadgeText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerLockedBadge,
    projectAvailabilityStates = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.projectAvailabilityStates
  } = {}
) {
  const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
  if (!projectId) {
    return null;
  }

  const normalizedCurrentUserId = normalizeUserId(currentUserId);
  const lockOwnerUserId = normalizeUserId(project?.lockedBy?.userId);
  const lockOwnerDisplayName = String(project?.lockedBy?.displayName || '').trim();
  const lockOwner = lockOwnerDisplayName || String(project?.lockedBy?.userId || '').trim();
  const isLocked = isBackendProjectLocked(project);
  const isLockedByCurrentUser = Boolean(isLocked && normalizedCurrentUserId && lockOwnerUserId && lockOwnerUserId === normalizedCurrentUserId);
  const isSelectable = !isLocked || isLockedByCurrentUser;
  const title = String(project?.name || project?.slug || projectId).trim() || projectId;
  const slugText = String(project?.slug || '').trim();
  const statusText = isLocked
    ? (lockOwner ? `${lockedBadgeText}: ${lockOwner}` : lockedBadgeText)
    : '';

  return {
    project,
    projectId,
    title,
    slugText,
    statusText,
    isLocked,
    isLockedByCurrentUser,
    isSelectable,
    availabilityState: isSelectable ? projectAvailabilityStates.available : projectAvailabilityStates.locked
  };
}

export function resolveBackendProjectPickerProjectComment(
  project,
  {
    fallbackCommentText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardProjectFallbackComment
  } = {}
) {
  const comment = String(project?.comment || '').trim();
  return comment || fallbackCommentText;
}

export function normalizeBackendProjectPickerName(name) {
  return String(name || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ').toLocaleLowerCase();
}

export function resolveBackendProjectPickerCreateValidation({
  name = '',
  projects = [],
  emptyReason = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardCreateDisabledEmpty,
  duplicateReason = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardCreateDisabledDuplicate
} = {}) {
  const rawName = String(name || '');
  const trimmedName = rawName.trim();
  if (!trimmedName) {
    return {
      canCreate: false,
      normalizedName: '',
      reason: emptyReason
    };
  }

  const normalizedName = normalizeBackendProjectPickerName(trimmedName);
  const hasDuplicate = (Array.isArray(projects) ? projects : []).some((project) => {
    return normalizeBackendProjectPickerName(project?.name || '') === normalizedName;
  });
  if (hasDuplicate) {
    return {
      canCreate: false,
      normalizedName,
      reason: duplicateReason
    };
  }

  return {
    canCreate: true,
    normalizedName,
    reason: ''
  };
}

export function showProjectSaveAsDialog({
  title = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectSaveAsTitle,
  nameLabel = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectSaveAsNameLabel,
  commentLabel = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectSaveAsCommentLabel,
  namePlaceholder = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectSaveAsNamePlaceholder,
  commentPlaceholder = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.projectSaveAsCommentPlaceholder,
  nameRequiredText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.projectSaveAsNameRequired,
  duplicateNameText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.projectSaveAsNameDuplicate,
  existingProjects = [],
  initialName = '',
  initialComment = '',
  confirmText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.projectSaveAsConfirm,
  cancelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog);

    const nameFieldNode = createElement('label', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogFieldGroup);
    const nameLabelNode = createElement('span', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogFieldLabel);
    nameLabelNode.textContent = nameLabel;
    const nameInputNode = createElement('input', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogInput);
    nameInputNode.type = 'text';
    nameInputNode.value = String(initialName || '');
    nameInputNode.placeholder = namePlaceholder;
    nameFieldNode.appendChild(nameLabelNode);
    nameFieldNode.appendChild(nameInputNode);

    const commentFieldNode = createElement('label', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogFieldGroup);
    const commentLabelNode = createElement('span', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogFieldLabel);
    commentLabelNode.textContent = commentLabel;
    const commentInputNode = createElement('textarea', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogTextarea);
    commentInputNode.value = String(initialComment || '');
    commentInputNode.placeholder = commentPlaceholder;
    commentFieldNode.appendChild(commentLabelNode);
    commentFieldNode.appendChild(commentInputNode);

    const validationNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogValidation);

    const actions = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogActions);
    const cancelButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessSecondaryButton}`
    );
    cancelButton.type = 'button';
    cancelButton.textContent = cancelText;

    const confirmButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessPrimaryButton}`
    );
    confirmButton.type = 'button';
    confirmButton.textContent = confirmText;

    const close = (value) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(value);
    };

    const { headerNode } = createDialogHeader({
      title,
      onClose: () => {
        close({
          resultId: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.resultIds.cancel
        });
      }
    });

    const hasDuplicateName = (name) => {
      const normalizedName = normalizeBackendProjectPickerName(name);
      if (!normalizedName) {
        return false;
      }
      return (Array.isArray(existingProjects) ? existingProjects : []).some((project) => {
        return normalizeBackendProjectPickerName(project?.name || '') === normalizedName;
      });
    };

    const validate = () => {
      const normalizedName = String(nameInputNode.value || '').trim();
      let validationMessage = '';
      if (!normalizedName) {
        validationMessage = nameRequiredText;
      } else if (hasDuplicateName(normalizedName)) {
        validationMessage = duplicateNameText;
      }
      const isValid = !validationMessage;
      validationNode.textContent = validationMessage;
      confirmButton.disabled = !isValid;
      return isValid;
    };

    cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
      close({
        resultId: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.resultIds.cancel
      });
    });
    confirmButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (!validate()) {
        nameInputNode.focus();
        return;
      }
      const fieldNames = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.fieldNames;
      close({
        resultId: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.projectSaveAsDialog.resultIds.confirm,
        [fieldNames.name]: String(nameInputNode.value || '').trim(),
        [fieldNames.comment]: String(commentInputNode.value || '').trim()
      });
    });

    nameInputNode.addEventListener('input', () => {
      validate();
    });

    nameInputNode.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        confirmButton.click();
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancelButton.click();
      }
    });

    commentInputNode.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancelButton.click();
      }
    });

    overlay.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancelButton.click();
      }
    });

    actions.appendChild(cancelButton);
    actions.appendChild(confirmButton);
    modal.appendChild(headerNode);
    modal.appendChild(nameFieldNode);
    modal.appendChild(commentFieldNode);
    modal.appendChild(validationNode);
    modal.appendChild(actions);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);

    overlay.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    validate();
    nameInputNode.focus();
    nameInputNode.select();
  });
}

export function showSaveChangesDialog({
  title = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.saveChangesTitle,
  saveText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.save,
  discardText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.discard,
  cancelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog);

    const actions = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogActions);
    const { headerNode } = createDialogHeader({
      title,
      onClose: () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel)
    });

    const cancelButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessSecondaryButton}`
    );
    cancelButton.type = 'button';
    cancelButton.textContent = cancelText;

    const discardButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessSecondaryButton}`
    );
    discardButton.type = 'button';
    discardButton.textContent = discardText;

    const saveButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessPrimaryButton}`
    );
    saveButton.type = 'button';
    saveButton.textContent = saveText;

    const close = (value) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(value);
    };

    cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel));
    discardButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.discard));
    saveButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.save));

    overlay.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel);
      }
    });

    actions.appendChild(cancelButton);
    actions.appendChild(discardButton);
    actions.appendChild(saveButton);
    modal.appendChild(headerNode);
    modal.appendChild(actions);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);

    overlay.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    overlay.focus();
    saveButton.focus();
  });
}

function showBackendProjectDeleteConfirmDialog({
  title = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectDeleteConfirmTitle,
  message = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectDeleteConfirmMessage,
  confirmText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectDeleteConfirmAction,
  cancelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog);
    const messageNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogFieldLabel);
    messageNode.textContent = message;

    const close = (result) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(result);
    };

    const { headerNode } = createDialogHeader({
      title,
      onClose: () => close(false)
    });

    const actionsNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogActions);
    const cancelButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessSecondaryButton}`
    );
    cancelButton.type = 'button';
    cancelButton.textContent = cancelText;
    cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(false));

    const confirmButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogProcessPrimaryButton}`
    );
    confirmButton.type = 'button';
    confirmButton.textContent = confirmText;
    confirmButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(true));

    overlay.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        close(false);
      }
    });

    actionsNode.appendChild(cancelButton);
    actionsNode.appendChild(confirmButton);
    modal.appendChild(headerNode);
    modal.appendChild(messageNode);
    modal.appendChild(actionsNode);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
    overlay.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    overlay.focus();
  });
}

export function showBackendProjectPickerDialog({
  title = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerTitle,
  openText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerOpen,
  exportText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerExport,
  deleteText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerDelete,
  chooseText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerChoose,
  refreshTooltipText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerRefreshTooltip,
  createProjectText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCreateProject,
  importProjectText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerImportProject,
  projectFallbackCommentText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardProjectFallbackComment,
  retryText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerRetry,
  loadingText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerLoading,
  readyText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerReady,
  emptyText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerEmpty,
  errorText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerError,
  createDisabledEmptyText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardCreateDisabledEmpty,
  createDisabledDuplicateText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardCreateDisabledDuplicate,
  inlineNamePlaceholderText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardInlineNamePlaceholder,
  createCommentLabelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerCardInlineCommentPlaceholder,
  lockedBadgeText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPickerLockedBadge,
  currentUserId = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.userId,
  projectSelectionKind = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.selectionKinds.project,
  createProjectActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.createProject,
  deleteProjectActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.deleteProject,
  importProjectActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.importProject,
  exportProjectActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.actionIds.exportProject,
  defaultNamePrefix = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.prefix,
  defaultNameSeparator = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.separator,
  defaultNameMinimumNumber = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.defaultName.minimumNumber,
  loadProjects,
  executeAction
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement(
      'div',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerDialog}`
    );
    modal.id = APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendProjectPickerDialogId;

    const titlePrefixNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerHeaderTitle);
    const refreshButtonNode = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerRefreshButton);
    refreshButtonNode.type = 'button';
    refreshButtonNode.title = refreshTooltipText;
    refreshButtonNode.setAttribute('aria-label', refreshTooltipText);
    const refreshIconNode = createElement('img');
    refreshIconNode.src = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.dialog.refresh;
    refreshIconNode.alt = '';
    refreshIconNode.width = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
    refreshIconNode.height = APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon;
    refreshIconNode.setAttribute('width', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
    refreshIconNode.setAttribute('height', String(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon));
    refreshIconNode.decoding = 'async';
    refreshIconNode.loading = 'eager';
    refreshIconNode.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
    refreshButtonNode.appendChild(refreshIconNode);

    const { headerNode, titleRowNode } = createDialogHeader({
      title,
      titleClassName: `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogTitle} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerHeaderTitle}`,
      titlePrefixNode,
      onClose: () => {
        if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
          return;
        }
        close(null);
      }
    });
    titleRowNode.appendChild(refreshButtonNode);

    const statusNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerStatus);
    statusNode.id = APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendProjectPickerStatusId;

    const listNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerList);
    listNode.id = APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendProjectPickerListId;
    const cardsNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCards);
    listNode.appendChild(cardsNode);

    const retryButton = createElement(
      'button',
      `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonSecondary} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerRetryButton}`
    );
    retryButton.type = 'button';
    retryButton.textContent = retryText;
    retryButton.hidden = true;

    let activeLoadRequest = 0;
    let projects = [];
    let createProjectName = '';
    let createProjectComment = '';
    let createNameDraft = '';
    let activeInlineEditor = '';
    let isActionExecutionInProgress = false;

    const close = (value) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(value);
    };

    function resolveDefaultNewProjectName(projectItems) {
      const normalizedPrefix = String(defaultNamePrefix || '').trim();
      const normalizedSeparator = String(defaultNameSeparator || '');
      const normalizedMinimumNumber = Number.isInteger(defaultNameMinimumNumber) && defaultNameMinimumNumber > 0
        ? defaultNameMinimumNumber
        : 1;
      const expectedPrefix = `${normalizedPrefix}${normalizedSeparator}`;
      const usedNumbers = new Set();

      for (const project of projectItems) {
        const projectName = String(project?.name || '').trim();
        if (!projectName.startsWith(expectedPrefix)) {
          continue;
        }
        const suffix = projectName.slice(expectedPrefix.length).trim();
        if (!/^\d+$/.test(suffix)) {
          continue;
        }
        const number = Number.parseInt(suffix, 10);
        if (Number.isInteger(number) && number >= normalizedMinimumNumber) {
          usedNumbers.add(number);
        }
      }

      let candidate = normalizedMinimumNumber;
      while (usedNumbers.has(candidate)) {
        candidate += 1;
      }
      return `${normalizedPrefix}${normalizedSeparator}${candidate}`.trim();
    }

    function setActionExecutionInProgress(isInProgress, rootNode = cardsNode) {
      isActionExecutionInProgress = Boolean(isInProgress);
      retryButton.disabled = isActionExecutionInProgress;
      refreshButtonNode.disabled = isActionExecutionInProgress;
      const buttonNodes = rootNode.querySelectorAll('button');
      for (const buttonNode of buttonNodes) {
        const isLocked = buttonNode.getAttribute('data-action-locked') === 'true';
        if (!isLocked) {
          continue;
        }
        buttonNode.disabled = isActionExecutionInProgress;
      }
    }

    function setStatus(statusId, textValue) {
      statusNode.setAttribute('data-status-id', statusId);
      statusNode.textContent = textValue || '';
    }

    async function executePickerAction({
      actionId,
      payload,
      projectItems
    }) {
      if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
        return;
      }

      const normalizedActionId = String(actionId || '').trim();
      if (!normalizedActionId) {
        return;
      }

      if (typeof executeAction !== 'function') {
        return;
      }

      setActionExecutionInProgress(true);
      try {
        return await executeAction({
          actionId: normalizedActionId,
          projects: projectItems,
          payload
        });
      } catch (_error) {
        return null;
      } finally {
        if (overlay.isConnected) {
          setActionExecutionInProgress(false);
        }
      }
    }

    async function runActionAndClose({
      actionId,
      payload,
      projectItems
    }) {
      const actionResult = await executePickerAction({
        actionId,
        payload,
        projectItems
      });
      const normalizedActionId = String(actionId || '').trim();
      const resolvedProjectId = String(
        actionResult?.projectId
        || actionResult?.project?.id
        || ''
      ).trim();
      if (!resolvedProjectId) {
        return;
      }
      const resolvedProject = actionResult?.project
        || projectItems.find((item) => String(item?.id || '').trim() === resolvedProjectId)
        || null;
      close({
        selectionKind: projectSelectionKind,
        projectId: resolvedProjectId,
        project: resolvedProject,
        actionId: normalizedActionId
      });
    }

    function appendCardBase({
      cardClassName = '',
      titleText = '',
      statusText = ''
    }) {
      const cardNode = createElement(
        'div',
        `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCard}${cardClassName ? ` ${cardClassName}` : ''}`
      );
      const titleRowNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardRowTitle);
      const commentRowNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardRowComment);
      const statusRowNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardRowStatus);
      const statusNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardStatus);
      statusNode.textContent = statusText;
      const actionsNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardActions);

      if (String(titleText || '').trim()) {
        const cardTitleNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardTitle);
        cardTitleNode.textContent = titleText;
        titleRowNode.appendChild(cardTitleNode);
      }

      statusRowNode.appendChild(statusNode);
      statusRowNode.appendChild(actionsNode);
      cardNode.appendChild(titleRowNode);
      cardNode.appendChild(commentRowNode);
      cardNode.appendChild(statusRowNode);

      return {
        cardNode,
        titleRowNode,
        commentRowNode,
        statusRowNode,
        statusNode,
        actionsNode
      };
    }

    function appendCardButton({
      actionsNode,
      className,
      text,
      onClick,
      isLockedAction = true
    }) {
      const buttonNode = createElement('button', className);
      buttonNode.type = 'button';
      buttonNode.textContent = text;
      buttonNode.setAttribute('data-action-locked', isLockedAction ? 'true' : 'false');
      buttonNode.addEventListener('click', onClick);
      actionsNode.appendChild(buttonNode);
      return buttonNode;
    }

    function appendProjectCards(projectItems) {
      for (const project of projectItems) {
        const projectEntry = resolveBackendProjectPickerProjectEntry(project, { lockedBadgeText, currentUserId });
        if (!projectEntry) {
          continue;
        }

        const { cardNode, commentRowNode, actionsNode } = appendCardBase({
          cardClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardProject,
          titleText: projectEntry.title,
          statusText: projectEntry.statusText
        });
        cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-kind', projectSelectionKind);
        cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-id', projectEntry.projectId);
        cardNode.setAttribute('data-project-availability-state', projectEntry.availabilityState);

        const commentNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardComment);
        commentNode.textContent = resolveBackendProjectPickerProjectComment(project, {
          fallbackCommentText: projectFallbackCommentText
        });
        commentRowNode.appendChild(commentNode);

        const exportButtonNode = appendCardButton({
          actionsNode,
          className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonSecondary,
          text: exportText,
          onClick: async () => {
            if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
              return;
            }
            await executePickerAction({
              actionId: exportProjectActionId,
              payload: { projectId: projectEntry.projectId },
              projectItems
            });
          }
        });
        const deleteButtonNode = appendCardButton({
          actionsNode,
          className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonSecondary,
          text: deleteText,
          onClick: async () => {
            if (isActionExecutionInProgress || !projectEntry.isSelectable) {
              return;
            }
            const isConfirmed = await showBackendProjectDeleteConfirmDialog();
            if (!isConfirmed || !overlay.isConnected) {
              return;
            }
            const projectIdToDelete = String(
              cardNode.getAttribute('data-entry-id')
              || projectEntry.projectId
            ).trim();
            const actionResult = await executePickerAction({
              actionId: deleteProjectActionId,
              payload: { projectId: projectIdToDelete },
              projectItems
            });
            const deletedProjectId = String(
              actionResult?.deletedProjectId
              || actionResult?.projectId
              || ''
            ).trim();
            if (deletedProjectId && overlay.isConnected) {
              await refreshProjects();
            }
          }
        });
        const openButtonNode = appendCardButton({
          actionsNode,
          className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonPrimary,
          text: openText,
          onClick: () => {
            if (isActionExecutionInProgress || !projectEntry.isSelectable) {
              return;
            }
            close({
              selectionKind: projectSelectionKind,
              projectId: projectEntry.projectId,
              project: projectEntry.project
            });
          }
        });

        if (!projectEntry.isSelectable) {
          cardNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerListItemLocked);
          openButtonNode.disabled = true;
          deleteButtonNode.disabled = true;
          openButtonNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonDisabled);
          deleteButtonNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonDisabled);
          exportButtonNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonDisabled);
        }

        cardsNode.appendChild(cardNode);
      }
    }

    function appendCreateProjectCard(projectItems) {
      const { cardNode, titleRowNode, commentRowNode, statusRowNode, actionsNode } = appendCardBase({
        cardClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardCreate
      });
      cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-kind', APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.selectionKinds.action);
      cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-id', createProjectActionId);

      const nameLabelNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardFieldLabel);
      const nameValueNode = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardInlineValue);
      nameValueNode.type = 'button';
      const nameInputNode = createElement('input', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardInput);
      nameInputNode.type = 'text';
      nameInputNode.hidden = true;
      nameInputNode.value = createProjectName;
      const nameEditorNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardInlineEditor);
      nameEditorNode.hidden = true;
      nameEditorNode.appendChild(nameInputNode);
      nameLabelNode.appendChild(nameValueNode);
      nameLabelNode.appendChild(nameEditorNode);

      const commentLabelNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardFieldLabel);
      const commentInputNode = createElement('textarea', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardTextarea);
      commentInputNode.value = createProjectComment;
      commentInputNode.placeholder = '';
      commentLabelNode.textContent = createCommentLabelText;
      commentLabelNode.appendChild(commentInputNode);

      const validationNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardValidation);
      statusRowNode.replaceChildren(validationNode, actionsNode);

      const createButtonNode = appendCardButton({
        actionsNode,
        className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonPrimary,
        text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.create,
        onClick: () => {
          if (activeInlineEditor === 'name') {
            createProjectName = nameInputNode.value.trim();
            nameInputNode.value = createProjectName;
          }
          createProjectComment = commentInputNode.value.trim();
          commentInputNode.value = createProjectComment;
          const validation = resolveBackendProjectPickerCreateValidation({
            name: createProjectName,
            projects: projectItems,
            emptyReason: createDisabledEmptyText,
            duplicateReason: createDisabledDuplicateText
          });
          if (!validation.canCreate) {
            return;
          }
          void runActionAndClose({
            actionId: createProjectActionId,
            payload: {
              name: createProjectName.trim(),
              comment: createProjectComment.trim()
            },
            projectItems
          });
        }
      });

      const updateCreateButtonState = () => {
        const validation = resolveBackendProjectPickerCreateValidation({
          name: createProjectName,
          projects: projectItems,
          emptyReason: createDisabledEmptyText,
          duplicateReason: createDisabledDuplicateText
        });
        createButtonNode.disabled = isActionExecutionInProgress || !validation.canCreate;
        createButtonNode.classList.toggle(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonDisabled,
          createButtonNode.disabled
        );
        validationNode.textContent = validation.reason || '';
      };

      const updateInlineValueTexts = () => {
        nameValueNode.textContent = createProjectName || inlineNamePlaceholderText;
      };

      function stopInlineEdit(editorId, { commit }) {
        if (editorId === 'name') {
          createProjectName = commit ? nameInputNode.value.trim() : createNameDraft;
          nameInputNode.value = createProjectName;
          nameEditorNode.hidden = true;
          nameInputNode.hidden = true;
          nameValueNode.hidden = false;
        }
        if (activeInlineEditor === editorId) {
          activeInlineEditor = '';
        }
        updateInlineValueTexts();
        updateCreateButtonState();
      }

      function startInlineEdit(editorId) {
        if (activeInlineEditor && activeInlineEditor !== editorId) {
          stopInlineEdit(activeInlineEditor, { commit: true });
        }

        if (editorId === 'name') {
          createNameDraft = createProjectName;
          nameInputNode.value = createProjectName;
          nameValueNode.hidden = true;
          nameEditorNode.hidden = false;
          nameInputNode.hidden = false;
          activeInlineEditor = 'name';
          nameInputNode.focus();
        }
      }

      nameValueNode.addEventListener('click', () => {
        startInlineEdit('name');
      });

      nameInputNode.addEventListener('blur', () => {
        stopInlineEdit('name', { commit: true });
      });
      nameInputNode.addEventListener('input', () => {
        if (activeInlineEditor !== 'name') {
          return;
        }
        createProjectName = nameInputNode.value.trim();
        updateCreateButtonState();
      });
      nameInputNode.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
        if (event.key === 'Escape') {
          event.preventDefault();
          stopInlineEdit('name', { commit: false });
          return;
        }
        if (event.key === 'Enter') {
          event.preventDefault();
          stopInlineEdit('name', { commit: true });
        }
      });

      titleRowNode.replaceChildren(nameLabelNode);
      commentRowNode.replaceChildren(commentLabelNode);
      cardsNode.appendChild(cardNode);
      updateInlineValueTexts();
      updateCreateButtonState();
    }

    function appendImportCard(projectItems) {
      const importTitleText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionLabels[
        APP_CONFIG.platform.app.platformActions.ids.importProject
      ] || importProjectText;
      const { cardNode, actionsNode } = appendCardBase({
        cardClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardImport,
        titleText: importTitleText
      });
      cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-kind', APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.selectionKinds.action);
      cardNode.setAttribute('data-entry-id', importProjectActionId);
      appendCardButton({
        actionsNode,
        className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendProjectPickerCardButtonPrimary,
        text: chooseText,
        onClick: () => {
          if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
            return;
          }
          void runActionAndClose({
            actionId: importProjectActionId,
            projectItems
          });
        }
      });
      cardsNode.appendChild(cardNode);
    }

    function renderProjects(projectItems) {
      projects = projectItems;
      cardsNode.replaceChildren();

      if (!createProjectName.trim()) {
        createProjectName = resolveDefaultNewProjectName(projectItems);
      }

      appendCreateProjectCard(projects);
      appendImportCard(projects);
      appendProjectCards(projects);
    }

    async function refreshProjects() {
      activeLoadRequest += 1;
      const requestId = activeLoadRequest;
      retryButton.hidden = true;
      setActionExecutionInProgress(false);
      renderProjects([]);
      setStatus(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.loading, loadingText);

      try {
        const result = await loadProjects?.();
        if (requestId !== activeLoadRequest) {
          return;
        }

        const nextProjects = Array.isArray(result) ? result : [];
        renderProjects(nextProjects);
        if (!nextProjects.length) {
          setStatus(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.empty, emptyText);
          return;
        }

        setStatus(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.ready, readyText);
      } catch (_error) {
        if (requestId !== activeLoadRequest) {
          return;
        }
        renderProjects([]);
        setStatus(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendProjectPicker.statusIds.error, errorText);
        retryButton.hidden = false;
      }
    }

    refreshButtonNode.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
        return;
      }
      void refreshProjects();
    });

    retryButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
        return;
      }
      void refreshProjects();
    });

    overlay.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (isActionExecutionInProgress) {
        return;
      }
      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        close(null);
      }
    });

    modal.appendChild(headerNode);
    modal.appendChild(statusNode);
    modal.appendChild(listNode);
    modal.appendChild(retryButton);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);

    overlay.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
    overlay.focus();
    void refreshProjects();
  });
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

export async function finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
  activeEntry,
  logger,
  source,
  reason,
  blockOnFailure = true
}) {
  const transitionOutcomes = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionOutcomes;

  if (!activeEntry?.runtime) {
    return { continued: true, outcome: transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
  }

  const runtime = activeEntry.runtime;

  try {
    if (typeof runtime.finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave === 'function') {
      const result = await runtime.finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave({ reason, blockOnFailure });
      return {
        continued: result?.continued !== false,
        outcome: result?.outcome || transitionOutcomes.noOp,
        reason: result?.reason || reason
      };
    }

    if (typeof runtime.finishActiveTableEditing === 'function') {
      const outcome = await runtime.finishActiveTableEditing();
      return { continued: true, outcome: outcome || transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
    }

    return { continued: true, outcome: transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
  } catch (error) {
    logger?.error?.(source, 'Ошибка завершения редактирования перед сменой контекста', {
      tabId: activeEntry.tabId,
      reason,
      message: error?.message || String(error)
    });

    return {
      continued: blockOnFailure ? false : true,
      outcome: transitionOutcomes.failed,
      reason
    };
  }
}
