export function resolveProcessPanelSurfaceNodes({
  documentRef = document,
  dom
} = {}) {
  return {
    processPanelNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processPanelId),
    processTitleNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processTitleId),
    processContextNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processContextId),
    processGenerateButton: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processGenerateButtonId),
    processStopButton: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processStopButtonId),
    processCommandLabelNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processCommandLabelId),
    processCommandNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processCommandId),
    processStatusLabelNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processStatusLabelId),
    processStatusNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processStatusId),
    processExitCodeLabelNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processExitCodeLabelId),
    processExitCodeNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processExitCodeId),
    processOutputNode: documentRef.getElementById(dom.processOutputId)
  };
}

export function setupProcessPanelSurface({
  processPanelNode,
  processTitleNode,
  processContextNode,
  processGenerateButton,
  processStopButton,
  processCommandLabelNode,
  processCommandNode,
  processStatusLabelNode,
  processStatusNode,
  processExitCodeLabelNode,
  processExitCodeNode,
  processOutputNode,
  classNames,
  text
}) {
  if (processPanelNode) {
    processPanelNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanel);
  }

  if (processTitleNode) {
    processTitleNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanelTitle);
    processTitleNode.textContent = text.processPanelTitle;
  }

  if (processContextNode) {
    processContextNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanelContext);
  }

  if (processCommandLabelNode) {
    processCommandLabelNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processCommandLabelNode.textContent = text.processMetaCommandLabel;
  }

  if (processStatusLabelNode) {
    processStatusLabelNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processStatusLabelNode.textContent = text.processMetaStatusLabel;
  }

  if (processExitCodeLabelNode) {
    processExitCodeLabelNode.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processExitCodeLabelNode.textContent = text.processMetaExitCodeLabel;
  }

  if (processGenerateButton) {
    processGenerateButton.classList.add(classNames.processPanelActionPrimary);
    processGenerateButton.textContent = text.processGenerateButton;
  }

  if (processStopButton) {
    processStopButton.classList.add(classNames.processPanelActionSecondary);
    processStopButton.textContent = text.processStopButton;
  }

  processCommandNode?.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processStatusNode?.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processExitCodeNode?.classList.add(classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processOutputNode?.classList.add(classNames.processPanelOutput);
}

function isProcessStatusIn(status, statuses) {
  const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
  return Array.isArray(statuses) && statuses.includes(normalizedStatus);
}

function resolveProcessStatusText({
  process,
  commandFailure,
  processStatusByCode,
  processNoneText,
  processUnknownStatusText,
  backendCommandFailedText
}) {
  if (
    !process
    && commandFailure
  ) {
    const codeSuffix = commandFailure.code ? ` [${commandFailure.code}]` : '';
    const messageSuffix = commandFailure.message ? ` ${commandFailure.message}` : '';
    return `${backendCommandFailedText}${codeSuffix}${messageSuffix}`.trim();
  }

  if (!process) {
    return processNoneText;
  }

  const normalizedStatus = String(process.status || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedStatus) {
    return processUnknownStatusText;
  }

  return processStatusByCode[normalizedStatus] || processUnknownStatusText;
}

function resolveProcessModuleText({
  commandId,
  commandModuleByCommand,
  processNotAvailableText
}) {
  const command = String(commandId || '').trim();
  if (!command) {
    return processNotAvailableText;
  }

  const moduleLabel = commandModuleByCommand[command];
  return moduleLabel ? `${moduleLabel}.${command}` : command;
}

function resolveProcessStreamLabel({
  streamName,
  streamLabels
}) {
  const normalizedStream = String(streamName || '').trim();
  return streamLabels[normalizedStream] || streamLabels.system;
}

function resolveProcessOutputLineClassName({
  streamName,
  processStreams,
  classNames
}) {
  const normalizedStream = String(streamName || '').trim();
  if (normalizedStream === processStreams.stderr) {
    return classNames.processPanelOutputLineStderr;
  }
  if (normalizedStream === processStreams.stdout) {
    return classNames.processPanelOutputLineStdout;
  }
  return classNames.processPanelOutputLineSystem;
}

function normalizeGenerationReadiness(readiness) {
  if (!readiness || typeof readiness !== 'object') {
    return {
      isReady: true,
      reason: ''
    };
  }

  return {
    isReady: readiness.isReady !== false,
    reason: String(readiness.reason || '').trim()
  };
}

function normalizePreflightRejection(preflightRejection) {
  if (!preflightRejection || typeof preflightRejection !== 'object') {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    command: String(preflightRejection.command || '').trim(),
    code: String(preflightRejection.code || '').trim(),
    message: String(preflightRejection.message || '').trim()
  };
}

export function resolveProcessPanelPresentationState({
  contextProjectId,
  runtimeSnapshot,
  preflightRejection,
  generationReadiness,
  processRuntimeConfig,
  processStatusByCode,
  processStreams,
  classNames,
  text
}) {
  const normalizedRuntimeSnapshot = runtimeSnapshot && typeof runtimeSnapshot === 'object'
    ? runtimeSnapshot
    : {
      process: null,
      commandFailure: null,
      outputChunks: []
    };
  const runtimeProcess = normalizedRuntimeSnapshot.process || null;
  const runtimeCommandFailure = normalizedRuntimeSnapshot.commandFailure || null;
  const runtimeOutputChunks = Array.isArray(normalizedRuntimeSnapshot.outputChunks)
    ? normalizedRuntimeSnapshot.outputChunks
    : [];
  const normalizedContextProjectId = String(contextProjectId || '').trim();
  const hasBackendContext = normalizedContextProjectId.length > 0;
  const normalizedGenerationReadiness = normalizeGenerationReadiness(generationReadiness);
  const readinessBlocked = hasBackendContext && !normalizedGenerationReadiness.isReady;
  const normalizedStatus = String(runtimeProcess?.status || '').trim();
  const blockingStatus = Boolean(runtimeProcess) && isProcessStatusIn(normalizedStatus, processRuntimeConfig.activeStatuses);
  const stoppableStatus = Boolean(runtimeProcess) && isProcessStatusIn(normalizedStatus, processRuntimeConfig.stoppableStatuses);
  const terminalStatus = Boolean(runtimeProcess) && isProcessStatusIn(normalizedStatus, processRuntimeConfig.terminalStatuses);
  const normalizedOutputChunks = Array.isArray(runtimeOutputChunks) ? runtimeOutputChunks : [];
  const normalizedPreflightRejection = normalizePreflightRejection(preflightRejection);
  const normalizedCommandFailure = runtimeCommandFailure && typeof runtimeCommandFailure === 'object'
    ? {
      command: String(runtimeCommandFailure.command || '').trim(),
      code: String(runtimeCommandFailure.code || '').trim(),
      message: String(runtimeCommandFailure.message || '').trim()
    }
    : null;
  const hasPreStartCommandFailure = !runtimeProcess
    && Boolean(normalizedCommandFailure);
  const hasPreflightRejection = !runtimeProcess
    && Boolean(normalizedPreflightRejection);
  const preflightMessage = normalizedPreflightRejection?.message
    || normalizedGenerationReadiness.reason
    || text.processGenerateBlockedByValidationPrefix;

  const lines = normalizedOutputChunks.map((chunk) => ({
    className: resolveProcessOutputLineClassName({
      streamName: chunk?.stream,
      processStreams,
      classNames
    }),
    text: `[${resolveProcessStreamLabel({
      streamName: chunk?.stream,
      streamLabels: processRuntimeConfig.streamLabels
    })}] ${String(chunk?.content || '')}`
  }));
  if (hasPreflightRejection && lines.length === 0) {
    lines.push({
      className: classNames.processPanelOutputLineSystem,
      text: preflightMessage
    });
  } else if (hasPreStartCommandFailure && lines.length === 0) {
    const codeSuffix = normalizedCommandFailure.code ? ` [${normalizedCommandFailure.code}]` : '';
    const messageSuffix = normalizedCommandFailure.message ? ` ${normalizedCommandFailure.message}` : '';
    lines.push({
      className: classNames.processPanelOutputLineSystem,
      text: `${text.backendCommandFailed}${codeSuffix}${messageSuffix}`.trim()
    });
  }
  const statusText = hasPreflightRejection
    ? preflightMessage
    : resolveProcessStatusText({
      process: runtimeProcess,
      commandFailure: normalizedCommandFailure,
      processStatusByCode,
      processNoneText: text.processNone,
      processUnknownStatusText: text.processUnknownStatus,
      backendCommandFailedText: text.backendCommandFailed
    });

  return {
    contextText: !hasBackendContext
      ? text.processContextMissing
      : readinessBlocked
        ? (normalizedGenerationReadiness.reason || text.processGenerateBlockedByValidationPrefix)
        : `${text.processContextReadyPrefix}: ${normalizedContextProjectId}`,
    commandText: runtimeProcess
      ? resolveProcessModuleText({
        commandId: runtimeProcess.command,
        commandModuleByCommand: processRuntimeConfig.commandModuleByCommand,
        processNotAvailableText: text.processNotAvailable
      })
      : hasPreflightRejection
        ? resolveProcessModuleText({
          commandId: normalizedPreflightRejection.command,
          commandModuleByCommand: processRuntimeConfig.commandModuleByCommand,
          processNotAvailableText: text.processNotAvailable
        })
      : hasPreStartCommandFailure
        ? resolveProcessModuleText({
          commandId: normalizedCommandFailure.command,
          commandModuleByCommand: processRuntimeConfig.commandModuleByCommand,
          processNotAvailableText: text.processNotAvailable
        })
      : text.processNotAvailable,
    statusText,
    exitCodeText: terminalStatus
      ? String(runtimeProcess?.exitCode ?? text.processNotAvailable)
      : text.processNotAvailable,
    canGenerate: hasBackendContext && !blockingStatus && !readinessBlocked,
    canStop: stoppableStatus,
    generateDisabledReason: !hasBackendContext
      ? text.processContextMissing
      : readinessBlocked
        ? normalizedGenerationReadiness.reason
        : blockingStatus
          ? text.processGenerateBlockedByActiveProcess
          : '',
    outputIsEmpty: lines.length === 0,
    outputEmptyText: text.processOutputEmpty,
    outputLines: lines
  };
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/app-config.js';
import { getDocumentLabel, getDocumentIdentityKey } from '../../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';

export const TREE_NODE_TYPES = APP_CONFIG.project.tree.nodeTypes;
export const TREE_ACTION_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.tree.actionIds;

const TREE_CLASS_NAMES = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames;

const MODULE_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE = {
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetagen,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metalab]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetalab,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metaview]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetaview
};

const DOCUMENT_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE = {
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetagen,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metalab]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetalab,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metaview]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetaview
};

export function createTreeBehaviorConfig() {
  return {
    inlineRenameEnabled: false,
    slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled: false
  };
}

export function buildProjectTreeNodes({ project, moduleSections, getDocumentsByModule }) {
  if (!project) {
    return [];
  }

  return [
    {
      nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.project,
      id: `${APP_CONFIG.project.identity.treeProjectPrefix}${project.project?.id || APP_CONFIG.project.defaults.unnamedProject}`,
      label: APP_CONFIG.project.tree.labels.root,
      project
    },
    ...moduleSections.map((sectionConfig) => ({
      nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.module,
      id: `${APP_CONFIG.project.identity.treeModulePrefix}${sectionConfig.moduleId}`,
      moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
      moduleName: sectionConfig.moduleName,
      label: sectionConfig.moduleName,
      sectionConfig,
      children: getDocumentsByModule(sectionConfig.moduleId).map((documentRecord) => ({
        nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.document,
        id: getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord),
        label: getDocumentLabel(documentRecord),
        moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
        path: documentRecord.path,
        documentRecord
      }))
    }))
  ];
}

export function getNodeActions(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return [{
      id: TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent,
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.createComponent.title,
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.createComponent.iconAssetPath,
      visible: true
    }];
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
    return [{
      id: TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent,
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.deleteComponent.title,
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.deleteComponent.iconAssetPath,
      visible: true
    }];
  }

  return [];
}

export function getNodeRowClassNames(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project) {
    return [TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeProjectRow];
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return [MODULE_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE[nodeData.moduleId]].filter(Boolean);
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
    return [DOCUMENT_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE[nodeData.moduleId]].filter(Boolean);
  }

  return [];
}

export function createTreeInteractionController({ tabs, onCreateComponentRequest, onDeleteComponentRequest }) {
  async function onNodePrimaryClick(nodeData) {
    if (nodeData?.nodeType !== TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
      return { handled: false, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.nonDocumentNode };
    }

    await tabs.openOrActivateDocument(nodeData.documentRecord);
    return { handled: true, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.documentOpenOrActivate };
  }

  async function onNodeActionClick({ actionId, nodeData, event }) {
    if (event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
    }

    if (actionId === TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent && nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
      await onCreateComponentRequest?.(nodeData.moduleId, nodeData);
      return { handled: true, reason: TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent };
    }

    if (actionId === TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent && nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
      await onDeleteComponentRequest?.(nodeData.documentRecord, nodeData);
      return { handled: true, reason: TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent };
    }

    return { handled: false, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.unsupportedAction };
  }

  return { onNodePrimaryClick, onNodeActionClick };
}

FILE: ui/renderer/ui/tabEditLifecycle.js

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition } from './editorContextLifecycle.js';

export async function finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({ activeEntry, nextTabId, logger }) {
  if (!activeEntry || activeEntry.tabId === nextTabId) {
    return true;
  }

  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
    activeEntry,
    logger,
    source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
    reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.tabSwitch,
    blockOnFailure: true
  });

  if (!result.continued) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

export function resolvePlatformActionSurfaceNodes({
  documentRef = document,
  dom = APP_CONFIG.ui.dom,
  actionIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.platformActions.ids
} = {}) {
  const surfaceNode = documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionSurfaceId);

  return {
    surfaceNode,
    buttonsById: new Map([
      [actionIds.createProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionCreateProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.openProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionOpenProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.closeProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionCloseProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.saveProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionSaveProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.saveProjectAs, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionSaveProjectAsButtonId)],
      [actionIds.importProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionImportProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.exportProject, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionExportProjectButtonId)],
      [actionIds.exit, documentRef.getElementById(dom.platformActionExitButtonId)]
    ])
  };
}

export function setupPlatformActionSurface({
  surfaceNode,
  buttonsById,
  actionOrder = [],
  actionDomByActionId = {},
  classNames = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames,
  labelsByActionId = {},
  ariaLabelsByActionId = {}
} = {}) {
  if (surfaceNode) {
    surfaceNode.classList.add(classNames.platformActionSurface);
  }

  for (const actionId of actionOrder) {
    const expectedDomId = actionDomByActionId[actionId];
    const buttonNode = buttonsById.get(actionId);
    if (!buttonNode || buttonNode.id !== expectedDomId) {
      continue;
    }
    buttonNode.classList.add(classNames.platformActionButton);
    buttonNode.textContent = labelsByActionId[actionId] || '';
    buttonNode.setAttribute('aria-label', ariaLabelsByActionId[actionId] || '');
  }
}

export function createPlatformActionSurfaceController({
  surfaceNode,
  buttonsById,
  actionIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.platformActions.ids,
  actionOrder = [],
  actionDomByActionId = {},
  classNames = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames,
  labelsByActionId = {},
  ariaLabelsByActionId = {},
  disabledHintsByActionId = {},
  getCurrentProject = () => null,
  resolveEnabledState = () => true,
  backendSource = APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
} = {}) {
  setupPlatformActionSurface({
    surfaceNode,
    buttonsById,
    actionOrder,
    actionDomByActionId,
    classNames,
    labelsByActionId,
    ariaLabelsByActionId
  });

  let surfaceStateVersion = 0;

  function updateState() {
    for (const actionId of actionOrder) {
      const buttonNode = buttonsById.get(actionId);
      if (!buttonNode) {
        continue;
      }

      const isEnabled = resolveEnabledState({
        actionId,
        actionIds,
        currentProject: getCurrentProject?.() || null,
        backendSource
      });

      buttonNode.disabled = !isEnabled;
      if (!isEnabled) {
        buttonNode.title = disabledHintsByActionId[actionId] || '';
      } else {
        buttonNode.removeAttribute('title');
      }
    }

    surfaceStateVersion += 1;
  }

  function getStateVersion() {
    return surfaceStateVersion;
  }

  return {
    updateState,
    getStateVersion
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: rtb/README.md
==================================================

# MetaPlatform

Web-only IDE runtime: frontend on Vite + runtime backend on FastAPI.

## Project Runtime

- **Web UI** - web interface for the application.
- **Vite** - dev server for frontend.
- **Runtime backend** - Python API, backend-managed project lifecycle (DB canonical state + workspace mirrors for transport/artifacts), import/export, process execution, lock/heartbeat/save/close semantics.

## Main Workflows

- **Primary flow:** backend-managed project lifecycle.
- **File operations:** only **import/export**.
- Backend runs **separately**.
- `npm run dev` **does not start backend**.

### Backend project lifecycle

- Browse backend projects
- Create backend project
- Open backend project
- Save backend project
- Save As as a workspace copy (transport mirror only; canonical state remains in backend DB)
- Close backend project
- Delete backend project

### File operations

- **Import**
- **Export**

## Active Process Blocking Policy

Runtime backend enforces active-process blocking in backend command dispatch and import API entrypoint.
This is a backend process ownership/lifecycle rule, not a UI-only guard.

### Status contract

- Active statuses (blocking): `running`, `stopping`.
- Terminal statuses (not blocking): `completed`, `failed`, `stopped`.
- Source of truth: `rtb/app/core/constants.py` (`PROCESS_EXECUTION.active_statuses`, `PROCESS_EXECUTION.statuses`) and `rtb/app/services/process_execution.py` (`get_active_process_blocking_state`).

### Allowed during active process

When active process state is blocking, backend allows only:

- `listProjects`
- `projectHeartbeat`
- `process.getState`
- `process.readOutput`
- `process.stop`

### Blocked during active process

When active process state is blocking, backend blocks:

- `createProject`
- `openProject`
- `deleteProject`
- `saveAll`
- `closeProject`
- `saveProjectAs`
- `exportProject`
- `metagen.generate`
- `importProject` (see import route notes below)

Unknown command ids not explicitly listed in block list are treated as allowed by policy helper; command validity is then handled by normal command validation.

### `/api/commands` vs import route

- `/api/commands` blocking is enforced in `dispatch_command()` via `ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active()`.
- Import is not sent through `/api/commands`. It is a dedicated endpoint: `POST /api/project-imports`.
- Import route explicitly applies the same active-process guard by checking command id `importProject` before multipart parsing/import work.

### Relevant backend error codes

- `ACTIVE_PROCESS_BUSY`: command/import blocked by active process policy.
- `NO_ACTIVE_PROCESS`: `process.stop` requested with no active process.
- `PROCESS_STOP_FAILED`: backend failed to terminate active process after terminate/kill attempts.

`ACTIVE_PROCESS_BUSY` responses include details like `command`, `activeProcessId`, `activeProcessStatus`.

### Expected UI handling for blocked responses

UI lock-release and catalog transitions must treat blocked close/release as hard stop:

- Do not clean up current project/tabs/log state when close/release is blocked.
- Do not continue follow-up create/open/import flow after blocked close/release.
- Keep heartbeat and lock token intact for `blockedActiveProcessBusy` / `blockedFailure`.
- Preserve structured backend error fields (`code`, `message`, `details`) in warning logs.

This behavior is implemented in `ui/renderer/runtime/backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.js` and transition helpers in `ui/renderer/app.js`.

### Safe local verification (bounded only)

Use bounded tests only; do not run long-lived foreground servers for this policy check.

- `cd ./ui && npm.cmd test`
- `cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:integration`
- `cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:backend`

Key backend coverage is in `rtb/tests/test_active_process_policy.py` and active-process cases in `rtb/tests/test_process_execution.py`. UI release-gating coverage is in `tests/backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.test.js` and `tests/backendOpenWiring.integration.test.js`.

## Install

From repository root:

```bash
cd ui && npm install
python -m pip install -r rtb/requirements.txt
```

## Run In Development

Use **two terminals** from repository root.

### Terminal 1 - backend

```bash
python -m uvicorn rtb.app.main:app --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8000
```

### Terminal 2 - web UI

```bash
cd ui && npm run dev
```

## Dev SQLite Reset

If local dev backend fails to start because `rtb/runtime_data/platform.db` has stale or incompatible schema, remove the DB file and start backend again.

PowerShell:

```powershell
Remove-Item .\rtb\runtime_data\platform.db -Force
```

On next backend startup, bootstrap recreates `platform.db` and the canonical runtime schema automatically.

## Test Suite

From repository root:

```bash
cd ./ui && npm.cmd test
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:integration
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:backend
```

Compatibility alias (not required for reviewer verification):

```bash
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:all
```

`test:integration` currently aliases `npm.cmd test`, and `test:all` is kept as a compatibility alias that chains `test` + `test:backend`.

﻿from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

from rtb.app.api.commands import router as commands_router
from rtb.app.core.constants import CORS_POLICY
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import bootstrap_storage
from rtb.app.services.command_dispatcher import process_execution_service

app = FastAPI(title='MetaPlatform Runtime Backend')
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=CORS_POLICY['allow_origins'],
    allow_credentials=bool(CORS_POLICY['allow_credentials']),
    allow_methods=CORS_POLICY['allow_methods'],
    allow_headers=CORS_POLICY['allow_headers'],
)


@app.on_event('startup')
def _startup() -> None:
    bootstrap_storage()


@app.on_event('shutdown')
def _shutdown() -> None:
    process_execution_service.stop_active_process_if_any()


app.include_router(commands_router)

﻿from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from email.parser import BytesParser
from email.policy import default as email_default_policy

from fastapi import APIRouter, BackgroundTasks, HTTPException, Request
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from pydantic import ValidationError

from rtb.app.core.constants import (
    API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
    API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    API_PROJECT_IMPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    COMMANDS,
    ERROR_CODES,
    PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY,
)
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.models.command import CommandRequest
from rtb.app.services.command_dispatcher import (
    dispatch_command,
    ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active,
    make_error_response,
    project_storage_service,
)
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue, ProjectCreateIssue, ProjectImportIssue, ValidationIssue

router = APIRouter()


def _cleanup_export_artifact(path: Path) -> None:
    # Export ZIPs are temporary transport artifacts and are deleted after download.
    path.unlink(missing_ok=True)


def _extract_archive_from_multipart(content_type: str, body: bytes) -> tuple[str, bytes]:
    # Multipart parsing is only for transient import upload transport, not project persistence.
    normalized_content_type = str(content_type or '').strip()
    if 'multipart/form-data' not in normalized_content_type.lower() or 'boundary=' not in normalized_content_type:
        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Multipart form-data payload is required',
            {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
        )

    mime_message = BytesParser(policy=email_default_policy).parsebytes(
        (
            f'Content-Type: {normalized_content_type}\r\n'
            'MIME-Version: 1.0\r\n\r\n'
        ).encode('utf-8')
        + body
    )
    if not mime_message.is_multipart():
        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Multipart form-data payload is required',
            {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
        )

    for part in mime_message.iter_parts():
        field_name = str(part.get_param('name', header='content-disposition') or '').strip()
        if field_name != PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']:
            continue
        file_name = Path(str(part.get_filename() or '').strip()).name
        file_bytes = bytes(part.get_payload(decode=True) or b'')
        return file_name, file_bytes

    raise ValidationIssue(
        'Project archive field is required',
        {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
    )


@router.post(API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT)
def handle_commands(raw_payload: dict[str, Any], request: Request):
    request_id = str(raw_payload.get('requestId', '')).strip()
    request_user_id = str(
        request.headers.get(SETTINGS.request_user_id_header, SETTINGS.default_user_id)
    ).strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id

    try:
        command_request = CommandRequest.model_validate(raw_payload)
    except ValidationError as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            'Invalid request payload',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )

    return dispatch_command(command_request, user_id=request_user_id)


@router.get(f'{API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT}' + '/{export_token}')
def download_project_export(export_token: str, background_tasks: BackgroundTasks):
    artifact = project_storage_service.consume_project_export_artifact(export_token)
    if artifact is None:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail='Project export not found')

    artifact_path = Path(str(artifact['path']))
    background_tasks.add_task(_cleanup_export_artifact, artifact_path)

    return FileResponse(
        artifact_path,
        media_type='application/zip',
        filename=str(artifact['fileName']),
    )


@router.post(API_PROJECT_IMPORTS_ENDPOINT)
async def import_project_archive(request: Request):
    request_id = PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['request_id']
    try:
        ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(COMMANDS['platform']['import_project'])
        normalized_file_name, archive_bytes = _extract_archive_from_multipart(
            content_type=request.headers.get('content-type', ''),
            body=await request.body(),
        )
        if not normalized_file_name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Project archive filename is required',
                {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
            )
        if Path(normalized_file_name).suffix.lower() != PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_extension']:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Project archive must be a .zip file',
                {
                    'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name'],
                    'fileName': normalized_file_name,
                    'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                },
            )

        return {
            'ok': True,
            'result': project_storage_service.import_project_archive(
                archive_name=normalized_file_name,
                archive_bytes=archive_bytes,
            ),
        }
    except ValidationIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_create_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ProjectImportIssue as error:
        error_reason = str((error.details or {}).get('reason', '')).strip()
        error_code = (
            ERROR_CODES['project_import_invalid_archive']
            if error_reason in PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_archive_reasons']
            else ERROR_CODES['project_import_failed']
        )
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            error_code,
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ActiveProcessBusyIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['active_process_busy'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)

FILE: rtb/app/core/settings.py

import os
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

from .constants import (
    DEFAULT_USER,
    PROCESS_EXECUTION,
    PROJECT_LOCKS,
    RUNTIME_DATA_DIR_NAME,
    SQLITE_FILE_NAME,
    WORKSPACE_EXPORT_ARTIFACTS_DIR,
    WORKSPACE_IMPORT_STAGING_DIR,
)


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class Settings:
    runtime_root: Path
    data_root: Path
    sqlite_path: Path
    # Temporary export ZIP artifacts.
    workspace_project_export_artifacts_root: Path
    # Temporary import upload/unpack staging.
    workspace_project_import_staging_root: Path
    # Compatibility aliases for older call sites only.
    workspace_project_exports_root: Path
    workspace_project_imports_root: Path
    default_user_id: str
    default_username: str
    request_user_id_header: str
    lock_ttl_seconds: int
    lock_heartbeat_interval_seconds: int
    session_mode_edit: str
    process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds: float
    process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds: float
    process_stop_force_timeout_seconds: float


def load_settings() -> Settings:
    default_runtime_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
    configured_runtime_root = str(os.environ.get('METAPLATFORM_RUNTIME_ROOT', '')).strip()
    runtime_root = (
        Path(configured_runtime_root).expanduser().resolve()
        if configured_runtime_root
        else default_runtime_root
    )
    configured_data_root = str(os.environ.get('METAPLATFORM_DATA_ROOT', '')).strip()
    data_root = (
        Path(configured_data_root).expanduser().resolve()
        if configured_data_root
        else (runtime_root / RUNTIME_DATA_DIR_NAME).resolve()
    )
    workspace_project_export_artifacts_root = data_root / WORKSPACE_EXPORT_ARTIFACTS_DIR
    workspace_project_import_staging_root = data_root / WORKSPACE_IMPORT_STAGING_DIR
    return Settings(
        runtime_root=runtime_root,
        data_root=data_root,
        sqlite_path=data_root / SQLITE_FILE_NAME,
        workspace_project_export_artifacts_root=workspace_project_export_artifacts_root,
        workspace_project_import_staging_root=workspace_project_import_staging_root,
        workspace_project_exports_root=workspace_project_export_artifacts_root,
        workspace_project_imports_root=workspace_project_import_staging_root,
        default_user_id=DEFAULT_USER['id'],
        default_username=DEFAULT_USER['username'],
        request_user_id_header=PROJECT_LOCKS['request_user_id_header'],
        lock_ttl_seconds=int(PROJECT_LOCKS['ttl_seconds']),
        lock_heartbeat_interval_seconds=int(PROJECT_LOCKS['heartbeat_interval_seconds']),
        session_mode_edit=PROJECT_LOCKS['session_mode_edit'],
        process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stream_policy']['drain_timeout_seconds']),
        process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stop_policy']['soft_timeout_seconds']),
        process_stop_force_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stop_policy']['force_timeout_seconds']),
    )


SETTINGS = load_settings()

import sqlite3
from pathlib import Path

from rtb.app.core.constants import DB_BOOTSTRAP, DB_TABLES
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso

PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE = 'projects_legacy_schema'
PROJECTS_CANONICAL_REQUIRED_COLUMNS = (
    'id',
    'user_id',
    'name',
    'slug',
    'comment',
    'created_at',
    'updated_at',
)
PROJECTS_LEGACY_COLUMNS = frozenset({'root_path', 'project_file_path'})
PROJECT_LOCKS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS = frozenset(
    {
        'project_id',
        'user_id',
        'lock_token',
        'acquired_at',
        'last_heartbeat_at',
        'expires_at',
        'created_at',
        'updated_at',
    }
)
PROJECT_SESSIONS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS = frozenset(
    {
        'session_id',
        'project_id',
        'user_id',
        'lock_token',
        'opened_at',
        'last_seen_at',
        'mode',
        'is_active',
        'created_at',
        'updated_at',
    }
)
PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS = frozenset(
    {
        'project_id',
        'module_id',
        'document_id',
        'document_name',
        'document_kind',
        'serialized_payload',
        'created_at',
        'updated_at',
    }
)


def connect(sqlite_path: Path | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
    target = sqlite_path or SETTINGS.sqlite_path
    connection = sqlite3.connect(target)
    connection.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    connection.execute('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON;')
    return connection


def bootstrap_storage() -> None:
    SETTINGS.data_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    # Workspace roots are non-canonical runtime transport/artifact locations.
    SETTINGS.workspace_project_export_artifacts_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    SETTINGS.workspace_project_import_staging_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    with connect() as db:
        project_documents_table = DB_TABLES['project_documents']
        db.executescript(
            f'''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                slug TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                comment TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS project_locks (
                project_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                lock_token TEXT NOT NULL,
                acquired_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                last_heartbeat_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                expires_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(project_id) REFERENCES projects(id),
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS project_sessions (
                session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                project_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                lock_token TEXT NOT NULL,
                opened_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                last_seen_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                mode TEXT NOT NULL,
                is_active INTEGER NOT NULL,
                closed_at TEXT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(project_id) REFERENCES projects(id),
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS process_runs (
                process_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                command_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                status TEXT NOT NULL,
                pid INTEGER NULL,
                stop_requested INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
                exit_code INTEGER NULL,
                started_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                finished_at TEXT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS process_output_chunks (
                chunk_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                process_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                stream TEXT NOT NULL,
                content TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(process_id) REFERENCES process_runs(process_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS {project_documents_table} (
                project_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                module_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                document_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                document_name TEXT NOT NULL,
                document_kind TEXT NOT NULL,
                serialized_payload TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                PRIMARY KEY(project_id, module_id, document_id),
                FOREIGN KEY(project_id) REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE
            );

            CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_project_documents_project_module
            ON {project_documents_table}(project_id, module_id);
            '''
        )
        _ensure_projects_table_schema(db)
        _ensure_project_locks_columns(db)
        _ensure_project_sessions_columns(db)
        _ensure_project_documents_columns(db)

        now = utc_now_iso()
        db.execute(
            '''
            INSERT INTO users(id, username, created_at, updated_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(id) DO UPDATE SET
                username=excluded.username,
                updated_at=excluded.updated_at
            ''',
            (SETTINGS.default_user_id, SETTINGS.default_username, now, now),
        )
        db.commit()


def _ensure_project_locks_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    if not _table_exists(db, 'project_locks'):
        return

    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute("PRAGMA table_info(project_locks)").fetchall()
    }
    missing_columns = sorted(PROJECT_LOCKS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS - columns)
    if missing_columns:
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(table_name='project_locks', missing_columns=missing_columns)


def _ensure_projects_table_schema(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    if not _table_exists(db, DB_TABLES['projects']):
        return

    projects_table = DB_TABLES['projects']
    if _table_exists(db, PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE):
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(
            table_name=projects_table,
            details='found unexpected technical table projects_legacy_schema',
        )

    column_set = _table_column_set(db, projects_table)
    legacy_required_columns = set(PROJECTS_CANONICAL_REQUIRED_COLUMNS) - {'comment'}
    missing_legacy_required_columns = sorted(legacy_required_columns - column_set)
    if missing_legacy_required_columns:
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(table_name=projects_table, missing_columns=missing_legacy_required_columns)

    has_comment_column = 'comment' in column_set
    if has_comment_column and PROJECTS_LEGACY_COLUMNS.isdisjoint(column_set):
        _assert_projects_table_is_canonical(db)
        return

    # Narrow migration: rebuild projects table without legacy mirror metadata columns.
    foreign_keys_were_enabled = _foreign_keys_enabled(db)
    if foreign_keys_were_enabled:
        db.execute('PRAGMA foreign_keys = OFF;')

    savepoint_name = 'projects_schema_rebuild'
    try:
        db.execute(f'SAVEPOINT {savepoint_name};')
        if _table_exists(db, PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE):
            db.execute(f'DROP TABLE {PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE};')
        db.execute(f'ALTER TABLE {projects_table} RENAME TO {PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE};')
        db.execute(
            '''
            CREATE TABLE projects (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                slug TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                comment TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );
            '''
        )
        comment_projection = 'comment' if has_comment_column else "''"
        db.execute(
            f'''
            INSERT INTO {projects_table}(id, user_id, name, slug, comment, created_at, updated_at)
            SELECT id, user_id, name, slug, {comment_projection}, created_at, updated_at
            FROM {PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE}
            '''
        )
        db.execute(f'DROP TABLE {PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE};')
        db.execute(f'RELEASE SAVEPOINT {savepoint_name};')
    except Exception:
        db.execute(f'ROLLBACK TO SAVEPOINT {savepoint_name};')
        db.execute(f'RELEASE SAVEPOINT {savepoint_name};')
        raise
    finally:
        if foreign_keys_were_enabled:
            db.execute('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON;')

    _assert_projects_table_is_canonical(db)


def _ensure_project_sessions_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    if not _table_exists(db, 'project_sessions'):
        return

    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute("PRAGMA table_info(project_sessions)").fetchall()
    }
    missing_required_columns = sorted(PROJECT_SESSIONS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS - columns)
    if missing_required_columns:
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(table_name='project_sessions', missing_columns=missing_required_columns)

    # Optional lifecycle column can be added safely for already canonical-compatible schemas.
    if 'closed_at' not in columns:
        db.execute('ALTER TABLE project_sessions ADD COLUMN closed_at TEXT NULL')


def _ensure_project_documents_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    table_name = DB_TABLES['project_documents']
    if not _table_exists(db, table_name):
        return

    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({table_name})").fetchall()
    }
    missing_required_columns = sorted(PROJECT_DOCUMENTS_REQUIRED_COLUMNS - columns)
    if missing_required_columns:
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(table_name=table_name, missing_columns=missing_required_columns)


def _table_exists(db: sqlite3.Connection, table_name: str) -> bool:
    row = db.execute(
        "SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type = 'table' AND name = ?",
        (table_name,),
    ).fetchone()
    return row is not None


def _table_column_set(db: sqlite3.Connection, table_name: str) -> set[str]:
    return {
        str(row['name'])
        for row in db.execute(f'PRAGMA table_info({table_name})').fetchall()
    }


def _foreign_keys_enabled(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> bool:
    row = db.execute('PRAGMA foreign_keys;').fetchone()
    if row is None:
        return False
    return bool(row[0])


def _assert_projects_table_is_canonical(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    projects_table = DB_TABLES['projects']
    column_set = _table_column_set(db, projects_table)
    if column_set != set(PROJECTS_CANONICAL_REQUIRED_COLUMNS):
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(
            table_name=projects_table,
            details=f"expected columns {sorted(PROJECTS_CANONICAL_REQUIRED_COLUMNS)}, got {sorted(column_set)}",
        )
    if _table_exists(db, PROJECTS_SCHEMA_REBUILD_TABLE):
        _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(
            table_name=projects_table,
            details='projects schema migration left technical table projects_legacy_schema',
        )


def _raise_incompatible_dev_db_schema(
    *,
    table_name: str,
    missing_columns: list[str] | None = None,
    details: str | None = None,
) -> None:
    reason = DB_BOOTSTRAP['incompatible_schema_reason']
    message_parts = [f'[{reason}] Incompatible dev SQLite schema detected for table "{table_name}".']
    if missing_columns:
        message_parts.append(f'Missing required columns: {", ".join(missing_columns)}.')
    if details:
        message_parts.append(details.strip().rstrip('.') + '.')
    message_parts.append(
        (
            'Run a manual dev reset for the DB file and restart backend: '
            f'Remove-Item -LiteralPath "{SETTINGS.sqlite_path}"'
        )
    )
    raise RuntimeError(' '.join(message_parts))

﻿from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator


class CommandRequest(BaseModel):
    request_id: str = Field(alias='requestId', min_length=1)
    module: str = Field(min_length=1)
    command: str = Field(min_length=1)
    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)


class CommandError(BaseModel):
    code: str
    message: str
    details: dict[str, Any] | None = None


class CommandResponse(BaseModel):
    request_id: str = Field(alias='requestId')
    ok: bool
    result: dict[str, Any] | None = None
    error: CommandError | None = None

    @model_validator(mode='after')
    def validate_envelope(self) -> 'CommandResponse':
        if self.ok and self.error is not None:
            raise ValueError('ok response cannot contain error')
        if self.ok and self.result is None:
            raise ValueError('ok response must include result')
        if not self.ok and self.result is not None:
            raise ValueError('error response cannot contain result')
        if not self.ok and self.error is None:
            raise ValueError('error response must include error')
        return self

from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


class ProjectSnapshotDocument(BaseModel):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    # Logical backend URI-like path derived from DB-canonical records.
    # Used as transport/export/import-facing metadata only; not a filesystem contract.
    path: str
    document: dict[str, Any]


class ProjectSnapshotProject(BaseModel):
    project_id: str = Field(alias='projectId')
    name: str
    slug: str
    comment: str = ''
    updated_at: str = Field(alias='updatedAt')


class ProjectSnapshot(BaseModel):
    # Backend snapshot source is DB-canonical storage.
    source: str
    project: ProjectSnapshotProject
    raw: dict[str, Any]
    documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]]


class ProjectSnapshotSave(BaseModel):
    raw: dict[str, Any]
    documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]]


class LockBoundProjectPayload(BaseModel):
    project_id: str = Field(alias='projectId')
    lock_token: str | None = Field(default=None, alias='lockToken')


class SaveAllPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    project_snapshot: ProjectSnapshotSave = Field(alias='projectSnapshot')


class CloseProjectPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    pass


class ProjectHeartbeatPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    pass


class SaveProjectAsPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    new_name: str = Field(alias='newName')
    comment: str = ''
    project_snapshot: ProjectSnapshotSave = Field(alias='projectSnapshot')


class CreateDocumentPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    document_name: str = Field(alias='documentName')
    document: dict[str, Any]


class RenameDocumentPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    document_id: str = Field(alias='documentId')
    document_name: str = Field(alias='documentName')


class SaveDocumentPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    document_id: str = Field(alias='documentId')
    document: dict[str, Any]


class DeleteDocumentPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    document_id: str = Field(alias='documentId')

﻿from __future__ import annotations

from rtb.app.core.constants import ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY, PROCESS_EXECUTION
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue


def is_command_allowed_during_active_process(command_id: str) -> bool:
    normalized_command_id = str(command_id or '').strip()
    if not normalized_command_id:
        return False

    allowed_commands = set(ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY['allow_during_active_process'])
    blocked_commands = set(ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY['block_during_active_process'])

    if normalized_command_id in allowed_commands:
        return True
    if normalized_command_id in blocked_commands:
        return False
    return True


def assert_command_allowed_during_active_process(*, command_id: str, active_process_state: dict) -> None:
    if not bool(active_process_state.get('isBlocking')):
        return

    if is_command_allowed_during_active_process(command_id):
        return

    raise ActiveProcessBusyIssue(
        PROCESS_EXECUTION['messages']['active_process_blocked'],
        {
            'command': str(command_id or '').strip(),
            'activeProcessId': str(active_process_state.get('processId') or '').strip() or None,
            'activeProcessStatus': str(active_process_state.get('status') or '').strip() or None,
        },
    )

FILE: rtb/app/services/command_dispatcher.py

﻿from pydantic import ValidationError

from rtb.app.core.constants import COMMANDS, ERROR_CODES
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.models.command import CommandRequest, CommandResponse
from rtb.app.services import project_catalog
from rtb.app.services.active_process_policy import assert_command_allowed_during_active_process
from rtb.app.services.errors import (
    ActiveProcessBusyIssue,
    LostProjectLockIssue,
    NoActiveProcessIssue,
    ProcessStopFailedIssue,
    ProjectCreateIssue,
    ProjectDeleteIssue,
    ProjectExportIssue,
    ProjectLockedIssue,
    ProjectNotFoundIssue,
    ProjectOpenIssue,
    ProjectSaveIssue,
    ValidationIssue,
)
from rtb.app.services.process_execution import ProcessExecutionService
from rtb.app.services.project_storage import ProjectStorageService

project_storage_service = ProjectStorageService()
process_execution_service = ProcessExecutionService()


def ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(command_id: str) -> None:
    active_process_state = process_execution_service.get_active_process_blocking_state()
    assert_command_allowed_during_active_process(
        command_id=command_id,
        active_process_state=active_process_state,
    )


def make_ok_response(request_id: str, result: dict | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    if result is None:
        normalized_result: dict = {}
    elif isinstance(result, dict):
        normalized_result = result
    else:
        raise TypeError('Command success result must be an object')

    return CommandResponse(requestId=request_id, ok=True, result=normalized_result)


def make_error_response(request_id: str, code: str, message: str, details: dict | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    return CommandResponse(
        requestId=request_id,
        ok=False,
        error={
            'code': code,
            'message': message,
            'details': details,
        },
    )


def dispatch_command(request: CommandRequest, *, user_id: str | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id
    try:
        platform_module = COMMANDS['platform']['module']
        if request.module != platform_module:
            raise ValidationIssue('Unsupported module', {'module': request.module})

        ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(request.command)

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['list_projects']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.list_projects())

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['create_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.create_project(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['open_project']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.open_project_snapshot(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['delete_project']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_catalog.delete_project(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_all']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['close_project']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.close_project_session(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['project_heartbeat']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.heartbeat_project_session(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_project_as']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot_as(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['export_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.export_project_archive(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['metagen_generate']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                process_execution_service.start_metagen_generate(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_get_state']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.get_active_state(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_read_output']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.read_output(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_stop']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.stop_active_process(request.payload))

        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Unsupported command',
            {'module': request.module, 'command': request.command},
        )
    except ValidationIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_create_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectNotFoundIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_not_found'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectLockedIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_locked'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_open_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except LostProjectLockIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['lost_project_lock'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectSaveIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_save_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectDeleteIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_delete_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectExportIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_export_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ActiveProcessBusyIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['active_process_busy'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except NoActiveProcessIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['no_active_process'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProcessStopFailedIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['process_stop_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except (ValidationError, ValueError) as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            'Invalid request payload',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['internal'],
            'Unexpected internal error',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )

﻿class ValidationIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectCreateIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectOpenIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectNotFoundIssue(ProjectOpenIssue):
    pass


class ProjectLockedIssue(ProjectOpenIssue):
    pass


class ProjectSaveIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class LostProjectLockIssue(ProjectSaveIssue):
    pass


class ProjectDeleteIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectExportIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectImportIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProcessExecutionIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ActiveProcessBusyIssue(ProcessExecutionIssue):
    pass


class NoActiveProcessIssue(ProcessExecutionIssue):
    pass


class ProcessStopFailedIssue(ProcessExecutionIssue):
    pass


==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/process_execution.py
