﻿from __future__ import annotations

import subprocess
import sys
import threading
import shutil
import stat
import os
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, TextIO
from uuid import uuid4

import yaml

from rtb.app.core.constants import COMMANDS, DB_TABLES, PROCESS_EXECUTION, PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.models.process_execution import (
    MetaGenGeneratePayload,
    ProcessReadOutputPayload,
    ProcessStatePayload,
    ProcessStopPayload,
)
from rtb.app.services import project_catalog
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue, NoActiveProcessIssue, ProcessStopFailedIssue, ValidationIssue
from rtb.app.services.project_document_storage import ProjectDocumentStorageService
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass
class ActiveProcessHandle:
    process_id: str
    process: subprocess.Popen[str]
    stream_threads: list[threading.Thread]
    waiter_thread: threading.Thread
    execution_root: Path


class ProcessExecutionService:
    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect
        self._project_document_storage = ProjectDocumentStorageService(db_connect=db_connect)
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self._active_process: ActiveProcessHandle | None = None

    def start_metagen_generate(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            generate_payload = MetaGenGeneratePayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid MetaGen generate payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(generate_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id
        session_project_id = self._resolve_active_session_project_id(normalized_user_id, project_id=project_id)
        if session_project_id != project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'MetaGen generate project must match the opened backend project session',
                {'projectId': project_id},
            )

        snapshot = self._project_document_storage.read_project_snapshot(project_id=project_id)
        if snapshot is None:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Canonical project snapshot is missing for generation',
                {'projectId': project_id},
            )

        metagen_module_id = str(PROJECT_STRUCTURE['metagen_module_id'])
        metagen_documents = list(snapshot.documents.get(metagen_module_id, []))
        if not metagen_documents:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'MetaGen generation requires at least one MetaGen document in canonical project state',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': metagen_module_id},
            )

        process_id = f'proc_{uuid4().hex}'
        execution_root = self._prepare_metagen_execution_boundary(
            process_id=process_id,
            project_id=project_id,
            metagen_documents=metagen_documents,
        )

        with self._lock:
            if self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process.poll() is None:
                self._cleanup_execution_boundary(execution_root)
                raise ActiveProcessBusyIssue(
                    'Active process is already running',
                    {'activeProcessId': self._active_process.process_id},
                )

            command_id = COMMANDS['platform']['metagen_generate']
            args = self._build_metagen_runner_command(
                project_id=project_id,
                input_dir=execution_root / PROCESS_EXECUTION['metagen_runner']['input_dir_name'],
                output_dir=execution_root / PROCESS_EXECUTION['metagen_runner']['output_dir_name'],
            )
            now_iso = utc_now_iso()

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    args,
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding='utf-8',
                    errors='replace',
                    bufsize=1,
                )
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                self._cleanup_execution_boundary(execution_root)
                raise ValidationIssue(
                    'Failed to start MetaGen process',
                    {'reason': str(error)},
                ) from error

            self._insert_process_run(
                process_id=process_id,
                command_id=command_id,
                status=PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['running'],
                pid=process.pid,
                started_at=now_iso,
            )

            stream_threads: list[threading.Thread] = []
            stdout_thread = self._start_stream_consumer(
                process_id=process_id,
                stream_name=PROCESS_EXECUTION['streams']['stdout'],
                stream_pipe=process.stdout,
            )
            if stdout_thread is not None:
                stream_threads.append(stdout_thread)

            stderr_thread = self._start_stream_consumer(
                process_id=process_id,
                stream_name=PROCESS_EXECUTION['streams']['stderr'],
                stream_pipe=process.stderr,
            )
            if stderr_thread is not None:
                stream_threads.append(stderr_thread)

            waiter_thread = threading.Thread(
                target=self._wait_for_completion,
                args=(process_id, process, stream_threads, execution_root),
                daemon=True,
            )
            waiter_thread.start()
            self._active_process = ActiveProcessHandle(
                process_id=process_id,
                process=process,
                stream_threads=stream_threads,
                waiter_thread=waiter_thread,
                execution_root=execution_root,
            )

        return {'process': self._read_process_state(process_id)}

    def get_active_state(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            ProcessStatePayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process state payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        with self._lock:
            active_process_id = self._active_process.process_id if self._active_process is not None else None
            is_running = self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process.poll() is None

        if not active_process_id or not is_running:
            return {'process': None}
        return {'process': self._read_process_state(active_process_id)}

    def read_output(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            read_payload = ProcessReadOutputPayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process output payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        process_row = self._get_latest_process_row()
        if process_row is None:
            return {'process': None, 'chunks': []}

        chunks = self._read_output_chunks(
            process_id=str(process_row['process_id']),
            after_chunk_id=int(read_payload.after_chunk_id),
        )
        return {
            'process': self._serialize_process_row(process_row),
            'chunks': chunks,
        }

    def stop_active_process(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            ProcessStopPayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process stop payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        with self._lock:
            handle = self._active_process

        if handle is None or handle.process.poll() is not None:
            raise NoActiveProcessIssue('No active process to stop')

        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        self._mark_stop_requested(
            process_id=handle.process_id,
            status=PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['stopping'],
            updated_at=now_iso,
        )

        soft_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds
        force_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stop_force_timeout_seconds

        try:
            handle.process.terminate()
            handle.process.wait(timeout=soft_timeout)
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            try:
                handle.process.kill()
                handle.process.wait(timeout=force_timeout)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                raise ProcessStopFailedIssue(
                    'Failed to stop active process',
                    {'processId': handle.process_id, 'reason': str(error)},
                ) from error
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProcessStopFailedIssue(
                'Failed to stop active process',
                {'processId': handle.process_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        handle.waiter_thread.join(timeout=max(soft_timeout, force_timeout))
        return {'process': self._read_process_state(handle.process_id)}

    def stop_active_process_if_any(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            handle = self._active_process

        if handle is None:
            return

        if handle.process.poll() is None:
            try:
                self.stop_active_process({})
            except NoActiveProcessIssue:
                return
            return

        wait_timeout = max(
            SETTINGS.process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds,
            SETTINGS.process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds,
            SETTINGS.process_stop_force_timeout_seconds,
        )
        handle.waiter_thread.join(timeout=wait_timeout)

    def get_active_process_blocking_state(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        with self._lock:
            handle = self._active_process
            if handle is None:
                return {'isBlocking': False, 'processId': None, 'status': None}
            is_running = handle.process.poll() is None
            process_id = handle.process_id

        if not is_running:
            return {'isBlocking': False, 'processId': process_id, 'status': None}

        process_row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
        status = (
            str(process_row['status'])
            if process_row is not None and process_row['status'] is not None
            else PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['running']
        )
        is_blocking = status in set(PROCESS_EXECUTION['active_statuses'])
        return {'isBlocking': is_blocking, 'processId': process_id, 'status': status}

    def _build_metagen_runner_command(self, *, project_id: str, input_dir: Path, output_dir: Path) -> list[str]:
        runner_policy = PROCESS_EXECUTION['metagen_runner']
        configured_generator_path = Path(str(runner_policy['generator_script_path']))
        generator_script_path = (
            configured_generator_path
            if configured_generator_path.is_absolute()
            else (SETTINGS.runtime_root.parent / configured_generator_path)
        ).resolve()

        return [
            sys.executable,
            '-m',
            runner_policy['module_path'],
            runner_policy['project_id_arg'],
            project_id,
            runner_policy['input_dir_arg'],
            str(input_dir),
            runner_policy['output_dir_arg'],
            str(output_dir),
            runner_policy['generator_script_arg'],
            str(generator_script_path),
        ]

    def _wait_for_completion(
        self,
        process_id: str,
        process: subprocess.Popen[str],
        stream_threads: list[threading.Thread],
        execution_root: Path,
    ) -> None:
        try:
            return_code = process.wait()
            stream_drain_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds
            for stream_thread in stream_threads:
                stream_thread.join(timeout=stream_drain_timeout)
            row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
            stop_requested = bool(row and row['stop_requested'])

            status = PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['stopped'] if stop_requested else (
                PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['completed'] if return_code == 0 else PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['failed']
            )
            now_iso = utc_now_iso()
            with self._db_connect() as db:
                db.execute(
                    f'''
                    UPDATE {DB_TABLES['process_runs']}
                    SET status = ?, exit_code = ?, finished_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                    WHERE process_id = ?
                    ''',
                    (status, int(return_code), now_iso, now_iso, process_id),
                )
                db.commit()
        finally:
            self._cleanup_execution_boundary(execution_root)
            with self._lock:
                if self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process_id == process_id:
                    self._active_process = None

    def _resolve_active_session_project_id(self, user_id: str, *, project_id: str) -> str | None:
        normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id
        normalized_project_id = str(project_id or '').strip()
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            project_catalog.cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(
                db=db,
                project_id=normalized_project_id,
                now_iso=now_iso,
            )
            row = db.execute(
                f'''
                SELECT session.project_id
                FROM {DB_TABLES['project_sessions']} AS session
                INNER JOIN {DB_TABLES['project_locks']} AS lock
                  ON lock.project_id = session.project_id
                 AND lock.user_id = session.user_id
                 AND lock.lock_token = session.lock_token
                WHERE session.user_id = ?
                  AND session.project_id = ?
                  AND session.is_active = 1
                  AND session.mode = ?
                  AND lock.expires_at > ?
                ORDER BY session.last_seen_at DESC, session.opened_at DESC
                LIMIT 1
                ''',
                (
                    normalized_user_id,
                    normalized_project_id,
                    SETTINGS.session_mode_edit,
                    now_iso,
                ),
            ).fetchone()
        if row is None:
            return None
        return str(row['project_id'] or '').strip() or None

    def _prepare_metagen_execution_boundary(
        self,
        *,
        process_id: str,
        project_id: str,
        metagen_documents: list[dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Path:
        policy = PROCESS_EXECUTION['metagen_runner']
        execution_root = self._create_execution_root_directory(policy=policy, process_id=process_id)
        input_dir = execution_root / policy['input_dir_name']
        output_dir = execution_root / policy['output_dir_name']
        input_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)

        for index, entry in enumerate(metagen_documents, start=1):
            if not isinstance(entry, dict):
                continue
            document_payload = entry.get('document')
            if not isinstance(document_payload, dict):
                continue
            file_name = self._resolve_generation_document_file_name(project_id=project_id, index=index, entry=entry)
            (input_dir / file_name).write_text(
                yaml.safe_dump(document_payload, sort_keys=False, allow_unicode=True),
                encoding='utf-8',
            )

        return execution_root

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_generation_document_file_name(*, project_id: str, index: int, entry: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        raw_name = Path(str(entry.get('path') or '')).name.strip()
        if not raw_name:
            raw_name = f'metagen-{index}.yaml'
        normalized_name = Path(raw_name).name
        if Path(normalized_name).suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
            normalized_name = f'{Path(normalized_name).stem}.yaml'
        if not normalized_name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Failed to resolve MetaGen document filename for generation input',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'index': index},
            )
        return normalized_name

    @staticmethod
    def _create_execution_root_directory(*, policy: dict[str, Any], process_id: str) -> Path:
        execution_root_parent = (SETTINGS.data_root / policy['execution_root_dir_name']).resolve()
        execution_root_parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        prefix = f"{policy['temp_root_prefix']}{process_id}_"
        for _ in range(8):
            candidate = execution_root_parent / f'{prefix}{uuid4().hex}'
            if candidate.exists():
                continue
            candidate.mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
            return candidate
        raise ValidationIssue('Failed to allocate temporary generation execution boundary')

    @staticmethod
    def _cleanup_execution_boundary(execution_root: Path) -> None:
        def on_remove_error(func, path, _exc_info):
            try:
                os.chmod(path, stat.S_IWRITE)
                func(path)
            except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
                return

        try:
            if not execution_root.exists():
                return
            shutil.rmtree(execution_root, onerror=on_remove_error)
        except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
            return

    def _start_stream_consumer(
        self,
        *,
        process_id: str,
        stream_name: str,
        stream_pipe: TextIO | None,
    ) -> threading.Thread | None:
        if stream_pipe is None:
            return None

        thread = threading.Thread(
            target=self._consume_stream,
            args=(process_id, stream_name, stream_pipe),
            daemon=True,
        )
        thread.start()
        return thread

    def _consume_stream(self, process_id: str, stream_name: str, stream_pipe: TextIO) -> None:
        try:
            for line in iter(stream_pipe.readline, ''):
                content = line.rstrip('\r\n')
                self._append_output_chunk(
                    process_id=process_id,
                    stream_name=stream_name,
                    content=content,
                )
        finally:
            stream_pipe.close()

    def _insert_process_run(self, *, process_id: str, command_id: str, status: str, pid: int, started_at: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                f'''
                INSERT INTO {DB_TABLES['process_runs']}(
                    process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, 0, NULL, ?, NULL, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (process_id, command_id, status, int(pid), started_at, started_at, started_at),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _mark_stop_requested(self, *, process_id: str, status: str, updated_at: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                f'''
                UPDATE {DB_TABLES['process_runs']}
                SET stop_requested = 1, status = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE process_id = ?
                ''',
                (status, updated_at, process_id),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _append_output_chunk(self, *, process_id: str, stream_name: str, content: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                f'''
                INSERT INTO {DB_TABLES['process_output_chunks']}(process_id, stream, content, created_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (process_id, stream_name, content, utc_now_iso()),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _get_latest_process_row(self):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            return db.execute(
                f'''
                SELECT process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                FROM {DB_TABLES['process_runs']}
                ORDER BY created_at DESC, process_id DESC
                LIMIT 1
                '''
            ).fetchone()

    def _get_process_row(self, process_id: str):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            return db.execute(
                f'''
                SELECT process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                FROM {DB_TABLES['process_runs']}
                WHERE process_id = ?
                ''',
                (process_id,),
            ).fetchone()

    def _read_process_state(self, process_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
        row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
        if row is None:
            return None
        return self._serialize_process_row(row)

    def _read_output_chunks(self, *, process_id: str, after_chunk_id: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            rows = db.execute(
                f'''
                SELECT chunk_id, stream, content, created_at
                FROM {DB_TABLES['process_output_chunks']}
                WHERE process_id = ? AND chunk_id > ?
                ORDER BY chunk_id ASC
                ''',
                (process_id, after_chunk_id),
            ).fetchall()

        return [
            {
                'chunkId': int(row['chunk_id']),
                'stream': str(row['stream']),
                'content': str(row['content']),
                'createdAt': str(row['created_at']),
            }
            for row in rows
        ]

    @staticmethod
    def _serialize_process_row(row) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            'processId': str(row['process_id']),
            'command': str(row['command_id']),
            'status': str(row['status']),
            'pid': int(row['pid']) if row['pid'] is not None else None,
            'stopRequested': bool(row['stop_requested']),
            'exitCode': int(row['exit_code']) if row['exit_code'] is not None else None,
            'startedAt': str(row['started_at']),
            'finishedAt': str(row['finished_at']) if row['finished_at'] is not None else None,
            'updatedAt': str(row['updated_at']),
        }


==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/project_catalog.py

﻿from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass

from rtb.app.core.constants import PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS  # compatibility monkeypatch target in tests
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.services.errors import ProjectCreateIssue, ProjectDeleteIssue, ProjectNotFoundIssue, ValidationIssue
from rtb.app.services.project_document_storage import ProjectDocumentStorageService
from rtb.app.utils.id_utils import make_project_id, slugify
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PreparedProjectMetadata:
    # Canonical project identity metadata persisted in DB.
    project_id: str
    name: str
    slug: str
    comment: str
    created_at: str
    updated_at: str


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class CanonicalProjectMetadata:
    project_id: str
    name: str
    slug: str
    comment: str
    updated_at: str


def canonical_project_metadata_from_row(row) -> CanonicalProjectMetadata:
    return CanonicalProjectMetadata(
        project_id=str(row['id']),
        name=str(row['name']),
        slug=str(row['slug']),
        comment=str(row['comment'] or ''),
        updated_at=str(row['updated_at']),
    )


def canonical_project_metadata_to_catalog_payload(
    metadata: CanonicalProjectMetadata,
    *,
    locked_by: dict[str, str] | None = None,
) -> dict:
    return {
        'id': metadata.project_id,
        'name': metadata.name,
        'slug': metadata.slug,
        'comment': metadata.comment,
        'updatedAt': metadata.updated_at,
        'lockedBy': locked_by,
    }


def _to_summary(row) -> dict:
    locked_by_user_id = str(row['locked_by_user_id'] or '').strip()
    locked_by_display_name = str(row['locked_by_display_name'] or '').strip()
    locked_by = None
    if locked_by_user_id:
        locked_by = {
            'userId': locked_by_user_id,
            'displayName': locked_by_display_name or locked_by_user_id,
        }

    metadata = canonical_project_metadata_from_row(row)
    return canonical_project_metadata_to_catalog_payload(metadata, locked_by=locked_by)


def cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(*, db, project_id: str | None = None, now_iso: str | None = None) -> None:
    normalized_project_id = str(project_id or '').strip()
    normalized_now_iso = str(now_iso or '').strip() or utc_now_iso()

    query = '''
        SELECT project_id
        FROM project_locks
        WHERE expires_at <= ?
    '''
    params: list[str] = [normalized_now_iso]
    if normalized_project_id:
        query += ' AND project_id = ?'
        params.append(normalized_project_id)

    stale_rows = db.execute(query, tuple(params)).fetchall()
    stale_project_ids = [str(row['project_id']) for row in stale_rows if str(row['project_id'] or '').strip()]
    if not stale_project_ids:
        return

    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(stale_project_ids))
    db.execute(
        f'''
        UPDATE project_sessions
        SET
            is_active = 0,
            closed_at = COALESCE(closed_at, ?),
            last_seen_at = ?,
            updated_at = ?
        WHERE is_active = 1 AND project_id IN ({placeholders})
        ''',
        (normalized_now_iso, normalized_now_iso, normalized_now_iso, *stale_project_ids),
    )
    db.execute(
        f'''
        DELETE FROM project_locks
        WHERE project_id IN ({placeholders})
        ''',
        tuple(stale_project_ids),
    )


def normalize_project_comment(comment: str | None) -> str:
    return str(comment or '').strip()


def build_initial_project_raw(*, project_id: str, project_name: str, project_comment: str = '') -> dict:
    normalized_comment = normalize_project_comment(project_comment)
    return {
        'kind': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['kind'],
        'version': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['version'],
        'project': {
            'id': project_id,
            'name': project_name,
            'description': normalized_comment,
        },
        'modules': list(PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_display_names']),
        'paths': {
            'metagen': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][0],
            'metalab': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][1],
            'metaview': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][2],
            'generated': PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir'],
        },
    }


def _next_available_slug(base_slug: str) -> str:
    with connect() as db:
        slug = base_slug
        suffix = 2
        while True:
            existing = db.execute(
                'SELECT 1 FROM projects WHERE slug = ?',
                (slug,),
            ).fetchone()
            if existing is None:
                return slug
            slug = f'{base_slug}-{suffix}'
            suffix += 1


def validate_project_name(name: str, *, field: str = 'name') -> str:
    normalized = str(name or '').strip()
    if not normalized:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is required', {'field': field})

    if len(normalized) > 120:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is too long', {'field': field, 'maxLength': 120})

    return normalized


def prepare_new_project_metadata(name: str, *, field: str = 'name', comment: str | None = None) -> PreparedProjectMetadata:
    # Prepare canonical DB metadata only.
    normalized_name = validate_project_name(name, field=field)
    normalized_comment = normalize_project_comment(comment)
    base_slug = slugify(normalized_name)
    if not base_slug:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name cannot be transformed into slug', {'field': field})

    slug = _next_available_slug(base_slug)
    project_id = make_project_id()
    now = utc_now_iso()
    return PreparedProjectMetadata(
        project_id=project_id,
        name=normalized_name,
        slug=slug,
        comment=normalized_comment,
        created_at=now,
        updated_at=now,
    )


def register_prepared_project(metadata: PreparedProjectMetadata) -> dict:
    # Register canonical DB project metadata only.
    try:
        with connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO projects(id, user_id, name, slug, comment, created_at, updated_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (
                    metadata.project_id,
                    SETTINGS.default_user_id,
                    metadata.name,
                    metadata.slug,
                    metadata.comment,
                    metadata.created_at,
                    metadata.updated_at,
                ),
            )
            created_row = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT id, name, slug, comment, updated_at
                FROM projects
                WHERE id = ?
                ''',
                (metadata.project_id,),
            ).fetchone()
            db.commit()
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to save project record',
            {'slug': metadata.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    if created_row is None:
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to load project record after create',
            {'projectId': metadata.project_id},
        )

    canonical_metadata = canonical_project_metadata_from_row(created_row)
    return {
        'project': canonical_project_metadata_to_catalog_payload(canonical_metadata, locked_by=None)
    }


def list_projects() -> dict:
    with connect() as db:
        cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(db=db)
        rows = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT
                projects.id,
                projects.name,
                projects.slug,
                projects.comment,
                projects.updated_at,
                project_locks.user_id AS locked_by_user_id,
                users.username AS locked_by_display_name
            FROM projects
            LEFT JOIN project_locks ON project_locks.project_id = projects.id
            LEFT JOIN users ON users.id = project_locks.user_id
            ORDER BY projects.updated_at DESC, projects.id DESC
            '''
        ).fetchall()
        db.commit()

    return {'projects': [_to_summary(row) for row in rows]}


def create_project(payload: dict) -> dict:
    prepared = prepare_new_project_metadata(
        payload.get('name', ''),
        field='name',
        comment=payload.get('comment'),
    )
    result: dict | None = None

    try:
        result = register_prepared_project(prepared)
    except ProjectCreateIssue:
        raise

    try:
        ProjectDocumentStorageService().replace_project_snapshot(
            project_id=prepared.project_id,
            raw=build_initial_project_raw(
                project_id=prepared.project_id,
                project_name=prepared.name,
                project_comment=prepared.comment,
            ),
            normalized_documents={
                module_id: []
                for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
            },
            allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=False,
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        with connect() as db:
            db.execute('DELETE FROM projects WHERE id = ?', (prepared.project_id,))
            db.commit()
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to initialize project snapshot',
            {'projectId': prepared.project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    if result is None:
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to save project record',
            {'projectId': prepared.project_id},
        )
    return result


def delete_project(payload: dict, *, user_id: str | None = None) -> dict:
    project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
    if not project_id:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})
    normalized_user_id = str(user_id or SETTINGS.default_user_id).strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id

    now = utc_now_iso()
    with connect() as db:
        cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(db=db, project_id=project_id, now_iso=now)
        row = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT id
            FROM projects
            WHERE id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id,),
        ).fetchone()

        if row is None:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})

        lock_row = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT project_locks.user_id AS user_id, users.username AS display_name
            FROM project_locks
            LEFT JOIN users ON users.id = project_locks.user_id
            WHERE project_locks.project_id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id,),
        ).fetchone()
        if lock_row is not None:
            locked_by_user_id = str(lock_row['user_id'] or '').strip()
            locked_by_display_name = str(lock_row['display_name'] or '').strip()
            if locked_by_user_id and locked_by_user_id != normalized_user_id:
                raise ProjectDeleteIssue(
                    'Cannot delete project while a live lock is active',
                    {
                        'projectId': project_id,
                        'lockedBy': {
                            'userId': locked_by_user_id,
                            'displayName': locked_by_display_name or locked_by_user_id,
                        },
                    },
                )

        try:
            db.execute('DELETE FROM project_locks WHERE project_id = ?', (project_id,))
            db.execute('DELETE FROM project_sessions WHERE project_id = ?', (project_id,))
            db.execute(
                '''
                DELETE FROM projects
                WHERE id = ?
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            )
            db.commit()
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectDeleteIssue(
                'Failed to delete project',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

    return {
        'projectId': project_id,
        'deleted': True,
    }



==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/project_document_storage.py

﻿from __future__ import annotations

import json
import re
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from uuid import uuid4

from rtb.app.core.constants import DB_TABLES, PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE, PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.models.project_snapshot import ProjectSnapshotDocument
from rtb.app.services.errors import ProjectNotFoundIssue, ProjectOpenIssue, ValidationIssue
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ProjectDocumentSnapshot:
    raw: dict[str, Any]
    documents: dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]]


class ProjectDocumentStorageService:
    # DB-canonical project snapshot/document storage service.
    # File names and backend paths handled here are transport metadata only.
    _DOCUMENT_GUID_REGEX = re.compile(PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['guid_regex'], re.IGNORECASE)

    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect

    def read_project_snapshot(self, *, project_id: str) -> ProjectDocumentSnapshot | None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            rows = db.execute(
                f'''
                SELECT module_id, document_id, document_name, document_kind, serialized_payload
                FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                WHERE project_id = ?
                ORDER BY module_id, lower(document_name), document_id
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            ).fetchall()

        if not rows:
            return None

        raw_payload: dict[str, Any] | None = None
        documents: dict[str, list[dict[str, Any]]] = {
            module_id: []
            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
        }
        raw_module_id = PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_module_id']
        raw_document_id = PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_document_id']

        for row in rows:
            module_id = str(row['module_id'] or '').strip()
            document_id = str(row['document_id'] or '').strip()
            payload = self._deserialize_payload(
                serialized_payload=str(row['serialized_payload'] or ''),
                project_id=project_id,
                module_id=module_id,
                document_id=document_id,
            )
            if module_id == raw_module_id and document_id == raw_document_id:
                if isinstance(payload, dict):
                    raw_payload = payload
                continue

            if module_id not in documents:
                continue
            if not isinstance(payload, dict):
                continue

            document_name = str(row['document_name'] or '').strip() or document_id
            documents[module_id].append(
                ProjectSnapshotDocument(
                    moduleId=module_id,
                    path=self._to_backend_path(project_id=project_id, module_id=module_id, document_name=document_name),
                    document=payload,
                ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
            )

        if raw_payload is None:
            return None

        return ProjectDocumentSnapshot(raw=raw_payload, documents=documents)

    def replace_project_snapshot(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
        allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration: bool = False,
    ) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            self.replace_project_snapshot_in_transaction(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                raw=raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
                allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration,
            )
            db.commit()

    def replace_project_snapshot_in_transaction(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
        allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration: bool = False,
        now_iso: str | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        normalized_now_iso = str(now_iso or '').strip() or utc_now_iso()
        upsert_rows = self._collect_document_upsert_rows(
            project_id=project_id,
            normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration,
        )
        active_document_ids_by_module = self._group_active_document_ids(upsert_rows)
        self._upsert_raw_payload(
            db=db,
            project_id=project_id,
            raw=raw,
            now_iso=normalized_now_iso,
        )
        db.executemany(
            f'''
            INSERT INTO {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}(
                project_id,
                module_id,
                document_id,
                document_name,
                document_kind,
                serialized_payload,
                created_at,
                updated_at
            )
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(project_id, module_id, document_id) DO UPDATE SET
                document_name = excluded.document_name,
                document_kind = excluded.document_kind,
                serialized_payload = excluded.serialized_payload,
                updated_at = excluded.updated_at
            ''',
            [
                (
                    project_id,
                    row['module_id'],
                    row['document_id'],
                    row['document_name'],
                    row['document_kind'],
                    row['serialized_payload'],
                    normalized_now_iso,
                    normalized_now_iso,
                )
                for row in upsert_rows
            ],
        )
        self._delete_missing_documents(
            db=db,
            project_id=project_id,
            active_document_ids_by_module=active_document_ids_by_module,
        )
        return normalized_now_iso

    def touch_project_metadata_in_transaction(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        project_name: str,
        updated_at: str | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        normalized_updated_at = str(updated_at or '').strip() or utc_now_iso()
        update_result = db.execute(
            f'''
            UPDATE {DB_TABLES['projects']}
            SET name = ?, updated_at = ?
            WHERE id = ?
            ''',
            (project_name, normalized_updated_at, project_id),
        )
        if update_result.rowcount != 1:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})
        return normalized_updated_at

    def _upsert_raw_payload(self, *, db, project_id: str, raw: dict[str, Any], now_iso: str) -> None:
        db.execute(
            f'''
            INSERT INTO {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}(
                project_id,
                module_id,
                document_id,
                document_name,
                document_kind,
                serialized_payload,
                created_at,
                updated_at
            )
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(project_id, module_id, document_id) DO UPDATE SET
                document_name = excluded.document_name,
                document_kind = excluded.document_kind,
                serialized_payload = excluded.serialized_payload,
                updated_at = excluded.updated_at
            ''',
            (
                project_id,
                PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_module_id'],
                PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_document_id'],
                PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_document_name'],
                PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_document_kind'],
                self._serialize_payload(raw),
                now_iso,
                now_iso,
            ),
        )

    def _collect_document_upsert_rows(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
        allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration: bool,
    ) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
        rows: list[dict[str, str]] = []
        document_ids_by_module: dict[str, set[str]] = {
            module_id: set()
            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
        }
        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            for document_name, document_payload in normalized_documents.get(module_id, []):
                normalized_document_name = str(document_name or '').strip()
                if not normalized_document_name:
                    continue

                normalized_payload = self._clone_payload(document_payload)
                document_id = self._resolve_document_id(
                    normalized_payload,
                    allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration,
                )
                if document_id in document_ids_by_module[module_id]:
                    raise ValidationIssue(
                        'Duplicate document identity detected in snapshot',
                        {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, 'documentId': document_id},
                    )
                document_ids_by_module[module_id].add(document_id)
                rows.append(
                    {
                        'module_id': module_id,
                        'document_id': document_id,
                        'document_name': normalized_document_name,
                        'document_kind': self._resolve_document_kind(normalized_payload),
                        'serialized_payload': self._serialize_payload(normalized_payload),
                    }
                )

        return rows

    @staticmethod
    def _group_active_document_ids(rows: list[dict[str, str]]) -> dict[str, set[str]]:
        grouped: dict[str, set[str]] = {
            module_id: set()
            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
        }
        for row in rows:
            grouped[str(row['module_id'])].add(str(row['document_id']))
        return grouped

    def _delete_missing_documents(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        active_document_ids_by_module: dict[str, set[str]],
    ) -> None:
        raw_module_id = PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['raw_module_id']
        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            active_ids = sorted(active_document_ids_by_module.get(module_id, set()))
            if not active_ids:
                db.execute(
                    f'''
                    DELETE FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                    WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ?
                    ''',
                    (project_id, module_id),
                )
                continue

            placeholders = ', '.join('?' for _ in active_ids)
            db.execute(
                f'''
                DELETE FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND document_id NOT IN ({placeholders})
                ''',
                (project_id, module_id, *active_ids),
            )

        db.execute(
            f'''
            DELETE FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
            WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id NOT IN (?, ?, ?, ?)
            ''',
            (
                project_id,
                raw_module_id,
                *PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'],
            ),
        )

    @staticmethod
    def _clone_payload(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        cloned = json.loads(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False))
        return cloned if isinstance(cloned, dict) else {}

    def _resolve_document_id(
        self,
        payload: dict[str, Any],
        *,
        allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration: bool,
        id_field: str = 'document.id',
    ) -> str:
        identity_container = self._resolve_identity_container(payload)
        raw_document_id = str(identity_container.get('id') or '').strip()
        if self._DOCUMENT_GUID_REGEX.fullmatch(raw_document_id):
            return raw_document_id

        if not allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration:
            if not raw_document_id:
                raise ValidationIssue('Document id is required', {'field': id_field})
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document id must be a valid GUID',
                {'field': id_field, 'documentId': raw_document_id},
            )

        generated_id = str(uuid4())
        identity_container['id'] = generated_id
        return generated_id

    def create_document(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_name: str,
        document_payload: dict[str, Any],
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_module_id = self._normalize_module_id(module_id)
        normalized_document_name = self._normalize_document_name(
            document_name,
            project_id=project_id,
            module_id=normalized_module_id,
            field='documentName',
        )
        normalized_payload = self._clone_payload(document_payload)
        document_id = self._resolve_document_id(
            normalized_payload,
            allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=False,
            id_field='document.id',
        )
        document_kind = self._resolve_document_kind(normalized_payload)
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()

        with self._db_connect() as db:
            self._ensure_document_name_available(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                module_id=normalized_module_id,
                document_name=normalized_document_name,
                excluded_document_id=document_id,
            )
            db.execute(
                f'''
                INSERT INTO {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}(
                    project_id,
                    module_id,
                    document_id,
                    document_name,
                    document_kind,
                    serialized_payload,
                    created_at,
                    updated_at
                )
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ON CONFLICT(project_id, module_id, document_id) DO UPDATE SET
                    document_name = excluded.document_name,
                    document_kind = excluded.document_kind,
                    serialized_payload = excluded.serialized_payload,
                    updated_at = excluded.updated_at
                ''',
                (
                    project_id,
                    normalized_module_id,
                    document_id,
                    normalized_document_name,
                    document_kind,
                    self._serialize_payload(normalized_payload),
                    now_iso,
                    now_iso,
                ),
            )
            db.commit()

        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'moduleId': normalized_module_id,
            'documentId': document_id,
            'documentName': normalized_document_name,
        }

    def rename_document(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_id: str,
        document_name: str,
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_module_id = self._normalize_module_id(module_id)
        normalized_document_id = self._require_document_id(document_id, field='documentId')
        normalized_document_name = self._normalize_document_name(
            document_name,
            project_id=project_id,
            module_id=normalized_module_id,
            field='documentName',
        )
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()

        with self._db_connect() as db:
            self._assert_document_exists(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                module_id=normalized_module_id,
                document_id=normalized_document_id,
            )
            self._ensure_document_name_available(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                module_id=normalized_module_id,
                document_name=normalized_document_name,
                excluded_document_id=normalized_document_id,
            )
            db.execute(
                f'''
                UPDATE {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                SET document_name = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND document_id = ?
                ''',
                (
                    normalized_document_name,
                    now_iso,
                    project_id,
                    normalized_module_id,
                    normalized_document_id,
                ),
            )
            db.commit()

        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'moduleId': normalized_module_id,
            'documentId': normalized_document_id,
            'documentName': normalized_document_name,
        }

    def save_document_content(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_id: str,
        document_payload: dict[str, Any],
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_module_id = self._normalize_module_id(module_id)
        normalized_document_id = self._require_document_id(document_id, field='documentId')
        normalized_payload = self._clone_payload(document_payload)
        resolved_payload_document_id = self._resolve_document_id(
            normalized_payload,
            allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=False,
            id_field='document.id',
        )
        if resolved_payload_document_id != normalized_document_id:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document id mismatch between payload and command',
                {
                    'field': 'documentId',
                    'documentId': normalized_document_id,
                    'payloadDocumentId': resolved_payload_document_id,
                },
            )

        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            self._assert_document_exists(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                module_id=normalized_module_id,
                document_id=normalized_document_id,
            )
            db.execute(
                f'''
                UPDATE {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                SET document_kind = ?, serialized_payload = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND document_id = ?
                ''',
                (
                    self._resolve_document_kind(normalized_payload),
                    self._serialize_payload(normalized_payload),
                    now_iso,
                    project_id,
                    normalized_module_id,
                    normalized_document_id,
                ),
            )
            db.commit()

        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'moduleId': normalized_module_id,
            'documentId': normalized_document_id,
        }

    def delete_document(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_id: str,
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_module_id = self._normalize_module_id(module_id)
        normalized_document_id = self._require_document_id(document_id, field='documentId')

        with self._db_connect() as db:
            deleted_rows = db.execute(
                f'''
                DELETE FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
                WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND document_id = ?
                ''',
                (project_id, normalized_module_id, normalized_document_id),
            ).rowcount
            if deleted_rows != 1:
                raise ValidationIssue(
                    'Document not found',
                    {
                        'projectId': project_id,
                        'moduleId': normalized_module_id,
                        'documentId': normalized_document_id,
                    },
                )
            db.commit()

        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'moduleId': normalized_module_id,
            'documentId': normalized_document_id,
            'deleted': True,
        }

    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_module_id(module_id: str) -> str:
        normalized_module_id = str(module_id or '').strip()
        if normalized_module_id not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            raise ValidationIssue('Unsupported module id', {'field': 'moduleId', 'moduleId': normalized_module_id})
        return normalized_module_id

    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_document_name(document_name: str, *, project_id: str, module_id: str, field: str) -> str:
        raw_name = str(document_name or '').strip()
        if not raw_name:
            raise ValidationIssue('Document name is required', {'field': field})
        if '/' in raw_name or '\\' in raw_name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document name must resolve to a single file name',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, field: raw_name},
            )

        normalized_name = Path(raw_name).name.strip()
        if not normalized_name:
            raise ValidationIssue('Document name is required', {'field': field})
        if Path(normalized_name).suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
            normalized_name = f'{Path(normalized_name).stem}.yaml'
        return normalized_name

    def _require_document_id(self, document_id: str, *, field: str) -> str:
        normalized_document_id = str(document_id or '').strip()
        if not normalized_document_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Document id is required', {'field': field})
        if not self._DOCUMENT_GUID_REGEX.fullmatch(normalized_document_id):
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document id must be a valid GUID',
                {'field': field, 'documentId': normalized_document_id},
            )
        return normalized_document_id

    def _assert_document_exists(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_id: str,
    ) -> None:
        row = db.execute(
            f'''
            SELECT 1
            FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
            WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND document_id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id, module_id, document_id),
        ).fetchone()
        if row is None:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document not found',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, 'documentId': document_id},
            )

    def _ensure_document_name_available(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_name: str,
        excluded_document_id: str,
    ) -> None:
        row = db.execute(
            f'''
            SELECT document_id
            FROM {DB_TABLES['project_documents']}
            WHERE project_id = ? AND module_id = ? AND lower(document_name) = lower(?)
            ''',
            (project_id, module_id, document_name),
        ).fetchone()
        if row is None:
            return

        existing_document_id = str(row['document_id'] or '').strip()
        if existing_document_id and existing_document_id != excluded_document_id:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document name already exists in module',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, 'documentName': document_name},
            )

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_identity_container(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        for key in PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['identity_object_keys']:
            candidate = payload.get(key)
            if isinstance(candidate, dict):
                return candidate
        return payload

    @staticmethod
    def _serialize_payload(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        return json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(',', ':'))

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_document_kind(payload: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        value = str(payload.get('kind') if isinstance(payload, dict) else '').strip()
        return value or PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['default_document_kind']

    @staticmethod
    def _to_backend_path(*, project_id: str, module_id: str, document_name: str) -> str:
        # Logical backend URI-like identifier used in API snapshots/export payloads.
        return f"{PROJECT_STRUCTURE['backend_document_path_prefix']}{project_id}/{module_id}/{document_name}"

    @staticmethod
    def _deserialize_payload(
        *,
        serialized_payload: str,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        document_id: str,
    ) -> Any:
        try:
            return json.loads(serialized_payload)
        except json.JSONDecodeError as error:
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project document payload is invalid',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'moduleId': module_id,
                    'documentId': document_id,
                    'reason': str(error),
                },
            ) from error

from __future__ import annotations

import re
import shutil
import time

import yaml

    API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    DB_TABLES,
    PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE,
    PROJECT_EXPORT_POLICY,
    PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS,
    PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY,
    PROJECT_STRUCTURE,
)
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.models.project_snapshot import (
    CloseProjectPayload,
    CreateDocumentPayload,
    DeleteDocumentPayload,
    ProjectSnapshot,
    ProjectSnapshotDocument,
    ProjectHeartbeatPayload,
    ProjectSnapshotProject,
    RenameDocumentPayload,
    SaveDocumentPayload,
    SaveProjectAsPayload,
    SaveAllPayload,

from rtb.app.services.project_document_storage import ProjectDocumentStorageService

class ProjectStorageService:
    _DOCUMENT_GUID_REGEX = re.compile(PROJECT_DOCUMENT_STORAGE['guid_regex'], re.IGNORECASE)

    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect
        self._project_document_storage = ProjectDocumentStorageService(db_connect=db_connect)
        self._project_export_artifacts: dict[str, dict[str, str | float]] = {}

    def open_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        project_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        raw, documents = self._read_snapshot_from_db(project_id=project_id)
        lock_token = self._acquire_or_refresh_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
        )

        snapshot = ProjectSnapshot(
            source=PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_source_backend'],
            project=self._snapshot_project_from_canonical_metadata(project_metadata),
            raw=raw,
            documents=documents,
        )

        return {
            'snapshot': snapshot.model_dump(by_alias=True),
            'lockToken': lock_token,
        }

    def save_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_payload = SaveAllPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid save payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = save_payload.project_id
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        lock_token = str(save_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        canonical_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )

        raw = save_payload.project_snapshot.raw
        if not isinstance(raw, dict):
            raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw is required', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

        normalized_raw = self._normalize_raw_project(raw, project_id)
        normalized_documents = self._normalize_snapshot_documents(
            project_id=project_id,
            documents=save_payload.project_snapshot.documents,
        )
        project_name_for_db_update = self._extract_project_name(
            normalized_raw,
            default_name=canonical_metadata.name,
        )

        try:
            with self._db_connect() as db:
                self._project_document_storage.replace_project_snapshot_in_transaction(
                    db=db,
                    project_id=project_id,
                    raw=normalized_raw,
                    normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
                    allow_legacy_document_id_autogeneration=True,
                )
                self._project_document_storage.touch_project_metadata_in_transaction(
                    db=db,
                    project_id=project_id,
                    project_name=project_name_for_db_update,
                )
                db.commit()
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        return {'project': self._load_snapshot_project_payload_from_db(project_id)}

    # Legacy internal document mutation helpers.
    # They are intentionally excluded from the public platform command contract
    # and should not be treated as primary project save API.
    def create_document(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            create_payload = CreateDocumentPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid document create payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(create_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        lock_token = str(create_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        canonical_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        result = self._project_document_storage.create_document(
            project_id=project_id,
            module_id=create_payload.module_id,
            document_name=create_payload.document_name,
            document_payload=create_payload.document,
        )
        updated_at = self._touch_project_metadata(
            project_id=project_id,
            project_name=canonical_metadata.name,
        )
        return {
            'project': {
                'projectId': project_id,
                'updatedAt': updated_at,
            },
            'document': result,
        }

    def rename_document(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:

        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001

        project_id = str(rename_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:

        canonical_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(

        )
        result = self._project_document_storage.rename_document(

        return {
            'project': {
                'projectId': project_id,
                'updatedAt': updated_at,

        }

    def save_document(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_payload = SaveDocumentPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid document save payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(save_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        lock_token = str(save_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        canonical_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        result = self._project_document_storage.save_document_content(
            project_id=project_id,
            module_id=save_payload.module_id,
            document_id=save_payload.document_id,

        )
        updated_at = self._touch_project_metadata(
            project_id=project_id,

        )
        return {
            'project': {
                'projectId': project_id,
                'updatedAt': updated_at,
            },
            'document': result,
        }

    def delete_document(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            delete_payload = DeleteDocumentPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid document delete payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(delete_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        lock_token = str(delete_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        canonical_metadata = self._load_project_canonical_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        result = self._project_document_storage.delete_document(
            project_id=project_id,

        return {

                'projectId': project_id,
                'updatedAt': updated_at,
